FR-01 欢迎仪式 / Welcoming Ceremony

？？？：来亚什基是我有幸途经的许多小镇之一。
???: I once traveled to a small town called Rayashki.

？？？：它坐落于北极，一个相当寒冷的地方。
???: It was located high up within the Arctic Circle, and it was frigid cold all year long.

？？？：在那之后，我途经西兰岛、巴尔干半岛……以及后来的许多地方。
???: After my visit there, I traveled to many more places, from Zealand to the Balkan Peninsula. My journey went on and on.

？？？：我始终怀念着这儿的一切，那炽热的光亮，那无比美好的初衷……
???: But above all other places, I kept finding my thoughts returning to that little town. To its incandescent lights glowing in the long dark of the polar night, to the shared dream of the people there.

？？？：我在来亚什基收获了这本画册。
???: I got this picture book from Rayashki.

它是一本小巧而温暖的儿童绘本。
It is a children's book—a thin one at that. But, story inside has the power to warm a frigid heart.

稚嫩而强烈的色彩笨拙地晕开在一张张白纸上。
Once opened, whirls of bright primary colors run into one another and flow up onto my palm.

在之后反复发生的恶劣天气里，我无处可去，悄悄抚摩了它许多次。
I found myself returning to it during stormy days when I was stuck at home.

远方的故人

Farewell, Rayashki
This is a story about honest and ordinary people.

—The Friend from Afar
是的，这是个关于无数平凡而质朴的人们的故事。

？？？：天鹅们正在跳舞，围成圈儿，来回——来去——地挥着手臂！
???: The swans are dancing in a circle. Their arms go back and forth!

？？？：在今天之前的一个星期里，维拉带着天鹅们已经跳了二十次……就是她教给了天鹅们最优美的舞步。
???: Vila and the swans have done this dance almost twenty times last week. She taught the swans all their beautiful moves.

？？？：“《天鹅湖》是最好的芭蕾舞剧。”——叶甫根尼先生好像是这样说的。他还说会有乌龟来看……乌龟为什么要看天鹅呢？
???: "Swan Lake is the best ballet ever," I remembered Mr. Evgeni once said so. He also said the tortoises would come to watch the show. But why would tortoises want to watch Swan Lake?

？？？：维拉不喜欢乌龟，她喜欢“知识”……我不记得“知识”，但维拉是对的。
???: Vila says she doesn't like the tortoises. She likes "knowledge." I don't know much about knowledge, but I think Ms. Vila is always right.

？？？：嘘——维拉身上有海藻和珊瑚的味道，很好闻。说不定她是海洋的公主呢……
???: Only between you and me—Vila smells like seaweed and coral. But those are "happy" smells to me. I think she must be the princess of the ocean.

？？？：但她告诉我们，所有人都是一样的，她一点儿也不特别。
???: But she tells us she is not special and that everyone here is equal, no matter if they are a princess or a swan!

？？？：我们都有双脚，有手指头，都可以一起“建设”我们的小镇，也可以一起表演。
???: That we all have two feet and ten fingers, and if we all work together, we can "build a beacon to the future." I hope in the future we still get to sing and dance, when we are not building beacons.

？？？：尼娜最喜欢的食物是阿廖卡巧克力。她在舞步跳错的时候总是流泪……但在维拉和她聊天之后，她就很少落泪了。
???: Nina's favorite food is called Alenka; it's a chocolate bar. She used to cry a lot whenever she made a mistake with her dancing, but then Vila talked to her, and now she doesn't cry so much.

？？？：有一次，她成功地完成了所有的舞步，维拉给了她一小块阿廖卡。
???: One time, she danced very, very perfectly, so Vila gave her a piece of an Alenka bar.

？？？：如果她不紧张的话，我想她会表演得很好……说不定还能再得到一小块巧克力！
???: I believe she will be a great dancer—if she doesn't get too nervous on stage, then she could have even more chocolate!

？？？：我很羡慕她，我也想吃巧克力。
???: I wish I was like her. I want chocolate too!

？？？：但我不是天鹅……而且，食堂里的橱柜里已经很久没有阿廖卡了。
???: But I'm not a swan like her. And now there's never any Alenka in the canteen's cupboard.

消图
视频1-小镇的天鹅湖芭蕾舞（使用氛围图1）孩子们围绕着小镇广场跳芭蕾舞，随着阿夫西维的讲述逐渐移动镜头

？？？：现在，尼娜成为了我们的天鹅公主——天鹅里面最漂亮的那一只。
???: Now, Nina is the swan princess—the most prettiest of all swans.

？？？：帕索诺是所有人都喜欢的王子，他是一只善良的天鹅，有很多天鹅朋友。
???: Pasono is the swan prince. He is a nice swan, and he has many many swan friends.

？？？：而彼得森是魔王，一只黑色的天鹅……大家都不希望成为魔王，但彼得森愿意。
???: And Pyotr is the evil sorcerer, a black swan. Nobody wanted to be the bad guy, but Pyotr doesn't mind.

？？？：他很认真，对每一个人都很严格。他只有很少的天鹅朋友。
???: He is very serious and always bossy to everyone, so he doesn't have many swan friends.

？？？：彼得森比任何人都希望做好他的工作……他很爱我们的小镇。
???: Pyotr just wants to do his job as perfectly as he can, because he loves our town.

阿夫西维：阿夫西维不是天鹅，但他也喜欢这儿。
Avgust: Now Avgust is not a swan, but he also loves his town.

阿夫西维：嗅嗅……
Avgust: *sniffs*

阿夫西维：凉飕飕、一阵风一样轻飘飘的小老鼠……
Avgust: Then there is the little mouse, who moves as quickly as the blowing wind.

阿夫西维：……是我们的新朋友吗？！
Avgust: Will it be our new visitor?!

阿夫西维：这是维拉说过的知识，我不记得了……
Avgust: What was it that Vila said about new visitors? I don't remember now.

结尾
视频结束
小镇广场（现实一面）

阿夫西维放下画纸，回到更喧哗的世界。
Avgust puts down his paper, returning to the world of noise and people.

他四处奔走，搜寻着那个熟悉的身影。
He looks around for a familiar face.

阿夫西维：维拉——！
Avgust: Vila!

他穿过层叠的人群，终于在一片雪地前发现了目标。
The boy slips through the crowd. Until at last he finds that face, looking out over a snowy field.

维拉：嗯……？
Vila: Mm?

阿夫西维：向你报告，维拉，我有一个重要的问题！
Avgust: Reporting to you, Comrade Vila! I have a very important question!

维拉：请说，阿夫西维同志。
Vila: Well, then go ahead, little Comrade Avgust.

阿夫西维：我们应该怎么对待新的客人？
Avgust: How should we receive the new visitors coming to town?

阿夫西维：是阿廖卡、友谊，还是别的什么呢……
Avgust: Maybe we can welcome them with Alenka, or friendship, or maybe something else?

维拉：呵呵～
Vila: *chuckles*

维拉：以白雪，以友好，以对待理想的同样热忱——我们欢迎每一位远道而来的朋友。
Vila: We will welcome them with white snow, with smiles on our faces, and with the welcoming arms we use to achieve our dreams. As we do for everyone who comes here, little comrade.

维拉站起身来，轻轻拂去孩子身上沾染的颜料。
Vila wipes away the paint from the child's face and stands.

维拉：好奇是很好的。但无论如何，别忘了属于你的劳动，好吗？
Vila: It's always good to ask questions. But don't forget your task today, alright?

她眨了眨眼，悄悄地指了指对方手上那幅尚未完成的“画作”。
She points to the unfinished painting in his hand.

孩子忙不迭地点头。
Avgust nods eagerly.

阿夫西维：我记住了——！
Avgust: I won't!

阿夫西维：画画很重要，欢迎新朋友也很重要，我该先做哪一个呢？
Avgust: My drawings are important, but Vila says entertaining our new friends is also important. Which one comes first?

忙碌的画板又支了起来。
He holds up his cluttered drawing board.

阿夫西维：天鹅们飞走了，叶甫根尼该上台了。
Avgust: After the swans have flown away, Evgeni will go up to the stage.

阿夫西维：叶甫根尼不是魔王，但他擅长让人不说话的魔法。
Avgust: Evgeni is not an evil sorcerer, but he knows a secret magic that makes everyone's tongues hide in their mouths.

阿夫西维：他的影子很长，连向日葵也看不懂……但他不是坏人，我想。
Avgust: He is not so much a bad person, I think. Evgeni's shadow is very long, but no one, not even my sunflower, can explain why.

阿夫西维：叶甫根尼走得很慢，没有人为他鼓掌。
Avgust: Evgeni walks heavily onto the stage; his appearance comes without any applause.

挺拔的身影终于登上了演讲台。
The tall figure reaches the podium.

叶甫根尼：咳——
Evgeni: *clears throat*

叶甫根尼：根据不久前收到的电报，芝诺调查员将在明日下午抵达来亚什基。
Evgeni: We have received a telegraph. Zeno's investigators will arrive here in Rayashki tomorrow afternoon.

叶甫根尼：这正是我们举行欢迎仪式的目的。
Evgeni: And we will be hosting a welcome ceremony.

台下维持着既有的沉默，无人应答。
The crowd is silent in reply.

推镜

叶甫根尼：我能理解各位的心情。你们并不希望芝诺过多地干预小镇的发展，更不希望让芝诺派驻军队保护小镇……
Evgeni: I understand your concerns. I know you don't want Zeno to interfere with your lives, nor do you want their troops stationed here.

叶甫根尼：事实上，他们在过去的数十年里确实是这么做的。
Evgeni: And I would remind you that they have honored their side of the deal for decades now.

人群中，有人举起手来。
A callused hand rises up to break the silence.

克努特：咱们给芝诺卢恩矿石，他们给我们报酬——很简单，就这么回事。
Knut: We give them runium ore, and they supply us in return. It should be as simple as that.

克努特：几十年过去了，从我的爷爷辈开始，咱们一直都是这么合作的……
Knut: Always it has been this way, since my grandfather's time.

叶甫根尼：不再是了，克努特同志。
Evgeni: Times have changed, Comrade Knut.

叶甫根尼：从前，我们能够开采卢恩矿石，它们是最好的神秘学单兵作战载具的燃料，芝诺也愿意为它们付个好价钱。
Evgeni: In the old days, Zeno used to pay us generously for mining this runium, because our ore was necessary for their arcane combat vehicles.

叶甫根尼：但现在，这儿的卢恩矿石几乎开采殆尽了。我想，你应该比我更加清楚。
Evgeni: But now, we have nearly exhausted all our mines. You know this better than I do.

克努特：……
Knut: ...

克努特：那咱们就不能干点别的劳动吗？就像现在这样，咱们能够盖房子，甚至还能在培育好的土地上种蔬菜。
Knut: But isn't there some other work we can do? Already, we built our own houses, and now we even grow our own crops.

镇民Ⅰ：没错，我们能自给自足，为什么要向芝诺低头呢？
Resident I: He's right. Why must we work with Zeno if we could feed ourselves?

镇民Ⅱ：冷静点，同志们！叶甫根尼也只是为了来亚什基考虑——难道你们忘了那些令人头大的小怪物们吗？
Resident II: Comrades, calm yourselves! Evgeni is doing this for everybody's sake—have you forgotten about those little monsters?

镇民Ⅱ：那些参加了保卫队的伙计们，有哪个身上是没挂彩的……？
Resident II: Is there anyone left on our defense team that hasn't been injured fighting them?

台下一时噤声，叶甫根尼抓住了这个宝贵的时机。
The audience falls quiet. Evgeni seizes on their momentary pause.

叶甫根尼：尼基塔同志是对的。
Evgeni: It is as Comrade Nikita said.

叶甫根尼：来亚什基周边的魔精愈发猖獗了，它们不仅占据了我们的大部分矿场，有些怪模怪样的家伙甚至窜进了镇子里。
Evgeni: The critters are running rampant these days. Not only have they occupied most of our mines, some have even found their way into the town.

叶甫根尼：仅仅靠着我们自己的保卫队，你们真的觉得能保护好这里吗？还是说，你们宁愿为了一个“来亚什基”的虚名，就罔顾周围人的死活？
Evgeni: Do you really think we can protect our people with our small defense team? Don't you care about your neighbors' safety? Do you want to keep Rayashki an isolated town just to let it die?

维拉：来亚什基并不只是一个虚名，叶甫根尼。
Vila: Rayashki is more than an isolated town, Evgeni.

维拉：你我都知道它代表着什么。
Vila: And we all know that.

叶甫根尼：现实摆在你我眼前，现在不是谈理想的时候了。
Evgeni: But this is the reality we all must face now.

维拉脸上的鳞片微微起伏着，她盯着叶甫根尼，半步也不肯退让。
The scales on Vila's face rise involuntarily. She holds her stare.

工人，厨师，保卫队人员……越来越多的人们加入了辩论。
Workers, cooks, security personnel ... Soon, all of Rayashki has joined in.

克努特：叶甫根尼同志，把那些高高在上的老爷们找来是你一个人的决定，你根本没有向大伙征求过意见，不是吗？
Knut: Comrade Evgeni. It was your idea to turn to these Zeno big guys for help. But you never even asked what we think, did you?

克努特：你得理解大伙的抵触情绪……
Knut: So you can't blame us for disagreeing now.

叶甫根尼：我是为了你们好。
Evgeni: I'm doing this for your good.

斩钉截铁的话语显然没能缓和争执。
His assurances did not seem to have much impact on the crowd.

遗憾的是，紧接而至的一阵寒风也无能为力。
A cold wind passes across the square.

维拉：我们能顾好自己——
Vila: We can take care of ourself- ...

她还想再说些什么，一阵浓郁的冰冷气息覆盖上了她脖颈的鳞片。
She has more to say, but as she moves to speak, her scales stand on edge and shiver audibly.

比起制止争端，寒风显然预示着某种更紧迫的危险。
She holds her hand up, signaling to the crowd. There is a scent on the wind—danger is near.

收镜
震屏

？？？：吼吼——！
???: *roars*

几头毛发耸立的魔精突兀地窜进了广场。
A horde of hairy critters burst into the square.

维拉：大家小心——！
Vila: Everyone, watch out!

她转过身，抄起一旁的木椅迎了上去。
She picks up a wooden chair to fend them off.

叶甫根尼：保卫队成员，全员备战！
Evgeni: Defense team!

保卫队员Ⅰ：明白！
Guard I: On it!

？？？：呜……
???: *wails*

长相古怪的魔精落荒而逃。
The critters flee in a panic.

值得庆幸的是，它们至少为制止争端贡献了一份必要的力量。
If nothing else, the attack served to bring the town together again.

叶甫根尼：向你的敏锐嗅觉致敬，维拉同志。你避免了更多的伤亡。
Evgeni: I salute your sense of smell, Comrade Vila. We could have suffered much more severe consequences without your forewarning.

握手，敬礼，像是一切都没有发生过。
Handshakes and salutes are shared, their dispute now absent from anyone's mind.

维拉：这没什么，只是……应对危险的一种天赋的应激反应。
Vila: Think nothing of it. It's just a reflex reaction when there is danger nearby.

她摸了摸手腕，不着痕迹地将凸起的神经按了下去。
She touches her scales, pressing them down until they settle.

叶甫根尼：但这正说明我们需要芝诺的协助——
Evgeni: But this incursion has proved my point. We need Zeno's help.

叶甫根尼：其他人并不具备像你这样的“种族天赋”，他们更容易遇上难以预料的危险，不是么？
Evgeni: The other townspeople are not gifted with your set of talents. We are all vulnerable to the growing dangers, wouldn't you agree?

叶甫根尼：我希望你能更多考虑普通人的处境。
Evgeni: I only ask you to put yourself in their shoes.

他的声音不大，却依然凌厉地刺入维拉的耳中。
He speaks softly, evenly, but even so, the words land like a heavy blow.

维拉：……我接受你的批评，叶甫根尼同志。
Vila: Your criticism is valid and well-accepted, Comrade Evgeni.

维拉：但我必须申明，芝诺对来亚什基的维和行动必须迅速完成。更重要的是，我想这儿的人都不会同意芝诺对我们指手画脚。
Vila: Perhaps I could agree with your plan. Provided Zeno's presence is a temporary one. We just don't want them to change things for us here.

广场的气氛终于缓和了下来。
The atmosphere in the square moves from joyful to serious, as the meaning of their words takes hold.

叶甫根尼：很高兴你们能想通这一点。
Evgeni: I'm glad that you have finally come to realize what is best for us.

叶甫根尼：芝诺是一个严谨而理性的机构，他们致力于维护世界各地的和平。我相信，他们会做出正确的决断。
Evgeni: Zeno is known for their rigorous methods and rational decision-making, and they are committed to maintaining peace around the world. I'm sure they will make the right decision.

叶甫根尼：正如他们与来亚什基过往的无数次合作。我们解决了芝诺的能源问题，成了他们坚固的资源保障。而芝诺，则在第一线解决了许多国际问题。
Evgeni: They trusted us to supply their ore, and we have faithfully played our part in supporting them. Thanks to our help, Zeno has successfully tackled many international issues.

叶甫根尼：来亚什基与芝诺共同努力，为了更美好的世界而拼搏——
Evgeni: It has always been them and us together, fighting for a better world.

克努特：哈哈～
这话说得没错，我们都该为之骄傲——！
Knut: Hahaha! When he puts it that way, he's right. We should be proud of our cooperation!

四周终于产生了一些刻意压低的、自豪的笑声。
Even without a punchline, Knut's deep belly laugh breaks the tension.

叶甫根尼：在这之前，我们理应向芝诺表达敬意。我宣布，排练继续……
Evgeni: Therefore, we will show our appreciation to Zeno for the contributions they've made to the world with our help. Now, let's continue our rehearsals.

吵吵嚷嚷的声音终于停了下来，眼尖的孩子四处张望，终于发现了不对劲。
As the adults return to their duties, a sharp-eyed child notices that someone is missing.

帕索诺：你们瞧，阿夫西维不见啦！
Pasono: Have you seen Avgust? I can't find him!

维拉：嗯——？！
Vila: Hmm?!

尼娜：咦，阿夫西维同学去做什么啦？
Nina: Strange, where did he go?

彼得森：哼，说不定是去偷吃阿廖卡了……违反规矩，自顾自地干自己的事，他最擅长的就是这个！
Pyotr: Hmph, looking for any Alenka left in the cupboards, I'd bet! He's always breaking the rules doing whatever he wants.

尼娜：我们不应该贬低他人，彼得森同学！阿夫西维同学也是我们的一份子……
Nina: We shouldn't talk badly about our classmate, Pyotr! He's one of us.

彼得森沉默着把头低了下去。许久，他才发出比小棕熊还细微的声音。
Pyotr lowers his head, his face crumpling, until at last, he lets out a grumble fit for a bear.

彼得森：对不起……我只是想让大家都做好自己的事。
Pyotr: *sighs* Yes, you're right. I just want everyone to do their best, even him.

维拉：别担心，孩子们，大人们会找到他的。
Vila: Don't worry, kids. We will find him.

维拉拍了拍小姑娘的肩膀。
Vila pats Nina's shoulder softly.

维拉：我们的孩子失踪了，叶甫根尼同志，我要求暂停排练。
Vila: A child is missing, Comrade Evgeni. I suggest a temporary suspension of our rehearsals.

叶甫根尼哼了一声，像是想起了什么。
Evgeni murmurs a half-response, until he catches the weight of her words.

叶甫根尼：又是那个古怪的孩子，这已经不是他第一次偷溜了……
Evgeni: Urgh, it must be that strange kid again! He is always sneaking away like this.

叶甫根尼毫不客气地皱了皱眉，他还想再说些什么，却迎上一双更加坚决的眼睛。
Avgust has been no small trouble in the past. Evgeni frowns, but Vila's determined glare tells him "No" is not an acceptable answer.

维拉：他在填补自己的世界。
Vila: He is only trying to understand the world in his own way.

叶甫根尼：……
Evgeni: ...

FR-02 大发现！ / Big Discoveries!

小镇广场（童话一面）
The question of where their curious little dreamer has disappeared soon becomes a true conundrum,

关心石头的孩子去了哪儿呢？
码头，邮站，电话亭……反正，不在这儿。

逐渐黑屏+窸窸窣窣的嗅闻声
as their search through the dockyard, the post office, and even the town phone booth reveals no trace of him.

他为自己赋予了更重要的迎新任务。
This is, of course, because he has assigned himself a more critical mission: welcoming newcomers.

它伴随着艰难、遥远，以及绵延了一路的向日葵。
A difficult task, especially when it leads him so far away. But he is not alone. His sunflower hops along with him.

阿夫西维：维拉说，向日葵很温暖，是所有人的朋友。
Avgust: Vila once said that sunflowers mean warmth, and that makes them everyone's friends.

阿夫西维：它们热情地欢迎所有客人。
Avgust: They would warmly welcome every guest that comes to town.

阿夫西维：就像我最好的朋友一样，对吗？
Avgust: Just like my best friend here, right?

他扬了扬手上的向日葵，附在对方叶片上小声嘀咕。
He raises the sunflower in his hand and whispers softly to its petals.

阿夫西维：好朋友，每个人都应该有一个好朋友。

而后，他捧起吊坠。
He then picks up the pendant.

一阵古怪的嘟哝后，吊坠散发出幽微的光芒。

向日葵膨胀、夸张地长大

阿夫西维：这样新来的客人就不会孤单了～
Avgust: So that our new guests won't feel so lonely when they come!

稚嫩的脚印继续向前绵延着，印在更模糊的雪地靴的印子上。
The small footprints continue forward through the snow, imprinting over older, larger steps.

他终于赶上了他的新朋友。
He has nearly caught up with Rayashki's newest guest.

北方哨歌：北方哨歌，看来上天还没有完全遗弃你和你的理论……
Windsong: Windsong, seems like life has been good to you and your theory.

她目不转睛地盯着眼前的那群野兽，刷刷地写着，连嘴巴也不肯闲下来。
She stares intently at the beasts in front of her, her written notes hardly keeping pace with her whispered observations.

北方哨歌：看来地脉能量的紊乱不仅体现在卢恩矿石的枯竭，甚至还给这儿的魔精们都打上了几针不同程度的异变剂。
Windsong: The disorder in ley energy here has not only caused the exhaustion of the runium mines, but has also mutated local critters to varying degrees.

北方哨歌：……

Windsong: Then Zeno was right. No wonder they have sent so many researchers here to look for abnormalities, even the crank ones like me.

北方哨歌：很显然，这座镇子的古怪之处远远不止那些过分活跃的常规魔精们……

北方哨歌：可他们又对这些古怪的魔精变异种兴趣缺缺……

Though, in fact, she is the one here uninvited.

Windsong: Just to be clear, I'm not a spy, kid. I'm just a traveler staying in town for the moment.

她随意扬了扬手上的证件，上面画着阿夫西维最熟悉的向日葵图案。
She casually raises an identification card in her hand, a card adorned with a familiar sunflower pattern.

阿夫西维：噢……可我从来没见过你！
Avgust: Oh! But I have never seen you before!

阿夫西维：你住在水里吗？……就像维拉那样。

阿夫西维：——你也有一条漂亮的蓝色尾巴吗？
Avgust: Do you also have a beautiful blue tail?

过于跳脱的思维显然令她难以招架，她费力制止了那个围着她打转的身影。
His strange questions prove difficult to parse, even one at a time, but the little boy circles around her, unleashing more in salvo after salvo.

北方哨歌：虽然我不明白你说的是什么，但毫无疑问，小家伙，我绝对不是你想象中的那种身份。
Windsong: I have no idea what you're talking about, but I'm certain that I'm not what you think I am, little fellow.

北方哨歌：我是个……咳，学者。当投身研究时，我们在大多数时候都深入简出，在谁也找不着的地方，你明白了吗？
Windsong: I am a researcher. We often stay in quiet corners when we work on a project, so you won't see us often. Understand?

Avgust: Researchers? Like those people on TV?

阿夫西维：他们站在很高的台子上，抱着鲜花，说很多很多的话，然后流下眼泪——每个人都能得到一个漂亮的金色奖章。

Avgust: Can I see your medal?

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

孩子的问题总是一针见血。北方哨歌的面庞不自然地抽动着。
This last salvo penetrated deep. Windsong's face twitches unnaturally.

北方哨歌：哈哈——你身上的水晶可真漂亮，它看起来可比那些矿车上的纯粹多了。

她的目光上下飘忽，终于抓住了那颗挂在脖子上的漂亮水晶。
Her gaze centered on it, a beautiful crystal hanging on the boy's neck. A chance possibly to stop his barrage of questions.

阿夫西维：当然，这是爸爸留给我的。
Avgust: Of course. Papa gave it to me.

小小的胸膛骄傲地鼓了起来。
His small chest swells with pride.

北方哨歌：它很珍贵，也很危险……比它更纯粹的，大概只有传说中的卢恩原矿了。对那些战争机器来说，它们是惹人垂涎的战略资源。
Windsong: It is precious, but also very dangerous. A crystal like this is almost as volatile as undiluted runium ore. They use this stuff for war machines!

北方哨歌：孩子，你得收好它，别让陌生人看见了，然后赶紧回家去，好吗？
Windsong: Kid, listen to me, put that away. Go home now, and don't let anyone see it. Understand?

Avgust: Ah!

阿夫西维：你能盖一个很高很高的房顶吗？把整个小镇都保护起来——就像刚才搭起积木那样！

北方哨歌：这只是个小把戏，过一会儿就不见了……

Avgust: Nina, Knut, Vila—everyone should learn from you!

阿夫西维：我也能像你一样，让土地和石头们乖乖听话——做出这些了不起的成就吗？
Avgust: Could I make the dirt and stones listen to me like you did one day? Will I be great like you?

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

北方哨歌：像你这样神神叨叨的孩子，更应该出现在新纪元运动的宝瓶座年代，或是什么冥思团体之类的地方。

北方哨歌：而不是这儿……
Windsong: And do it anywhere but here.

阿夫西维：新纪元运动——是什么？！
Avgust: The New Age Movement? What is that?!

阿夫西维并没有捕捉到对方的无奈。更糟糕的是，他对此产生了更高的兴致。
Her helpless attempt at turning him away goes without notice; worse still, it seems to intrigue him.

阿夫西维：你是从那儿来的吗？
Avgust: Is that where you're from?

北方哨歌：它是一场盛大的风潮，里面有很多有趣的东西。卢恩水晶、新兴学派、无数天马行空的想法……
Windsong: It's not a place. It's a spirit of a time. Full of interesting things—like crystals, new schools of thought, many crazy and creative ideas.

阿夫西维：他们那儿的太阳会闭眼吗？乌云们会吐口水吗？

阿夫西维：大船会在水底下吐泡泡吗……？
Avgust: Will their ships blow bubbles under the water?

孩子不依不饶的纠缠并不使人厌烦。
Somehow, the persistent questions stop being a source of annoyance.

细微的、童稚的温暖拨开了某种尘封已久的乌云。
The subtle warmth of his boundless wonder shakes loose the frost from her heart.

她放弃了早已准备好的熟稔套话与敷衍说辞。
Her smile turning from feigned to genuine.

北方哨歌：当然……他们甚至坚信脚下的世界是一张巨幅图纸，并立志画出上面的一切。

北方哨歌：不仅如此，他们着迷于各种稀奇古怪的问题，索尔兹伯里平原的石头们是从哪儿来的？马尾藻海的船只与飞机又去了哪儿……
Windsong: And not only that, they are obsessed with bizarre ideas. Where did the Stonehenge on the Salisbury Plain come from? Where are the ships and planes which traveled past the Sargasso Sea now?

阿夫西维：我喜欢他们——！
Avgust: I like them!

稚嫩的童声似乎模糊了回忆与现实的边缘，某些隐晦的遐想从记忆里漂浮了上来，令人一阵目眩神迷。
The child's voice blurs the edges between reality and pleasant memories of her past, to a time when there were others that thought like her.

北方哨歌：他们自称为理线师，来自于某个曾经显赫一时的学派……但许多人并不喜欢理线师，也不喜欢他们口中的图纸与答案。
Windsong: They called themselves ley hunters, the apprentices of a once-renowned school of thought. However, few people in academic circles accepted the idea of ley lines as an answer to their questions.

北方哨歌：对理线师来说，他们度过了一个漫长的夜晚。
Windsong: So for these ley hunters, it has been a long walk through a dark night.

阿夫西维：那他们可以到来亚什基来，太阳先生一直住在大家的头顶上！
Avgust: Then they can come to Rayashki! Here, the sun never sets! Half the year, anyways.

阿夫西维：我可以和他们做朋友……等我长大了，我也能成为一位理线师！
Avgust: Then I can be their friend! And when I grow up, I will be a ley hunter too!

北方哨歌紧了紧身上的围巾，像是在抵御某种寒意。
Windsong tightens her scarf, as if warding off a chill.

北方哨歌：恐怕已经来不及了，小家伙。
Windsong: I'm afraid it's a bit too late, little fellow.

北方哨歌：许多人都放弃了，放弃了对未解之谜的解释，放弃了图纸上的直线与曲线……当然也放弃了理线学。
Windsong: Most have already given up. They lost interest in solving the mysteries and lost their faith in finding the curves and the lines. So the study of ley lines has been all but abandoned.

北方哨歌：现在理线学就剩下一根可怜的独苗了。
Windsong: There's only one fool left that hasn't given it up.

北方哨歌说得入神，丝毫没有注意到吱嘎响起的脚步声。
She speaks wistfully, entranced in that daze of memory, oblivious to the nearing sound of footsteps behind her.

阿夫西维：嘘～～～
Avgust: Shhh!

北方哨歌：——？
Windsong: ...?

维拉：你就是那根仅剩的独苗么？——这位我从来没见过的女士。
Vila: And you, I suppose, are this "only one fool," yes?

她拉过藏在一边的阿夫西维，责备地揉了揉孩子的脑袋。
Vila pulls Avgust toward her protectively and reproaches him with a ruffle of the child's hair.

北方哨歌：我必须申明，女士，我绝对没有任何诱拐儿童的想法！
Windsong: Ah! Please, ma'am, believe me, I am not a child abductor!

维拉：嗯……
Vila: Well ...

对方不置可否地点了点头。
Windsong offers a pained gesture towards the boy.

维拉：我想，这儿算不上什么接待客人的好地方。对于新来的朋友，我们有更合适的安排。
Vila: I think this isn't a good place to receive our guest. We have much more appropriate arrangements for new friends.

维拉：不过——
Vila: But ...

维拉：倘若是行为可疑的破坏分子，我们也有另外的处理方式。
Vila: If our guest has any ill intentions, we will retaliate.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: Umm.

FR-03 羽茅地 / Needle-Grass

小镇广场（现实一面）

各怀心思的一行人回到了小镇。
The group, each harboring their own thoughts, returns toward the small town. Vila and Avgust humming out a sing-song tune.

惴惴不安的北方哨歌沉默了一路。
And anxious Windsong remains silent for the journey.

恍惚之际，走在前面的维拉与她似有若无的歌声一同回过头来。
Vila wheels around just as they arrive at the outskirts, keeping up the cadence of the song.

维拉：我们到了。
Vila: We're here.

维拉：向你的热心肠表示感谢，女士。
Vila: Thank you for taking care of our little Comrade Avgust, miss.

北方哨歌：……？
Windsong: ...?

北方哨歌：——不是来审判我或者给我定罪之类的？
Windsong: You mean I'm not here to be questioned? Or arrested?

维拉：呵呵～当然不是。
Vila: *chuckles* Of course not.

维拉：对一切已发生或尚未发生的事情保持乐观与好奇，大概是这儿人们的通病。
Vila: Perhaps we are a little too optimistic, but when we meet a stranger, we prefer to welcome them.

维拉仔细地观察起眼前略显窘迫的身影，值得庆幸的是，她的好奇心并未等待太久。
Vila looks over the awkward figure, reading the expression on her face. The researcher breaks the silence with a stumble.

北方哨歌：北方哨歌。
Windsong: Oh, well, I'm Windsong.

维拉：很特别的名字，听起来——你是从那边来的？
Vila: That's a very unique name. And where is it you come from?

北方哨歌：那边……？算是吧，我来自德涅斯特河的东岸……
Windsong: From the east side of the Dniester River.

她还想再说些什么，微微咸涩的海风挟着脖颈上的细腻鳞片便一同凑到了她的跟前。
Vila's scales are hit with a sea breeze. It halts her and their conversation.

维拉：……
Vila: *sniffs*

北方哨歌：——？！
Windsong: ...?!

许久，对方终于抬起头来。
The teacher breaks out from her pause.

维拉：无意冒犯，女士。你的身上混杂着许多我从未闻到过的气息。
Vila: No offense, Ms. But you have a complicated and unfamiliar scent about you.

维拉：它们有的像坚硬的石头，有的又像海岸线上的灯塔、潮热的雨水……但至少，我没有从中闻到丝毫敌意。
Vila: The smell of hard rocks, a lighthouse by the sea, rainwater in a humid summer. Mm. Nothing hostile, though.

北方哨歌：呵呵……无根漂泊者大都如此。
Windsong: *chuckles* I think most rootless travelers like me smell like that.

维拉：欢迎你到来亚什基来，北方哨歌女士。
Vila: Welcome to Rayashki, Ms. Windsong.

维拉认真地敬了个礼。
Vila motions inward to the town.

北方哨歌：……谢谢。
Windsong: Thank you.

北方哨歌：我理解你们的警惕，但……
Windsong: I understand your caution. But ...

北方哨歌同样狐疑地打量着对方。
Windsong is seized by her own suspicion, spying the unusual scales on her host's neck.

维拉不动声色地扯紧袖口，缩了缩脖子，稍微向后退了几步。
Vila catches the glance. She subtly tugs at her sleeve and shrinks her neck into her coat, taking a few cautious steps backward.

维拉：别担心，这并不是恶性疾病，只是些无足轻重的小事。
Vila: You have nothing to worry about; it's not a disease.

维拉：我们还是来聊聊你的故事吧……
听你的说法，你是一位研究学者。
Vila: Anyway, let's talk about you. I heard that you're a researcher.

维拉：不久前，这儿曾涌入过许多学者和探险家们，他们流连于小镇的各个角落，就像现在的你。我以为他们受到了来亚什基的吸引……
Vila: Not long ago, many of your peers visited here. They wandered around and looked under every rock and floorboard in the town, like you do. I thought perhaps they were attracted here by the town itself.

维拉：但令人遗憾的是，没过多久，他们便一个接一个地，揣着失望离开了。
Vila: But regrettably, not long after, they left one after another in disappointment.

维拉：当然，我也很失望。
Vila: I was disappointed, too.

她的语气并不像自己所说的那般失落，更多的是好奇。
There is a curiousness in her tone.

维拉：你会和他们一样吗？
Vila: Will you be like them?

北方哨歌：哈哈……
Windsong: Haha.

北方哨歌：他们大多是声名在外的学者，自然不会对着一个看不见方向的研究投注过久的目光。但我……早已习惯了失败。
Windsong: Those people are famous scholars; of course, they won't spend too much time on a project with unclear prospects. But I, I'm used to those.

她摊了摊手，没有继续说下去。
She spreads her hands out to the town, with nothing more to say.

维拉：为你无畏的探索精神——致敬。
Vila: I salute you for your courage and spirit of exploration.

北方哨歌：我以为你的态度会更恶劣一点儿……像是“你们凭什么染指这儿，这是小镇的私有财产”……
Windsong: I thought you ... I thought you might be more hostile to me. Shouting things like "Who do you think you are to prowl about on our private property!"

维拉：……？
Vila: ...?

北方哨歌：外面的人都觉得理线学是羽茅，在西伯利亚的土壤中遍地都是的那一种，不仅毫不起眼，缺乏营养，更是惹人厌烦，最大的用途是抢夺属于它们的营养。
Windsong: Many see the study of ley lines like finding a needle in the grass of a Siberian field—wasted effort with negligible results.

维拉：劳动并无高低贵贱之分。
Vila: There's no such thing as meaningless work.

维拉：不论是什么身份，来自何方，也不论你投身于何种事业，都能在这儿发光发热。
Vila: It doesn't matter who you are, where you're from, or what you do. You will find your purpose here.

维拉的目光投向不远处被其他孩子们围在中间的阿夫西维。
Vila shifts her gaze over to Avgust, who has been found and surrounded by the other children not far away.

北方哨歌：难怪这儿能有阿夫西维这样……特别的孩子。
Windsong: Is that so? No wonder how you have such an unusual student like Avgust.

维拉：你也没有破坏这样的一颗童心，不是么？
Vila: All that childhood wonder, innocence—somehow you've preserved it in him, haven't you?

一旁的孩子显然并不关心成年人之间的问候，他们有着独属于孩子们的世界与规则。
The children seem unconcerned with the new adult; they have their own world and their own rules to be addressed.

阿夫西维：……我们的表演结束了吗？
Avgust: Is the show finished?

尼娜：排练暂时中止了，阿夫西维同学……叶甫根尼先生刚才气冲冲地离开了。
Nina: We cancelled our rehearsal, Avgust. Mr. Evgeni just left red-faced.

彼得森：是啊——！多亏了你的叛逃，临走之前，他取消了食堂菜单上的奶酪。
Pyotr: Yes! And he canceled the "Friendship" cheese on the food menu, all thanks to you.

阿夫西维：可我在欢迎新朋友呀～
Avgust: But I was welcoming our new friend!

彼得森：你害得我们失去了宝贵的“友谊”……这全是你的错，阿夫西维。
Pyotr: And we have lost our cheese because of you. This is all your fault!

彼得森：你是来亚什基最调皮的孩子！
Pyotr: You're the most bothersome kid in Rayashki!

阿夫西维：我知道，“最”是很好的意思！——谢谢你的夸奖，彼得森。
Avgust: I know that word! "Most" means the best! So thank you, Pyotr.

彼得森：你——！
Pyotr: You!

其他的孩子们也凑了上来。
The other children gather close.

帕索诺：阿夫西维同学，我们都没有见过这位新朋友，你该不会又在骗人吧？
Pasono: Avgust, we don't see anyone new here. You're not lying again, are you?

阿夫西维：她在维拉的身边，她们打招呼，分享脚印，一起唱歌……
Avgust: She's with Vila! They greet each other, share footprints, and even sing together.

阿夫西维：北方哨歌也是“最”，她画出很多线条，在雪地上、海鸥的身上——
Avgust: Windsong is also the "best"! She can draw many lines on the snow, and even on a seagull.

彼得森：……
Pyotr: ...

彼得森：她该不会和你一样奇怪吧？
Pyotr: We're not having another freak in town, right?

尼娜：是在黑板上画画吗？就像维拉老师那样。
Nina: Do you mean drawing on the blackboard? Like Ms. Vila did?

阿夫西维故作神秘地摇了摇头。
Avgust playfully shakes his head, feigning an air of mystery.

阿夫西维：她捏好泥土，墙壁就竖了起来，再吹一口气，房子就建好了……
Avgust: She made the earth turn into a tall tall wall, and she blew her breath at it, and made a building appear.

阿夫西维：如果有许多理线师一起工作的话，大家就能把向日葵送到天上去！
Avgust: If we had enough ley hunters like her working together, we would be able to send sunflowers high into the sky!

彼得森：这听起来没什么稀奇的～工厂的每一个叔叔都擅长建房子。
Pyotr: Ah, that's not so tough! All the men in town know how to build stuff like that!

彼得森：等我们长大，我们也能学会使用锄头和铲子。
Pyotr: When we grow up, we will work like them, with hoes and shovels.

帕索诺：可那还要很久很久呢……
Pasono: But that will take ages.

尼娜：如果我们现在就学会了理线师的魔法……那我们就能帮大人们一起造房子了！
Nina: If we can learn how to build like the ley hunters, then we could help the adults right now!

彼得森：你们可别被阿夫西维骗了——！
Pyotr: Don't listen to Avgust!

孩子们热烈地讨论着，彼得森与他鼓起的脸颊一同被挤了出来。
The children discuss the notion animatedly. Pyotr finds himself squeezed out of their huddle.

他快步跑到大人们的跟前。
He puffs his cheeks and hurries over to the adults.

彼得森：向您问好，北方哨歌女士。
Pyotr: Greetings, Ms. Windsong.

北方哨歌：嗯……？
Windsong: Mm?

彼得森：您真的能把土地变成各种各样的形状，搭起高高的房子吗？
Pyotr: Is it true? Can you really shape the earth into different things and build things from it?

北方哨歌：……这是一种短暂起效的神秘术，它来自我所研究的学派，理线学。
Windsong: Not exactly. The things I build with my arcane skill have only a momentary effect. I can't use it that way. I learned it as a part of my research while studying ley lines.

其他的孩子们也拥上前来。
The other children join in.

尼娜：北方哨歌女士，阿夫西维说的都是真的吗？
Nina: Ms. Windsong, those things Avgust told us, are they true?

尼娜：闭眼的太阳，吐泡泡的乌云，还有能看清一切的图纸……
Nina: The sun that closes its eyes, the dark clouds that spit on people, and the lines that can reveal everything.

帕索诺：北方哨歌女士，您能像维拉老师一样，为我们讲课吗？
Pasono: Ms. Windsong, will you be our teacher, like Ms. Vila?

彼得森：您能拿出证据吗……？
Pyotr: Can you prove anything?

维拉：调皮鬼们，一个个来。
Vila: Kids. One question at a time.

越来越多的孩子们簇拥着北方哨歌，这显然令她措手不及。
The children surround Windsong, catching her off guard.

她略带歉意地望向维拉。
She looks apologetically at Vila.

北方哨歌：抱歉……维拉女士，我会向孩子们说明的。
Windsong: Sorry, Ms. Vila. I should explain it to them.

北方哨歌：这只是个被大众疏远的非正式学科……沿用世俗评价的说法，“依赖神秘学家视角的观测”、“结论与大众需求不符”……
Windsong: Mine is not a ... formal discipline. Many people believe that it "relies too much on the observations of arcanists" and "the conclusions aren't useful for the public."

北方哨歌：大概并不适合这个年纪的孩子们。
Windsong: So it is best that you kids do not study it.

她耸了耸肩，呼出的温热水汽在她的面庞前起落。
She shrugs her shoulders.

北方哨歌：我想，它仅仅适合像我这样的顽固分子的自娱自乐。
Windsong: A pursuit of passion, fit for only a very stubborn fool like me.

维拉：原来如此。
Vila: I see.

维拉会意地点了点头，她转过身去，面向一团热闹的云。
Vila nods in understanding.

维拉：当然可以，孩子们。
Vila: Then, you must show us all about it. Shouldn't she, kids?

维拉：北方哨歌女士很愿意为你们开展一堂特别的通识课。
Vila: I'm sure Ms. Windsong would be very happy to give us a special lesson about her studies.

北方哨歌：嗯……？！
Windsong: Huh?!

阿夫西维：太好啦——！
Avgust: Yay!

而后，这团云转眼便飘向了更远的地方。
Escaping this unasked-for obligation may prove more difficult than expected.

北方哨歌：维拉女士，你没听明白吗……？
Windsong: Ms. Vila! I thought I made myself clear!

维拉：你为自身热爱的事业付出了许多努力，不是么？
Vila: You have worked hard in this "pursuit of passion," haven't you?

北方哨歌：理线学是门“多余”的学问。
Windsong: Regardless, the study of ley lines is ... Well, it's useless.

北方哨歌轻拍着手中泛黄的笔记本，上面画满了密密麻麻的线条与笔记。
Windsong lightly taps her yellowed notebook filled with cryptic scribbles and notes.

维拉：多余……？
Vila: Useless?

北方哨歌：世界上早就有了相当完备的地理学。
Windsong: These kids should learn something like geography. It's a much more thorough and important field.

北方哨歌：无论是人们，还是其他的学术机构，他们并不需要一个看上去和它差不多的，立足于更“狭隘”的神秘学视角的小众学科。
Windsong: As far as the general public and academic institutions are concerned, the study of ley lines is just a niche aspect of geography, worse still, one that is solely accessible to arcanists.

北方哨歌：瓜分研究经费，分流研究人员……大部分人都不乐意见到这样。
Windsong: To devote any real time to its investigation would take up valuable research funds and equally valuable researchers.

维拉：一种糟糕的学术倾轧。
Vila: At least that was how they felt about it.

维拉皱了皱眉头，用力踩实脚下的土壤。
Vila furrows her brow.

北方哨歌：……谁知道呢？
Windsong: Who can say for certain?

维拉：那么你呢，你也认为理线学是毫无意义的么？
Vila: What about you? Do you also think that the study of ley lines is a waste of funds and manpower?

北方哨歌：我——当然不……理线学并非一无是处。它能让人了解当地的神秘学现象，分析神秘动物，了解地表甚至是地壳中的秘密。
Windsong: I, of course, I don't. Through ley lines, we can detect arcanum-related events in the area, learn about local arcane creatures, and find the secrets hidden both above and below the earth's surface.

北方哨歌：只是……我目前还没法证明更多的事。
Windsong: But, I can't yet prove this to people.

维拉拍了拍北方哨歌的肩膀。
Vila places her hand on Windsong's shoulder.

维拉：那么，我们也一样。
Vila: Well, you don't have to prove it alone.

维拉：外界的承认与否并没有那么重要，能否发挥作用才是最重要的。
Vila: It doesn't matter what others think of your work. The only important thing is finding its uses.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

维拉：最早的时候，来亚什基仅仅是一个鲜为人知的偏远极区，人们为了同一个理想来到这儿。值得庆幸的是，我们在这儿发掘出了卢恩矿石。
Vila: At first, Rayashki was just a remote village far north in the Arctic Circle. People came here to share a dream of a better future. It was only by luck that we found the runium.

维拉：再后来，芝诺找到了我们，成了来亚什基的第一个合作者。
Vila: Then Zeno approached us and became our business partner.

维拉：这儿的人们为之奋斗六十余年，将它建设成了现在的样子。
Vila: For over 60 years, people here have worked together to make it what it is now.

维拉：我们为它创造了学校，创造了游泳馆、电影院……当然，这也是为了我们每一个人。
Vila: We built the school, the swimming pool, and the cinema ... For everyone.

维拉：来亚什基接纳也鼓舞着身处其中的每一个人……当然也包括你与理线学。
Vila: Rayashki embraces and takes in every newcomer. You and your studies are no exception.

维拉：我们殊途同归，不是么？
Vila: This is where our paths meet.

维拉亲切地笑了笑，像一阵暌违已久的暖风。
Vila smiles warmly. It hits like a warm sea breeze.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

一双掩藏起棘刺与棱角的手伸到了北方哨歌的面前。
A pair of hands, concealing sharp scales, extends toward Windsong.

维拉：我需要申明的是——
Vila: Please know that ...

维拉：这一邀请并不只是为了鼓励你，更是为了我们的未来。
Vila: I'm not just doing this for you. I'm doing this for a better future.

推镜

维拉望向不远处的孩子们，有人正认真地对着一株向日葵敬礼。
Vila glances at the children not far away. Some of them seem to be solemnly saluting a sunflower, as if it were a security team guard.

维拉：最优秀的科学家与劳动者们往往诞生于全科教育与通识教育并进的时代。
Vila: A well-rounded education is vital in bringing up the next generation of scientists and workers.

维拉：孩子们理应接受更丰富、更全面的知识，哪怕它并未受到广泛的认可。
Vila: Our children should learn more about this world, even from those perspectives and types of knowledge that aren't widely accepted.

北方哨歌会意地看了过去，她目光与阿夫西维撞在一起，后者兴奋地向她挥手。
Windsong looks out to them and meets the face of her unexpected friend. He waves back excitedly.

回

北方哨歌：感谢你的邀请，维拉女士。
Windsong: Thank you, Ms. Vila.

她回握住那只冰凉却格外热情的手。
She clasps her hand; it is colder than expected, but welcoming.

FR-04 园丁对花儿说 / Said the Gardener to Flowers

北方哨歌：理线学希望将世界变成一张简洁的图纸。
Windsong: The study of ley line sees the world as a clear map.

北方哨歌：在我们眼里，城市是一个个整齐的方格，大自然是许多条交叠的曲线。
Windsong: The cities look like squares to us, while natural landscapes appear to be curves overlapping one another.

北方哨歌：但世界上有许多奇怪的地方，比如发生大爆炸的通古斯、神秘的北纬30度……它们并不能被归入其中。
Windsong: Many bizarre places in the world, such as the location of the Tunguska explosion or the mysterious 30th Parallel North, can't be drawn in squares and curves like cities and ordinary landscapes.

北方哨歌：所以我们不得不将它们画出来。
Windsong: We need to find a way to indicate them,

北方哨歌：以更清晰的方式。
Windsong: in a clear, precise way.

阿夫西维：是迷宫！
Avgust: It's a maze!

北方哨歌：实际上，这是一张属于某座城市的地脉能量网。当然，你们也可以将它视为迷宫。
Windsong: Well, it is the ley line map of a city. But you are right. It does look like a maze.

北方哨歌：首先，我想给各位介绍理线学理论中最重要的概念——地脉能量。
Windsong: To begin with, I should introduce the most crucial concept in the study of ley lines—that of ley energy.

北方哨歌：这是一种特殊的能量形式，我们能从城市的任何地方观察到它的存在。它们从地底向上渗出、蒸腾，在一切生物与非生物之中富集。
Windsong: It is a special energy which we can easily detect throughout the town. See how it comes out from underneath the ground and goes into the local biosphere, circulating around like a system.

北方哨歌：如果将城市本身看作一张巨大的食物网，地脉能量则位于食物网的最底层。
Windsong: If we think of the town's ley lines as a food web, then ley energy lies at its foundation.

阿夫西维：大鱼吃小鱼，小鱼吃——更小的鱼！
Avgust: Like how big fish eat small fish, and small fish eat even smaller fish!

他抓住了这个更简洁的形容词。
The boy's comparative is simple but essentially correct.

北方哨歌：是的，它们是最小的“小鱼”，“大鱼”们吃掉它们，我们抓住“大鱼”，分析它们的鱼肉，从而找到别的“大鱼”们。
Windsong: Exactly. They are the smallest "fish" eaten by the "big fish." If we catch the "big fish" and study what they eat, we will know where to find the other "big fish."

北方哨歌：而后，地脉能量……咳，随着“大鱼”们的死亡与分解，“小鱼”回到原点，就像跃入一条永恒循环的长河。
Windsong: And the ley energy, I mean, when the "big fish" die and break down, the "small fish" will go back to where they first came from. The circulation goes on and on.

维拉：这是个很有趣的假说，北方哨歌女士。
Vila: You've put it very well, Ms. Windsong.

维拉：它正如我们所见的雨水、河流……从大海中来，也终将回到海洋。
Vila: Like the rainwater that comes from the ocean, to the rivers, and returns back to the ocean.

她的语气明显地兴奋了起来，连鳞片都微微张开。
Her tone rises, the scales along her neck unfurling slightly.

北方哨歌：你理解得很快。
Windsong: You are a quick learner.

北方哨歌：但与之不同的是，地脉能量的富集现象远比水源与小鱼要明显的多。当我们找到它的源头，我们便能借此发现它所流经的一切痕迹。
Windsong: But it is not exactly like water. The concentration of ley energy is far more noticeable than that of a lake or a school of fish. Once we find its densest spot, we will be able to trace it back to its source.

尼娜：那这些发亮的光点是什么呢……？
Nina: Then what are these bright spots?

北方哨歌：它们代表着地脉能量最丰裕的地方，也在某种程度上指引着地脉能量的流向。
Windsong: These are the energy-rich locations. In a way, they indicate the energy flow.

阿夫西维：比天上的星星更多——！
Avgust: So many, they look like stars in the sky!

北方哨歌：是的，确认地脉能量的富裕点是一份需要耗费许多时间与人力的工作。
Windsong: Yes, and finding these locations can be very costly in terms of time and manpower.

帕索诺：那……发现它们之后呢？
Pasono: Then, what do we do after finding them?

北方哨歌：它们是理线师们的“眼睛”。我们观察地脉能量的走向，分析地脉能量中富集的成分与痕迹，把它们与现实中存在的资源一一对应……
Windsong: They can "tell" us many things. The ley hunters will follow their courses, analyze the components in them, and match those components to each resource.

北方哨歌：那些无法确认来源的痕迹，便预示着我们尚未发现的新资源。
Windsong: Some of the components don't match with any of the known resources, which means there might be a new resource waiting to be discovered.

北方哨歌：当然，周边那些怪模怪样的魔精们，它们的痕迹与习性一定会在地脉能量中有所显示。
Windsong: Of course, from the ley energy, we can also learn about the local critters.

彼得森：您说的话与阿夫西维一样难懂！
Pyotr: You talk about strange things, almost like Avgust does!

不服气的孩子撅起嘴巴，他显然难以相信这一切。

在浮窗道具上的特效，一个个小光点在无规则地游荡
He pouts, finding all of this hard to believe.

彼得森：它们不就是些普通的线条吗？
Pyotr: These are just lines.

阿夫西维：蚯蚓们在跳舞，摇摇——摆摆——它们一定很快乐～
Avgust: Like dancing earthworms! They wriggle, they twist, they are having fun!

阿夫西维：它们跳到了水花上，跳到了四方格……最后跳回了小圆球里！
Avgust: Jumping on the waves, then into the little boxes, and back into the little balls!

彼得森：唉……这儿又多了一位“阿夫西维”。
Pyotr: *sighs* Great, we have two of them now.

收起浮窗
课室

尼娜：它们看上去很有趣，但我们不明白……
Nina: They look interesting, but we don't really understand.

但无论如何，理解一个新理论对孩子们而言过于复杂了，哪怕只是一张图纸。
Her theories are a bit too complex for children at this level, even with the aid of a drawing.

北方哨歌：别灰心，小家伙们……实际上，这只是个半成品。
Windsong: Cheer up, kids. It's not finished yet.

北方哨歌：绘制完整的地图是一项复杂的工作。它需要许多理线师们一同考察、分析环境，甚至需要深入城市禁区与危险的地方……
Windsong: Ley line cartography is complicated. It takes the efforts of many ley hunters working together, investigating the area, even braving dangerous and forbidden places.

北方哨歌：所以我们始终没能绘制出一张完整的地脉能量图。
Windsong: To this day, we've never been able to finish a completed ley energy map.

得到安慰的孩子们平静下来，但仍有人沉浸在线条的世界之中。
Their enthusiasm dims, but some remain immersed in the world of ley lines.

阿夫西维兴奋地扬起了那张并不完整的图纸。
Avgust raises up the incomplete drawing.

阿夫西维：我、我知道了！
Avgust: I know! I know it now!

阿夫西维：——这是我们的来亚什基！
Avgust: This is Rayashki!

维拉：……？
Vila: ...?

帕索诺：啊！原来如此——这儿是游泳场，那个方格是我们的广场，那些小圆球是我们的家！
Pasono: Ah! I see it too! And here is the swimming pool. That little square is our square. These little balls are our homes!

尼娜：我住在这儿，就在你左边的第三个圆球。
Nina: Oh! I live here, the third ball on the left of yours.

孩子此起彼伏地惊讶着，北方哨歌鼓起了掌。
The children react with surprise. Windsong applauds.

北方哨歌：你果然很敏锐，阿夫西维……这确实是来亚什基的地脉能量图。
Windsong: You're very bright, Avgust. This is the ley energy map of Rayashki.

尼娜：可是，北方哨歌老师，您为什么要画下我们的小镇呀？
Nina: But, Ms. Windsong, why are you mapping the energy of our town?

尼娜：难道这儿还有连我们也不知道的秘密吗……？
Nina: Have you found any secrets that we don't know?

北方哨歌：小家伙们，你们看到的只是它的表面，而地脉能量会告诉我们完整的答案。
Windsong: Children, right now, you can only see what's above the ground, but there is even more ley energy beneath the ground.

北方哨歌摇了摇头，像是回到了某种久违的过去，台下的人们认真地倾听着关于理线学的一切。
Windsong lowers her head, feeling momentarily transported back to a time long past, while her audience listens intently below.

北方哨歌：太阳会一直挂在天上吗？远处的冰山会消融吗？地底下又有多少秘密？
Windsong: Will the sun always be in the sky? Will the glaciers ever melt away? What lies in the darkness beneath us?

北方哨歌：小镇的周围是否又藏着你们从没见过的魔精，我们又应该如何应付它们呢？
Windsong: Are there other critters around here that you've never seen? How should we deal with them?

这一话题显然更能吸引孩子们的兴趣。
This topic sets off a clamor of excitement from the children.

帕索诺：我听说过——！学校的窗户上就出现过许多奇怪的脚印。
Pasono: I heard once that there were many strange footprints next to the school windows.

尼娜：食堂的帕特里基大叔也见过，那是一种长着六只脚的可怕怪物，腿上全是比锉刀更锋利的刺！
Nina: Uncle Patrik saw it! A monster with six legs, and each one has spikes!

北方哨歌：奇肯恩【Qiqirn】，一种小巧的犬科魔精，大多时候生存在寒冷的地方。
Windsong: That must be a Qiqirn, a small sized canidae critter, mostly seen in cold areas.

北方哨歌：当然，由于受地脉能量变化而导致的反季节情况的影响，它们确实出现在了这里，那条深蓝色的线条正是它的痕迹。
Windsong: But the ley energy might have affected the weather of their habitat, or they wouldn't be here in Rayashki in summer. The deep blue line here shows that particular one's movement.

彼得森：帕特里基大叔肯定是喝醉了……
Pyotr: Or maybe Uncle Patrik could have drunk too much.

北方哨歌：从它们体内所富集的地脉能量可以看出，它们主要的食物是雪地下的泥土与小虫，且常出没于离小镇更近的地方。
Windsong: The ley energy accumulated in them suggests that they mostly feed on moss and worms under the snow and stay near town.

北方哨歌：我们可以推断，这是一种温顺的草食性魔精，且对人类的行为相当好奇。如果你们见到了它，我想，喂食比驱赶要有用得多。
Windsong: We can infer that this is a docile, herbivorous kind of critter that is merely curious about human behavior. I think feeding them will be much more useful than driving them away.

收起浮窗
Vila nods thoughtfully.

维拉若有所思地点了点头。

维拉：自打小镇周边的魔精泛滥以来，保卫队就见到了许多从未见过的新怪物。尽管我能感受到些许它们的怪异，但我始终没能理解它们的差异……
Vila: Since these critters began to overrun the area, the defense team has encountered many new creatures. I can feel there's something strange about them, but I can't yet understand the differences.

维拉：你为我们提供了一个新鲜的视角，北方哨歌女士。我想，这或许能解决保卫队面临的许多难题。
Vila: You provided a different angle on the situation, Ms. Windsong. I believe it could help the defense team greatly.

新课题，新发现，大人们的，孩子们的，源源不断。
These new discoveries have provoked interest in the teacher and her students alike.

阿夫西维：炉子里的火熄灭了，蜜蜂和风筝在水池跳舞，围墙长出白色的苔藓……
Avgust: The fires in the furnaces are out, the bees and kites dance around the pond, white mosses on the wall.

阿夫西维：呜呜～天上的石头要砸下来了！
Avgust: Oh, oh! Stones will fall down from the sky!

北方哨歌：嗯……？！
Windsong: Huh?!

稚嫩而清晰的结论显然震惊了不止一人。
His bizarre yet ominous statements seem to upset the others.

彼得森：你在胡说些什么呢，阿夫西维！
Pyotr: Stop saying these strange things, Avgust!

彼得森：那些可怕的魔精只会乖乖地待在小镇的外面，保卫队会保护好大家！小镇里面是最安全的地方！
Pyotr: The defense team will keep the critters out of town and protect everyone!

彼得森：这儿更不会有什么石头砸下来——！
Pyotr: And there will not be any stones falling from the sky!

彼得森气鼓鼓地站了起来，拳头握得很紧。
Pyotr stands up, his fists clenched and face flush red.

阿夫西维：你难过吗……？彼得森。
Avgust: Is everything alright, Pyotr?

彼得森：它们……它们都是假的——来亚什基很安全，我们可以一直住在这儿！
Pyotr: You! You're lying! Rayashki is safe. It will be our home forever!

北方哨歌：我不想骗你，小家伙。但阿夫西维的说法并不完全是错的，我同样有类似的设想——
Windsong: I hate to tell you this, kid. But what Avgust just said could be right. I have the same feeling that ...

北方哨歌：像现在这样的好天气，大概持续不了太久了。
Windsong: The good weather here won't last too long.

她望向窗外，天灰蒙蒙的，像是蒙上了一层阴影。
She gazes outward. The sky above is gray and growing darker.

北方哨歌：瞧瞧那些灰白相间的粗线条～
Windsong: Look at those thick, gray lines.

北方哨歌：它们是云朵与水汽的痕迹。而现在，它们混成了一团。
Windsong: Those are the traces of cloud movements and moisture. Now, they're mingled together.

尼娜：可太阳一直都在呀……维拉老师说过，来亚什基的极昼还会持续很久呢～
Nina: But the sun will still be shining. Ms. Vila said that the polar day will last for a very, very long time!

北方哨歌：当然，历年的天气数据不会骗人。它告诉我们，在近期的几个月里，这儿的天气都不会有什么变化。
Windsong: Ms. Vila was right, and past statistics don't lie. According to the data, the weather here should continue for the next few months.

北方哨歌：可就理线学的推测来说，这儿的天气极其不稳定，随时可能转向更糟糕的状况。
Windsong: Yet the ley lines say otherwise. They say the weather will be extremely unpredictable.

彼得森：您在骗人——！
电视上的播报员说过，这几个月，来亚什基的天气都很凉爽。
Pyotr: You are making things up! The forecaster on TV said the weather in Rayashki will be temperate in the coming months.

北方哨歌：当然，官方给出的数据总是对的，但这并不绝对。
Windsong: And the weather forecaster was right according to his analysis, but life is full of surprises.

维拉：我能理解你的担忧，北方哨歌女士。我也感受到了周围冰山的轻微融化，它们似乎成为了更温暖的水流，而又升上天空……
Vila: I know why you're concerned, Ms. Windsong. I feel the glaciers are melting slightly faster than usual. There's going to be a warm front forming from the melting water.

北方哨歌讶异地看着台下，预想中的反对与鄙夷并未抵达。
Windsong looks at her audience. She had half-hoped for some opposition from them.

尼娜：那、那天上真的会有可怕的石头出现吗？
Nina: But, but will there really be stones falling from the sky?

北方哨歌：我不能保证，小姑娘～
Windsong: I can't say anything for certain just yet, kid.

北方哨歌：以目前这份残缺的地脉能量图来看，许多痕迹都没能对应上它们的主人，理线学暂时无法给出更确切的结论……
Windsong: All I have is this incomplete map, and as you can see, many sources of the marks and traces haven't been located, which means we can't come up with a precise calculation.

北方哨歌：但毫无疑问，天气的恶化、环境的改变，甚至某些更危险的魔精……它们都有可能出现在来亚什基。
Windsong: But there's no question that Rayashki will soon face many challenges. The weather could become much worse, the environment might change, maybe some unknown critters might turn up.

彼得森：……
Pyotr: ...

彼得森：我才不相信……你们都是骗子！
Pyotr: Liar! You are all liars!

彼得森：小镇是我们的家园，它是最好的地方！
Pyotr: Rayashki is our home, so it can't be dangerous!

下课铃声不合时宜地响了起来。
The class bell rings at an inopportune moment.

孩子们一前一后地冲出了教室。
The children rush out of the classroom one after another.

阿夫西维：彼得森，魔王的羽毛是不能被打湿的。
Avgust: Pyotr, you can't fly if your feathers get wet!

北方哨歌叹了口气，尽管还没能适应自己的新身份，但她得跟上孩子们的脚步。
Windsong sighs. Although she hasn't fully adapted to her new role, she must keep up with the children.

维拉及时地拦住了她。
Vila intercepts her.

维拉：一堂新课程的学习总需要一点儿时间，不是吗？
Vila: They will need some time to take in all this new knowledge, don't you agree?

小镇广场（童话一面）

彼得森蹲在地上，小声地嘟哝着。

向日葵也靠了过来。
A sunflower, and the boy attached to it, approaches.

彼得森：你是来嘲笑我的吗……？
Pyotr: Are you here to laugh at me?

FR-05 手风琴 / Accordion

北大西洋暖流的风并未吹及这里。
The warm current of the ocean is a stranger to this place.

但沉寂已久的码头确实收获了久违的喧闹。
The long-silent dock seems to be pining for use, for visitors, to bustle once more with industry.

有人在码头上远眺，有如沉默的塑像。
A lone figure stands there, resolute, unblinking.

叶甫根尼：……
Evgeni: ...

维拉努力地伸展身体，她手腕和脚踝上的鳞片裸露出来，在一片白色的映照下熠熠生光。
Vila stretches out as she stands beside him. The scales on her wrists and ankles catch the light, shimmering against a white reflection in the water.

维拉：你真的认为寻求芝诺的帮助是个好选择吗？
Vila: Do you really think it's a good idea to turn to Zeno for help?

叶甫根尼：为了驱逐盘踞在港口的魔精，我们甚至将矿区周边的人手都抽调了过来。
Evgeni: We have drawn almost every man and woman from the mining facilities to get rid of the critters nesting around the port.

叶甫根尼：保卫队的轻伤人员超过五成，其中的一部分人受伤更加严重，需要在家休养半月以上。
Evgeni: Most of the defense team were injured. Some lightly, but others got much worse. It will be weeks before they can return to duty.

叶甫根尼：如果再发生类似上次排练时的大规模魔精袭击事件，恐怕不是负伤这么简单了……
Evgeni: If an attack like the one at the rehearsal happens again, I'm not sure we will be able to protect ourselves.

他的身躯毫不动摇，目光落在更遥远的废弃矿山上。
His stance doesn't waver, but his face turns stiffly toward the abandoned mine far in the distance.

叫不出名字的尖嘴鸥鸟呼啸着掠过白茫茫的大地，此起彼伏的嘶吼声遥遥传来。
Kittiwakes screech as they swoop down over the vast white tundra.

维拉：……
Vila: ...

叶甫根尼：现在许多人都在为芝诺的到来而置气……我希望你能清醒一点，维拉。
Evgeni: I know most of our people are frustrated with Zeno's arrival. But I expected better from you, Vila.

叶甫根尼：人们信任你，愿意跟随在你身后，但这并不代表着正确。你们太年轻，对这个世界的认知尚不全面。
Evgeni: People trust you, and they will follow you, but that doesn't make you right. Maybe you're still too young to see the dangers.

维拉：历史不正是在一步步试错中向前的么？
Vila: I might be wrong, but history is a long lesson in learning what is right through being unafraid to be wrong.

叶甫根尼：可留给来亚什基的时间不多了。
Evgeni: Sadly, we don't have time for trial and error.

维拉：所以你替这儿的所有人做出了决定，而毫不在乎他们是否接受？
Vila: And this is your excuse for making decisions for us against our will?

叶甫根尼：我会为我做的一切决定负责，我保证。
Evgeni: I will hold myself responsible for my decisions. In that, you have my word.

谈话不可避免地又一次陷入僵局。
Their conversation reaches deadlock once again.

好在，我们仍能见到一个更简单的世界。
Fortunately, elsewhere, there are others with fewer and simpler burdens.

阿夫西维：今天是举行欢迎仪式的日子。维拉说，当钟声响起的时候，乌龟学院的大人物们就会来到我们的小镇。
Avgust: Today is the day of our welcome ceremony. Vila said, when the bell rings, the important people from the tortoise academy will arrive.

阿夫西维：是的，每一个人都很高兴。
Avgust: Everyone looks excited.

阿夫西维：尼娜穿上了她最漂亮的裙子，她一定能跳得很好。
Avgust: Nina has put on her best dress. I know she will be great on stage.

阿夫西维：帕索诺即将与彼得森决斗，他必须保护好公主。
Avgust: Pasono will duel with Pyotr. It's his duty to protect the princess.

阿夫西维：叶甫根尼先生为我安排了新的工作。
Avgust: As for me, I got a new job from Mr. Evgeni.

阿夫西维：“敬礼，握手，向来到这儿的每一位先生致以最诚挚的问候。”
Avgust: "Salute, shake hands, and give them the warmest welcome."

孩子努力地回想着肩负在身的重大使命。
The child nods solemnly, aware of the weighty mission he must undertake.

很快，这位新晋的仪仗队员便迎来了第一位客人。
The little standard-bearer stands ready to receive Rayashki's latest guests.

奇肯恩：呜嗷、嗷——！
Qiqirn: Boawh ... arrh!

阿夫西维：咦……？水里出现了泡泡！
Avgust: What this? There are bubbles in the water!

咧开嘴的魔精从水中探出头来，两双懵懂的眼睛毫无准备地交错在一起。
The critter pops its head out of the water, two eyes staring out at the boy with bewilderment.

阿夫西维：我们又见面了，奇肯恩！……你在水面上种太阳吗？
Avgust: We meet again, Qiqirn! Are you planting sunflowers under the water?

奇肯恩：咕噜咕噜～～～
Qiqirn: *blows bubbles*

阿夫西维：你带来了你的朋友们——？
Avgust: Have you brought your friends?

水面的泡泡们接连不断地出现，越来越多的奇肯恩破开浮冰，漂浮在水面上。
Bubbles swell on the open surface of the water as more Qiqirns break up through the slurry of ice.

它们的长相古怪不一，睁大如油灯般的明黄瞳孔，好奇地打量着人们的一切。
Though their peculiar appearances differ from one to the next, they all possess large, lamp-like eyes that look out and around with curiosity.

阿夫西维：一、二……天啊，你的朋友们也有六条腿呢！
Avgust: One, two ... Oh, your friends also have six legs!

阿夫西维：它们腿上的花纹可真漂亮，像羽茅、锉刀，还有……
Avgust: Look, they are wearing needlegrass and flat files on their legs.

阿夫西维：你们是来参加我们的聚会吗？
Avgust: Are you also here for the ceremony?

孩子为自己增长的智慧而骄傲。
The child takes pride in his imagined duties.

阿夫西维：欢迎你们的到来——奇肯恩和朋友们！
Avgust: Welcome, Qiqirn and friends!

阿夫西维：很高兴你们能来参观这儿最漂亮的小镇，来亚什基。
Avgust: Welcome to the prettiest town in all of the Arctic—Rayashki!

阿夫西维：请欣赏合唱曲目——
Avgust: Please enjoy our song—

他的脸颊通红，响亮的童声回荡在辽阔的海面上，热烈地传了出去。
His cheeks flush as spirited childish voices reverberate in unison out into the sea ahead.

海鸥惊叫着飞起，皱眉的先生快步走上前来。
Seagulls take flight as a distant stern statue springs to life and rushes over.

叶甫根尼：阿夫西维同志，你在做什么？！
Evgeni: Comrade Avgust, what are you doing?!

阿夫西维：嗯？我在欢迎奇肯恩呀～
Avgust: Oh? I'm welcoming the Qiqirn.

孩子高兴地向登上码头的奇肯恩们致意。
The child happily salutes the Qiqirns as they step onto the dock.

叶甫根尼：离开那儿，它们很危险——！
Evgeni: Get out of there. They are dangerous!

叶甫根尼：保卫队，清除这些捣乱的魔精们！
Evgeni: Defense team, drive them away!

维拉：等等——它们是奇肯恩，一种温驯的魔精。它们并无恶意，只是对人类世界感到好奇，孩子们都很喜欢它们……
Vila: Wait! These are Qiqirn. They are not aggressive! They are just curious about us. The kids seem to like them.

对方的动作没有丝毫迟疑，甚至没有回头看一眼。
The defense team moves swiftly and without hesitation.

叶甫根尼：消灭它们。
Evgeni: Get rid of them.

保卫队员Ⅰ：是——！
Guard I: As you command, comrade!

弹孔与火光将平静的水面搅得七零八落，奇肯恩们纷纷窜入水中。
Sprays of bullets and bursts of flame disrupt the water's surface, following the Qiqirns as they dive in, one after another.

它们在响起的钟声里潦草地退场，甚至没能目睹随之盛开的礼花。
Alarms wail in the distance, but the Qiqirns are already long gone.

闻讯而来的孩子们也没能为它们送行。
The children who came to see them are left on the ground, gripping their hats over their ears.

尼娜：奇肯恩们逃跑了，它们一定不喜欢我们的小镇了……
Nina: The Qiqirns are all gone. I think they don't like us anymore.

孩子众：……
Kids: ...

维拉：叶甫根尼同志……
Vila: Comrade Evgeni ...

叶甫根尼：带领孩子们归队，维拉同志，这是你的责任。
Evgeni: Take the kids back to where they were, Comrade Vila. It was your duty to protect them.

毫无情绪的命令被冷漠地掷在了地上。
His orders fizzle out as soon as they are said.

彼得森：只要我们能把小镇建设得更好，就能吸引更多的好朋友。
Pyotr: Maybe if we make the town a better place, more friends will come back.

彼得森：它们也一定会回来！
Pyotr: Then they will also come back!

帕索诺：没错——！
Pasono: That makes sense!

不远处的学者注视着这一切。一阵无人发觉的叹息后，笔记本沙沙作响。
The researcher observes all this from a nearby vantage. Her notebook rustles with a sigh.

北方哨歌：奇肯恩的家族有数十个种类，但无论在哪个区域，任何一个种类的奇肯恩都不曾表现出如此优秀的适水性。也就是说——
Windsong: The family of Qiqirn includes dozens of subspecies, but none of them are so greatly adapted to water as this. That is to say ...

北方哨歌：它们同样是受来亚什基的地脉能量变动影响而产生的特例。
Windsong: They might also be affected by the ley energy under Rayashki.

北方哨歌：只可惜没法获得更详细的研究数据了……
Windsong: Pity that they were driven away. There was much we could have learned from them.

抬头

她抬起头，一团浓郁的云遮住了太阳，几缕散逸的光艰难地穿过了它。
She looks up. A blanket of clouds obscures the sun, with only a few rays of light breaking through.

北方哨歌：嘶——！
Windsong: *gasps*

北方哨歌：这儿的温度上升得也太快了，甚至比我的预期还要快上几天。
Windsong: The temperature here is rising much faster than expected, and much earlier in the season.

北方哨歌：按照历年的官方数据，如此严重的异常升温现象显然是一种超出标准的“无效数据”……
Windsong: I imagine if you asked the weather bureau, they would say this is just an "odd occurrence of unseasonable weather outside of expected ranges."

“砰——”

轰鸣的礼炮声打断了北方哨歌对遥远海岸线的目送与致意。
*boom*

对岸
The booming sound of cannon fire interrupts Windsong's train of thought.

叶甫根尼：约定的时间到了，芝诺的调查员很快就会抵达这里。
Evgeni: It's time. The Zeno investigators should be here any minute.

叶甫根尼：我需要重申，这是一次相当重要的仪式。
Evgeni: I must stress again how important this ceremony could be for our future.

叶甫根尼：小镇的经济情况并不乐观，我想每一个人都能从我们各项物资的配给中有所发觉。
Evgeni: Our town's economy is facing a cliff, and I am sure each one of you has noticed the increased rationing.

叶甫根尼：为了照顾好更多的人们，也为了应付周围愈发频繁的魔精袭击，芝诺的支持必不可少。
Evgeni: If we wish to take care of our people in the future and protect our friends and family from these frequent critter attacks, we need Zeno's support.

叶甫根尼：我们亟需与芝诺建立新的合作关系。
Evgeni: So we will work with Zeno. Because we must!

叶甫根尼：它关乎着来亚什基的命运，也关乎着我们每一位同胞的未来。
Evgeni: The future of Rayashki is in our hands, so is the future of every comrade here.

叶甫根尼：这需要我们每一个人的共同努力。
Evgeni: And we need the cooperation of every man and woman here.

他的目光落在那尾鲜艳的鲁萨尔卡身上。
His stare falls toward the Rusalka's vibrant tail.

许久，视线里的人影终于开口了。
After a pause, his target replies.

维拉：当芝诺的船帆出现在海平面时——
Vila: Zeno's ships are very fast, so, as soon as they appear on the horizon,

维拉：欢迎仪式正式开始。
Vila: our ceremony will begin.

合唱队员们：明白。
Choir Members: Understood.

人们不约而同地站直了身子，凝望着蓝白色相接的一线。
The choir rises in unison, looking out at the pale blue horizon.

遗憾的是，万众瞩目的海平面并没有承载起这份厚重的期待。
The sea responds placidly.

红鲑鱼在海面上跃起又落下，鸥鸟盘旋在空无一船的海岸线上……
Salmon leap out from the water. Seagulls circling along the empty coastline.

而绘制着芝诺图案的旗帜却始终没能升起。
Yet no sign of the anticipated ship appears.

过于安静的大人们显然引起了孩子们的注意。
The quiet expectations of the adults set the children to whisper.

帕索诺：芝诺的先生迟到了。
Pasono: Zeno is late.

彼得森：按照学校里的规定，这种行为属于旷课。
Pyotr: So late that Ms. Vila would say they were absent!

尼娜：他们遇上了什么不好的事情吗……？
Nina: Do you think something bad happened to them?

阿夫西维：他们在做什么呢……？
Avgust: What are they doing there?

值得庆幸的是，更具吸引力的事物很快便落了下来。
No answers come, but a new event catches their attention.

全屏特效-小雪

阿夫西维：咦——！有什么落下来了！
Avgust: Oh! Something is falling!

阿夫西维：轻飘飘，软绵绵……好多好多的熊毛！
Avgust: Light and soft, like a polar bear's hair!

乌云压了过来，遮住了最后一丝阳光。
Dark clouds press down on them, blocking out the final rays of sunlight.

全屏变暗，像是天气昏沉

阿夫西维：……可怜的北极熊，它的身上一定光秃秃的。
Avgust: Poor bear, losing all his hair.

全屏特效-雪越下越大，形成猛烈的暴雪

漫天的雪花纷纷扬扬地洒落。
Snowflakes flutter down across the gray sky.

它们相互拥抱、汇合，飘落在这座不大的镇子上。
Converging in the blustering wind, they fall towards the town.

尼娜：……嗯？
Nina: Mmm?

帕索诺：下雪了——！
Pasono: It's snow!

彼得森：怎么可能？！……原来来亚什基的夏天，也会下雪吗？
Pyotr: What?! How can there be snow in summer?

帕索诺：咦～这就是阿夫西维说的奇怪的东西吗？
Pasono: Mm? Is this related to the strange thing Avgust said earlier?

尼娜：幸好它们不是石头，也不是湿漉漉的口水。
Nina: If so, I'm happy that these aren't stones or a dark cloud's spit.

孩子们靠向阿夫西维，围在这位坚定的先行者身旁。
The children huddle near Avgust, astonished by the accuracy of his predictions.

帕索诺：阿夫西维同学，真不可思议，我可没见过你有这么聪明的时候呀～
Pasono: Avgust, I can't believe it! You were never right before!

尼娜：唔，好冷……这些小雪花可真刺人！
Nina: *shivers* Oh, oh, it's chilly. The snow is biting against my skin.

彼得森：我向你道歉，阿夫西维同学——你没有骗人。
Pyotr: I'm sorry, Avgust. I shouldn't call you a liar.

他扭扭捏捏地低下了头。
He lowers his head hesitantly.

彼得森：可是，来亚什基会变得更糟吗……？
Pyotr: But will Rayashki really get into trouble?

一双稚嫩的手拍了拍彼得森的肩膀。
A gentle hand nudges Pyotr, a motion learned from someone older and wiser.

阿夫西维：彼得森，我们不会被乌云打败，也不会输给北极熊。
Avgust: Pyotr, we will not be defeated, not by clouds, or bears.

阿夫西维：你看——！
Avgust: Look!

阿夫西维：慢吞吞的乌龟先生还没有来。
Avgust: Mr. Tortoise is walking very slowly.

阿夫西维：但是大家都认真地站在自己的位置上。
Avgust: But no one has left their position.

阿夫西维：大家都喜欢来亚什基。
Avgust: For Rayashki.

阿夫西维：天鹅们也要回到湖里，快点儿，再快点——！
Avgust: You little swans must go back to your lake too! Go as fast as you can!

尼娜：……嗯！
Nina: We will!

彼得森：别忘了你自己……阿夫西维同学！
Pyotr: Don't forget your own job, Avgust!

孩子们回到了各自的位置，正如最开始的那般。
The children return to their positions and ready themselves.

北方哨歌：好吧……看来这条乳白色的痕迹属于这场暴雪。
Windsong: So, this milky white line is this snowstorm.

北方哨歌：毫无疑问，来亚什基的平均气温甚至已经越过了近五年的夏季最高点，它们与同样反常的丰富水汽一同协作，造成了这场越下越大的暴雪……
Windsong: The average temperature in Rayashki has reached its highest point in the last five years, which, together with the abnormally rich air moisture, has produced an unseasonal and odd kind of snow.

北方哨歌：官方的数据被推翻了，理线学是对的！
Windsong: The weather forecast was wrong; ley lines were right!

北方哨歌相当振奋。
Windsong can't hide her excitement.

她倚靠在更远一些的围墙边，运笔如飞，翻过了一页又一页的笔记。
She leans up on a wall some distance from the event, her pen flying across page after page of notes.

许久，她终于回过神来。
Until she is compelled to snap back to reality.

北方哨歌：嗯……？
Windsong: Mm?

留在原地的显然不止她一人。
The assembly before her has barely moved.

暴雪无声地落下，淹没越来越多的地方。
The snow claims more territory by the minute.

海面，栏杆，以及一双双或大或小的长靴。
Over sea and land, piling up on the railings, and rising over boots, large and small.

北方哨歌：——！
Windsong: ...!

换图

遥远的汽笛声裹着芝诺的旗帜终于姗姗来迟。
A distant foghorn accompanies the sight of a flag piercing up into the horizon. Zeno arrives at last.

叶甫根尼：全体人员，准备！
Evgeni: Everyone, listen!

叶甫根尼：欢迎仪式正式开始。
Evgeni: Our ceremony will begin.

镇民众：是——！
Residents: As you command, comrade!

叶甫根尼：……奏乐！
Evgeni: Music, please!

镇民众：“时光呀它缓缓地飘远——”
Residents: "Let go of yesterday, let it fade away."

镇民众：“朋友呀别为那不停留的怀念——”
Residents: "Each step paints a brand-new day."

镇民众：“失去的昨日令我们遗憾——”
Residents: "Don't look behind, no shadows will be seen in the daylight."

镇民众：“但更美好的仍旧在前方——”
Residents: "Under brighter skies, we leave on our journey."

汽船缓缓停靠在这个简陋的港口，再也没有任何动静。
The steamship pulls into their rudimentary harbor, but no further movement follows.

而终于打开的舷窗边，没有问候，没有声响。
A porthole opens, but no voice comes out, no sound whatsoever beyond the lapping waves.

只有一封古怪的信件，轻飘飘地落在了所有人的面前。
A letter flutters out toward the anxious crowd.

？？？：很高兴与你们会面，来亚什基的朋友们。
???: It's a pleasure to speak to you all, our valued friends in Rayashki.

？？？：我在此谨代表芝诺军备学院，发表对于“芝诺与来亚什基合作条例”的初步通知。
???: On behalf of Zeno Arms Academy, I am here to announce the details of the "Zeno-Rayashki Cooperation Agreement."

？？？：如你们所期待的那样，我们带来了一整支精锐的武装小队，我相信，他们一定能为各位解决眼前的魔精麻烦。
???: As many of you have expected, a squad of armed troops will soon be sent to aid you with the critter problem.

？？？：但同样，我们很遗憾地宣布——经过反复且慎重的考量，芝诺初步决定，暂时中止对来亚什基的一切支持政策，并建议各位尽早开展在来亚什基的撤离工作。
???: However, having given it careful consideration, we have decided that the town of Rayashki is no longer viable for our continued support and must be abandoned. We advise that all residents prepare to be transferred to a new post, immediately.

？？？：希望各位能予以配合。
???: Thank you for your cooperation.

维拉：什么——？！
Vila: What?!

FR-06 好日子，坏日子 / Good Days, Bad Days

会议室

贝托尔特：我不理解你们坚持的理由。
Bertolt: I don't see the point of your reluctance.

皱着眉头的先生理了理信上的龟形纹样，将那页轻飘飘的纸张塞进了信封的嘴里。
The frowning master of ceremonies straightens the tortoise-patterned letter and then shoves it back into its envelope.

贝托尔特：关于芝诺的决定，信上已经写得很清楚了。
Bertolt: The letter conveyed Zeno's decision clearly.

贝托尔特：我建议，我们应该找个暖和的酒馆，喝上最后几杯……如果你们这儿有斯托利的话。
Bertolt: I suggest we warm ourselves up with a few drinks before we go. Do you have any Stolich in town?

贝托尔特：而不是坐在这个冷冰冰的地方，讨论着一些早有答案的问题。
Bertolt: Better than sitting here dwelling on the things that cannot be changed.

贝托尔特：……这儿没准备点可可豆之类的吗？
Bertolt: Please tell me you have something like cocoa here.

他旁若无人地伸了个懒腰，陷进了沙发里。
Their long-awaited guest stretches lazily, as if no one is around, and sinks into the couch.

空气近乎凝固，底下的暗流几乎要翻涌上来。
The tension in the air hangs like fumes waiting to ignite.

维拉：贝托尔特先生，这和说好的不一样。
Vila: This is not what we agreed on earlier, Mr. Bertolt.

叶甫根尼：冷静点，维拉。
Evgeni: Calm yourself, Vila.

贝托尔特：你似乎误会了什么，这位冷冰冰的女士。
Bertolt: You must be mistaken, my very passionate friend.

贝托尔特：芝诺早在数个月前便寄出了通知：“来亚什基的现有价值已不足以支撑芝诺的后续支持……”
Bertolt: Zeno sent a warning months ago. "The estimated value Rayashki can add to Zeno's program is less than satisfactory. Further support is no longer recommended."

贝托尔特：“若该区域发现了尚未报告的、更具价值的资源，请相关负责人尽早回复，并提请芝诺调查员的进一步评估。”
Bertolt: "Should any new valuable resources be found in the region, please reply to this letter as soon as possible for further assessment."

维拉：——！
Vila: ...!

贝托尔特：之后，我们收到了来亚什基方面的回信。
Bertolt: Then we heard back from Rayashki.

贝托尔特：发件人是——叶甫根尼。
Bertolt: In fact, the sender was you, Evgeni.

叶甫根尼：……是的。
Evgeni: Yes, it was.

贝托尔特：不得不承认，你的观点相当有趣，甚至引起了上头的注意……所以，我才被派到了这儿。
Bertolt: And it was you yourself that argued the most compelling point, I have to say. One that has drawn the higher-ups' attention, and the reason why I was sent here.

贝托尔特：“我认为，来亚什基的人们拥有着卓越的品质。他们团结、敬业、充满干劲，是一批相当优秀的可用之材。”
Bertolt: I believe you wrote: "I have total faith in the quality of the people of Rayashki. Their solidarity, dedication, and motivation have proven invaluable to us."

贝托尔特：“哪怕在芝诺的其他地方，我也始终确信，他们能够发挥出重要的作用。”
Bertolt: "I am certain they would carry those same strengths of character and skill to any post, no matter where they were assigned."

他折起信纸，递给一脸茫然的维拉。
He folds the letter and hands it to Vila, her face blank as a canvas.

叶甫根尼：芝诺受理了我的申请。
Evgeni: Zeno accepted my application.

叶甫根尼：当然，我私下询问了不少人，他们都对芝诺评价颇高。
Evgeni: Of course, I asked around before making my submission, and Zeno seemed to have a good reputation.

叶甫根尼：……加入芝诺是一个难得的机会。
Evgeni: It was a golden opportunity to join them.

贝托尔特：别误会，我们的考核可一点儿也不轻松，你们机会难得。
Bertolt: It is, but do not get us wrong. Our entrance requirements can be most difficult to meet.

贝托尔特：芝诺只需要无数优秀人才中的最优秀的那一丁点儿～
Bertolt: Zeno only takes in the best of the best.

维拉：让一部分人……搬去芝诺？！
Vila: You want some of us to work for Zeno?!

维拉：你从没有跟我们提过这些……叶甫根尼！
Vila: You never told us anything like that, Evgeni!

叶甫根尼：但从更理性的角度而言，我们应该让一部分人把握住这个投身芝诺的机会。
Evgeni: Be reasonable, Vila. Some of us deserve this opportunity.

维拉：那其他人呢？！——我们的老人、孩子、那些为了挖掘矿石而负伤甚至死亡的同胞……
Vila: What about the others?! We have elders and children. Some of our comrades have been injured and even died in the mine; are we to forget their sacrifices?

她尽力扼制自己的愤怒，脖颈上的细鳃剧烈地起伏。
She tries to suppress the gills on her neck as they heave violently.

贝托尔特：放心，我的朋友。这正是我们派出最为精锐的生物问题处理小队的原因。
Bertolt: Relax, my friend. That's why we sent our very best biological control squad.

贝托尔特：我们会协助你们撤离到最近的安全避难区。
Bertolt: We will escort you to the nearest shelter.

打击一浪接一浪，似乎永无尽头。
Another wave upon relentless waves of shock.

叶甫根尼：维拉，你得正视现实。我知道大家都为这儿付出了全部的努力，也理解你的目标——
Evgeni: Face reality, Vila. I know how much effort we have put into building this town, and I understand you have this dream to fulfill.

叶甫根尼：可我们必须面对它，做好放弃来亚什基的最坏打算。
Evgeni: But we must prepare for the worst: we may have to give up on our Rayashki.

他拿出了一份满是划痕与批注的文件，递给了对方。
He takes out a document covered in scratched notes and annotations and hands it to her.

叶甫根尼：看看这个吧……
Evgeni: Read this.

维拉：“经实地探测确认，来亚什基目前可供开采的卢恩矿约为0.00173万吨，已不足往年年均产量的0.275%。”
Vila: "Field investigation has confirmed that the remaining runium reserves in Rayashki are around 0.0173 kilotons, which is less than 0.275% of our average annual output."

维拉：“此外，该区域由于地处北极，矿石运输成本极高，且不适合作为卢恩矿石加工厂的选址。”
Vila: "The mine is located high within the Arctic Circle, which has entailed significant transportation costs. The harsh environment is also wholly unsuitable for building any permanent processing facilities."

维拉：“同时，考虑到当地愈发频繁的野兽与魔精的袭击事件，需配备的武装保护支出已累增至原成本的3.61倍，且呈现出递增趋势。”
Vila: "In addition, military spending on the region has recently been elevated 3.61 times due to increasing animal and critter attacks, and that number is still rising."

维拉：“显然，该区域已不具备负担区域自理的能力。”
Vila: "Clearly, the region is now incapable of self-management."

维拉：“据芝诺军备学院下辖减灾署《世界人道主义援助指南》规定，初步决议如下——”
Vila: "According to the Guide on Global Humanitarian Aid by the Office for Disaster Risk Reduction of Zeno Arms Academy, we propose to ..."

维拉：“安排负责人员前往该地区，协助当地住民的有序撤离；同时，在撤离完成后，接管该区域后续的一切危机清理事务。”
Vila: "... send a special squad to the region to evacuate all local citizens and subsequently take care of the remaining biological control issues."

收起浮窗

贝托尔特：此外，芝诺可适当放宽对于该地区的人员遴选标准，以补充芝诺各分部的人员。
Bertolt: And our admission standards will be lowered—at Zeno's discretion—so that you will all find work with us somewhere.

芝诺的代表人适时地补充了尚未写明的内容。
Zeno's representative offers a timely, if unconvincing, supplement to the letter.

纸张在维拉的手上生出一道道褶皱，最后被揉成一团凌乱的纸球。
The paper creases and crumples into a ball in her hands.

叶甫根尼：很遗憾，这就是现实。
Evgeni: I'm sorry, but this is reality.

叶甫根尼：对于芝诺而言……他们扶持来亚什基的初衷正是为了这些价值高昂的小石头。
Evgeni: From the start, this ore was the only thing they wanted from us.

叶甫根尼：我们克服了恶劣的开采环境，将它们一箱箱地装入矿船，运往芝诺的各个分部。
Evgeni: The environment here has always been harsh for mining, but we overcame it and sent our shipments to wherever Zeno had need of them.

贝托尔特：向你们每一个人致敬，我亲爱的朋友们。
Bertolt: And I salute each one of you for your work, my friends.

叶甫根尼：现在，这一使命完成了。
Evgeni: But now, our mission is over.

毫无疑问，卢恩矿石是小镇的命脉。而失去它之后，来亚什基羸弱得像个孩子。
There is no doubt in anyone's mind: runium has been the town's lifeblood and the key to its survival.

叶甫根尼：我坚信，这儿的所有人会在其他地方继续劳动，继续建设，哪怕……
Evgeni: I believe all of you will continue to work hard in your new positions. No matter what ...

维拉：……叶甫根尼，你对待来亚什基的未来太轻率了。
Vila: You shouldn't rush to a decision. We're discussing Rayashki's future here, Evgeni.

维拉：这个地方凝聚了数代人六十余年的血汗，离开并非是你我的一句话。
Vila: For six decades, the people here have put in great efforts to turn the town into what it is today. We won't leave just because you tell us so.

维拉：最早的时候，祖辈们甚至没有一台正常运行的起重机。他们用无数双手掘起了一块块巨石。
Vila: Our grandparents didn't even have construction equipment at the beginning. They built these houses with their own hands.

维拉：汽船们运来了种植蔬菜的土壤，我们砌起了抵挡风雪的围墙。
Vila: We shipped over the planting soil. We built walls to keep out the wind and snow.

闭塞的会议室里，空气又湿润了几分。
Within the meeting room's cloistered walls, the air is heavy with moisture once more.

叶甫根尼：后来你来到了这儿。你为孩子们带来了许多新课本，也让大家认识了在人类之外，还存在着许多特别的种族……你融入得很快。
Evgeni: When you came here, you brought books for the children and introduced us to a species different than humans. You became one of us.

叶甫根尼：我很抱歉，维拉同志。
Evgeni: I am not happy about this either, Comrade Vila.

维拉：我不接受你的同情，叶甫根尼同志。这不只是我个人的理想，而是这儿所有人的。
Vila: I won't buy that, Comrade Evgeni. This is not just about my dream, but everyone's dream.

维拉：难道你忘了来亚什基建立的初衷吗？
Vila: Or have you forgotten what Rayashki was meant to be?

叶甫根尼：一个为所有人而建，也欢迎所有人一同建设的理想城市，它会发展，壮大，直到遍布世界的每一寸土地。
Evgeni: A utopia built for and by everyone. The voice of a better future, one which would sound across the land and seas.

叶甫根尼：我一点儿也没忘。
Evgeni: I remember every word of it.

叶甫根尼的语气低沉，但仍旧斩钉截铁。
Evgeni's voice is low but still decisive.

贝托尔特：我很同情你们，朋友。
Bertolt: You have my sympathy, friends.

贝托尔特：因为某些原因，芝诺在世界各地都遭受了巨大的损失。
Bertolt: Zeno has also suffered huge losses in many regions.

贝托尔特：不只是来亚什基，我们也损失了许多人手，失去了许多战略要地、军工厂，甚至是下辖的军事学院。
Bertolt: We have lost manpower, territory, armament factories, and even some of our affiliated military schools. Rayashki is but one of these losses.

贝托尔特：我们对你们的现状感同身受。
Bertolt: We know how you feel right now.

他耸了耸肩，无奈挂满了整张脸。
He shrugs his shoulders, his face a picture of unhelpfulness.

贝托尔特：但这显然不只是芝诺的问题。
Bertolt: But Zeno has its own problems to be faced.

贝托尔特：新工业，让人眼花缭乱的电器，五花八门的新花样——到处都需要资金。哪怕是芝诺，我们也得在某些地方勒紧裤腰带了。
Bertolt: And investing in these new industries, purchasing fancy equipment, all these things Rayashki will need ... All of this takes money. And even Zeno must be economical.

维拉：那你们口口声声标榜的世界福祉呢？
Vila: Shouldn't the people in Rayashki also benefit from these global benefits Zeno has promised?

贝托尔特：当然是放缓了，我的朋友。相信我，芝诺已经为你们竭尽了全力。
Bertolt: We will get there, my friend. Maybe slowly, but we will get there. Trust me, Zeno has done everything they can for you.

贝托尔特：哪怕在这个动荡的时代，我们仍然有所坚持，并且不懈地抓牢我们向往的重要之物，对吧？
Bertolt: We need to keep our eyes on our goals and stay on the right course, so that we won't get lost in these turbulent times, yes?

维拉：……
Vila: ...

他略微靠近了维拉，压低了声音。
He leans toward Vila, providing an unnecessary whisper.

贝托尔特：我明白你在这座小镇的分量，也相信你能安抚好余下的其他人。
Bertolt: I know how much faith these people have in you, and I believe you can show them a different perspective about these coming changes.

贝托尔特：当然，这也会为你的考核加上不少分……
Bertolt: Of course, this will also help you during Zeno's assessment.

维拉：…………
Vila: ...

贝托尔特：祝你们好运，朋友。
Bertolt: Good luck, my friend.

FR-07 纸奖章 / A Paper Medal

旅馆房间

北方哨歌：匮乏的卢恩矿石，新的魔精亚种，骤降的暴雪……
Windsong: The reserves of runium running dry, the appearance of new critters, the sudden snowstorm.

北方哨歌：多亏了它们自证身份，这张地脉能量图越来越完整了！
Windsong: I've connected the ley lines of each of these phenomena. The map is nearly complete!

她展开了那张种种线条与光点堆叠在一起的繁复图纸。
She unfolds the complex blueprint filled with various lines and marks.

北方哨歌：可是……这里还有不少没有得到验证的线条与痕迹。
Windsong: But still haven't traced many lines and marks back to their source.

北方哨歌：光靠我自己，想再偷摸着溜进那些工厂、禁区之类的地方一点儿也不现实。
Windsong: Perhaps if I go back to the factories, into the restricted zones ... But, I can't do that alone.

北方哨歌：更何况，这座小镇还遭遇了更大的麻烦……
Windsong: Definitely not when the situation in town is so unstable.

北方哨歌趴倒在桌面，层层叠叠的典籍与稿纸堆把她埋在了最底下。
Windsong collapses onto the table. An avalanche follows, covering her in layers of books and manuscripts.

纷繁的故纸堆像是连绵的高山，遮蔽了所有的光线。
The piles around her loom like a mountain range, casting her in shadow.

北方哨歌：好吧，也许我早该放弃了……理线学根本没机会回到大众视野之中去。
Windsong: Well, I should have given this up long ago. There's no chance that the study of ley lines will ever be accepted again.

过往的讥讽与鄙夷悄无声息地追上了她。
Phantom voices of past mockery and scorn rise up to her ears.

回忆滤镜

“评述者”：我很抱歉，北方哨歌女士。光凭这些不知多少年以前的老旧资料和报告，我们显然不能通过理线学的复课申请。
"Reviewer": Regretfully, Ms. Windsong, with nothing but these outdated files and materials to back you up, there's simply no way to justify reinstating the study of ley lines into our curriculum.

“评述者”：我们的研究经费是有限的，理应拨调到能稳定产出名誉与成果的学科上……至于理线学嘛，呵呵……
"Reviewer": We don't have unlimited funds, and we must save our money for projects with greater potential. The study of ley lines is ...

“评述者”：当然，我们同样鼓励新兴学科的发展，但仅仅依靠你自己是不够的……
"Reviewer": Of course, we might be able to consider new ideas and projects. You can't be allowed to do this on your own.

“评述者”：你得拿出一块有诚意的敲门砖，地理研究学会、神秘动物协会，或是更有分量的背书。
"Reviewer": You will need endorsements from the Institution of Geographic Studies, the Arcane Creature Society, or other such organizations.

“评述者”：噢，让我想想，芝诺似乎最近对地理学者的兴致颇高，他们招徕了一大批编外研究员，我想，你大可以去那儿碰碰运气。
"Reviewer": Let me think. Zeno seems to be interested in geographers recently. They've just recruited a number of researchers for a new commission. Maybe you should go try your luck with them.

收起滤镜

窗外传来了叮叮咚咚的声音，像是儿歌的和声。
An echo of a nursery rhyme rings out from beyond her self-made mountain range.

但她沉浸在沉重的郁愤中，丝毫没有发觉。
But she is all but oblivious to it.

拉近

北方哨歌：芝诺指派的期限越来越近了……可光凭现在的成果，显然没法搞到芝诺的推荐信。
Windsong: The submission date is getting closer each day, but I've made poor progress. Zeno won't endorse me if I can't find a breakthrough.

北方哨歌：他们的动作越来越激进了，先是派来了一大堆杂七杂八的编外调查人员，甚至现在还派出了军队……
Windsong: They have become more and more radical and desperate lately. First, they sent those researchers here to conduct their haphazard studies, and now, an armed force.

北方哨歌：——就为了一个不知什么年代编造出的“永动能源”传闻？
Windsong: And all this effort just to chase the rumor of some source of "perpetual energy"?

北方哨歌：“永动的能源显然存在于永冻的土壤中！”
Windsong: "That this perpetual energy source must be hidden somewhere beneath the permafrost!"

北方哨歌：大人物们动动手指，从指甲缝里抠出点甜头，可怜的小狗学者就得屁颠屁颠地窜来窜去！
Windsong: The higher-ups call the shots. All they need to do is spread a little honey in the right places. Then all the little researchers will swarm on it like flies.

北方哨歌：可世界上真有这样神奇的能源吗？
Windsong: But could there really be a magical power source like that?

北方哨歌：无论如何，独自完成地脉能量图的绘制只是个遥不可及的梦……
Windsong: Whether there is or not, I still have a map to finish. There's no way that I can map every ley line in the region all by myself.

北方哨歌：…………
Windsong: ...

北方哨歌：永别了，我从未享受过的研究补助、万众期待的学术访谈，还有遥不可及的“地理视野”论坛。
Windsong: Goodbye research funds, goodbye lectures and seminars, and so long to my dreams of being chair of the "Geographical Perspectives" forum.

她推开了几本挡在面前的书，光线和一些细微的声响渗了进来。
She jostles the heaps of books, moving them just enough to let in some light and sound.

像是缀入黑夜的点点繁星。
They seep in through the cracks like starlight.

窗

？？？：当当——！
???: Took-took!

北方哨歌：……！
Windsong: ...!

返回

房门被迅速地关上了，北方哨歌紧张地靠在门上。
The door snaps shut. Windsong stands against it nervously.

桌上的仪器滚落一地，在窗台，在桌角，在床底。它们相互碰撞，一同奏起慌乱的乐章。
Instruments roll off the table, colliding with each other on the windowsill, the corners, and under the bed, falling in a cacophonous disarray.

北方哨歌：我眼花了吗……？
Windsong: What was that?

房门再一次被轻轻推了开来，一束向日葵从门缝里探出头来。
The door is gently pushed open again, revealing the curious face of a sunflower peeking in through the crack.

阿夫西维：北方哨歌，我们在等你～
Avgust: Ms. Windsong, we've been waiting for you!

这是一枚略显简陋的奖章，缺少精美的设计理念，也没有厚重的金属质感。
As far as medals go, the design is a little cruder than expected, and damp paper doesn't quite have the same gravitas as gold or silver.

北方哨歌曾为理线学幻想过无数次与之相似的画面。
Still, Windsong has fantasized countless times about receiving such an accolade for her work, even a paper one.

北方哨歌：……！
Windsong: ...!

尼娜：北方哨歌老师，我们为您和阿夫西维同学准备了授勋典礼！
Nina: Ms. Windsong, we prepared a special medal ceremony for you and Avgust!

帕索诺：我们欢迎您来参加仪式——！
Pasono: Please come to our ceremony!

彼得森：……
Pyotr: ...

彼得森：谢谢您教给我们知识……
Pyotr: We just wanted to thank you for teaching us.

彼得森：维拉老师说得对，我们不能随意地否定他人。
Pyotr: Ms. Vila was right. We shouldn't have been so quick to argue. We should have listened!

尼娜：你们应该受到表扬！
Nina: So you should be given an award for being right!

尼娜：不过，它要比电视上的简单多了……
Nina: But our ceremony will not be as big as the ones on TV.

是的，这是独属于孩子们的颁奖仪式。
Indeed, this is a very special and exclusive reward.

无比简陋，同时具备孩子气的童真和滑稽。
Simple as it is, it comes with something nothing else could: the innocence and laughter of children.

彼得森：北方哨歌老师，您愿意接受这枚勋章吗？
Pyotr: Ms. Windsong, will you accept this medal?

这是许久以来的时间里，理线学第一次受到了如此广泛的认可。
For the first time in a long while, the study of ley lines basks in the glow of scholarly acclaim.

纸质勋章被微微发颤的手包裹了起来。
The paper medal is cupped in her trembling hands.

儿童广场

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

北方哨歌：哪怕我现在没有能装进这枚勋章的杯子，也没法一口饮尽你们的鼓励。
Windsong: I have no cup to put this medal in, so we can't toast with it in celebration.

某种浓烈而激烈的气味冲撞着她的鼻腔。
She sniffles.

北方哨歌：但至少，这趟短暂的旅程不算一无所获……谢谢你们，小家伙。
Windsong: But now I know, no matter what, I won't be returning empty-handed. Thank you, kids.

尼娜：您要离开我们了吗……？
Nina: Do you mean, are you leaving us?

帕索诺：可我们还什么都没学会呢！
Pasono: But there is so much you still need to teach us!

彼得森：“来亚什基永远欢迎每一个人”，当然也包括您——难道您不喜欢我们的小镇吗？
Pyotr: "Rayashki embraces every guest," including you, Ms. Windsong—don't you like it here?

孩子们泫然欲泣，现在轮到另一个人慌乱了。
The children are on the verge of tears. She is pulled in helplessly, too.

北方哨歌：可在欢迎仪式上，我听说了那些不好的传闻……
Windsong: But those things I heard at the welcome ceremony ... Won't we all be leaving soon?

阿夫西维：大嘴信是小气鬼，不是好朋友！
Avgust: No! I don't believe it. That stranger was mean; he wasn't our friend!

彼得森：哼——这是我们的小镇，他们说了可不算。
Pyotr: Hmph. This is our town; they can't speak for us.

尼娜：没错！
Nina: That's right!

没有怀疑，没有难过，只有无数双坚定的眼睛。
Neither doubt nor sorrow will dim their eyes—before her lies only a sea of steadfast faces.

童稚的话语积极而炽热。
Their words encouraging and powerful despite their youth.

消解了她的愕然，又似乎悄悄种下了什么。
They plant some strange seed of hope within her.

彼得森：维拉老师“邀请”了那位来自芝诺的先生下船，他们一起去了叶甫根尼先生的会议室。
Pyotr: Ms. Vila "invited" the man from Zeno to leave his ship. Then they went into Mr. Evgeni's meeting room together.

尼娜：是的……克努特叔叔向我们保证过，没有人会放弃这儿。
Nina: Uncle Knut promised me that no one will give up this place.

尼娜：他们会继续和芝诺开会，得、得出“一个让大家都满意的方案”——
Nina: They will go to many meetings and find "a solution that satisfies both sides."

阿夫西维：乌龟们爬得很慢，他们需要瞪大眼睛，仔细观察！
Avgust: The tortoises move slowly. They need to keep their eyes opened and look for a better answer!

尼娜：……您还能继续为我们上课吗？
Nina: So will you stay and teach us?

彼得森：我再也不捣乱了，我保证！
Pyotr: I won't cause you any more trouble, I promise!

孩子们哄堂大笑。
The children burst into laughter.

甚至盖过了窗台传来的窸窣异响。
Their voices very nearly drown out the rustling noises coming from the windowsill.

阿夫西维：咦？尺子同志在说话——！
Avgust: Mm? Comrade Calculator is speaking!

孩子好奇地窜进了半掩着门的客房。
Curiosity propels the child through the half-open door of the guest room.

旅馆房间
窗边
尺子出现
漂浮在高空中的理线尺，旁边有许多无规律运动的线条

阿夫西维：你好～
Avgust: Hello!

“改线尺”：……
"Ley Calibrator": ...

阿夫西维：尺子同志，你在指挥蚯蚓们的方向吗？
Avgust: Comrade Calculator, are you giving the earthworms directions?

窗边的异响更加嘈杂，同时伴随着玻璃的震动。
The clamor by the window crescendos.

上

孩子踮起脚尖，堪堪够着了正散发着微光的改线尺。
Even on tiptoes, the child barely reaches the faintly glowing calibrator.

遗憾的是，有此意图的显然不止他一个人。
Unfortunately, he is not the only one reaching for it.

？？？：吼吼——！
???: *roars*

基基图克的爪子挥舞特效

更不幸的是，生满鳞片的爪子要比稚嫩的手指健硕得多。
More unfortunate still, scaly claws prove mightier than little fingers.

“改线尺”：咔嚓——
"Ley Calibrator": *cracks*

终于，其他孩子也发现了这儿的纷争，他们拥着北方哨歌一同挤进了这座愈发逼仄的屋子。
The other children notice the tug-of-war and crowd around Windsong, squeezing into the increasingly cramped room.

北方哨歌：你们在做什么？——噢，我的改线尺！
Windsong: What's going on here? Ah, my calibrator!

？？？：嚼嚼！吼%@#@——！
???: *chews*

北方哨歌：鲸鱼骨骼，菱形利齿，双足短粗，双目萎缩，极其尖锐的鼻端……是基基图克[Kikituk]！
Windsong: The whale-like backbone, the diamond-shaped teeth, two short legs, with dim eyes, and an extremely sharp nose. That must be a Kikituk!

基基图克：嘶——！
Kikituk: *gasps*

北方哨歌：根据资料记载，它们最近的聚居地应该在离这几百公里的卡尔王地群岛……
Windsong: But their closest habitat should be Kong Karls Land, hundreds of kilometers away.

红棕色的鼻尖直勾勾地对着北方哨歌手上的新食物。
Its snout fixates on the new treat in Windsong's grasp.

她掏出嘎吱作响的扫描仪，赤色的线条疯涌了上来。
She pulls out the scanner, its gears whining as ley lines flood forth.

北方哨歌：红棕色的痕迹，它的体内富集了相当丰裕的地脉能量。很显然，这个家伙处于食物链的上位圈……
Windsong: Their marks on the map appear to be red, sort of reddish brown, and there's a large amount of ley energy accumulated around them. Clearly, they're high on the food chain.

北方哨歌：看来这儿的“小鱼”勾来的可不止一条大鱼。
Windsong: Seems like the "small fish" have attracted more than one "big fish."

她一脚把龇牙咧嘴的魔精踹了下去，抵住了窗台。
With a swift kick, she sends the grinning critter tumbling.

北方哨歌：小脑袋瓜们，躲到我身后——！
Windsong: Kids, get behind me!

基基图克们显然并不打算就此作罢，它们围着狭小的窗台打转，试图再次扑跃而上。
The undeterred Kikituks close in on the narrow ledge.

基基图克：嘶嘶——！
Kikituk: *hissing*

阿夫西维：哇啊！基基图克们在表演节目！
