Avgust: Oh, oh! The Kikituks are giving a performance!

阿夫西维：鼻子歌唱，羽毛跳蹦蹦舞，肚皮跳摇摆舞……
Avgust: Their nose sings, their fur dances, and their belly shakes.

阿夫西维：咦……？
Avgust: Mm?

阿夫西维：它的耳朵为什么不表演节目呢？
Avgust: But why aren't their ears doing anything?

北方哨歌：阿夫西维，你在念叨些什么呢！——躲远点，它们可比奇肯恩凶猛一百倍！
Windsong: Avgust! What are you doing there? Stay back; those are not Qiqirn!

阿夫西维：可是，可是……
Avgust: But, but ...

他们都有着各自的、对方无法理解的焦急。
The meaning of both their messages is lost in the confusion.

阿夫西维：可是它们的耳朵一点儿也不听话，没有加入朋友们的舞蹈……
Avgust: But, but their ears are left behind. They-they can't join the dance.

阿夫西维：这样是没法得到表扬的——！
Avgust: Then they will not get their Alenka!

北方哨歌：耳朵……？
Windsong: Ears?

北方哨歌像是醒悟了什么，她死死盯着基基图克的脑袋。
Windsong, struck by her sudden revelation, fixes on the Kikituk's head.

它们藏在厚实的绒毛里，偶然露出的耳根显露出远甚其他部位的红棕色。
Beneath its tufts of plush fur lie well-hidden ears of a deeper color.

北方哨歌：Природа это числа и черты.
Windsong: Природа это числа и черты.

神秘学咒语攻击特效（线条形状）
After a brief incantation, lines converge in a beam that hits precisely on its ear.

短促的咒语后，一束线条迅速而准确地击中了耳根。

基基图克：呜……
Kikituk: *wails*

可怜虫吃痛地叫了起来。
The creature's cry pierces the air.

北方哨歌：看来这确实是它们的弱点……
Windsong: So that seems to be their weak spot.

北方哨歌：小家伙，干得不错。你的感知力比我想象得还要敏锐！
Windsong: Good job, little one. You're even more perceptive than I thought!

北方哨歌收起眼底的惊讶，拍了拍阿夫西维的脑袋。
Windsong pats Avgust's head.

北方哨歌：接下来嘛——
Windsong: Next ...

她露出一个危险而邪恶的微笑。
She reveals a dark and dangerous smile.

一道道白光接连不断地蹦跃着，像是盛放的烟花。

北方哨歌：哼哼～
Windsong: Hmph.

基基图克们终于放下了本就不属于它们的战利品，而后跃下窗台，转瞬便消失得无影无踪。
The Kikituks finally relinquish their ill-gotten gains, leaping down and away from the windowsill.

徒留一地浸润在口涎之中的改线尺碎片。
Leaving behind gnawed wet fragments of the ley calibrator.

北方哨歌：&%#！*【德涅斯特河东岸粗口】……这可是我为数不多的资产了。
Windsong: S**t! This was one of the last working instruments I had.

一束向日葵轻轻地拍了拍北方哨歌的肩膀。
A sunflower gently pats against Windsong's shoulder.

阿夫西维：别难过，北方哨歌。
Avgust: Don't be sad, Ms. Windsong.

阿夫西维：我们可以把它们种在土壤里。明年，它们就会长出许多朋友。
Avgust: If we plant them in the soil, many more will come out when spring comes.

北方哨歌：……谢谢你的安慰，阿夫西维。
Windsong: Heh. Thank you, Avgust.

彼得森：北方哨歌老师，我也能成为一名理线师吗？
Pyotr: Ms. Windsong, can I be a ley hunter too?

尼娜：如果我们也像您一样厉害，就能保护好您的尺子了……
Nina: If we were as good as you are, maybe we could've protected your machine.

彼得森：也一定能保护好我们的小镇。
Pyotr: And maybe we could protect our town.

北方哨歌转过头来，对上了无数双充满活力的眼睛。
Windsong turns her head, meeting many pairs of expectant eyes.

北方哨歌：小脑袋瓜们，理线师可不是什么值得骄傲的职业。
Windsong: Kids, ley hunting isn't a good profession.

北方哨歌：走上这条路，你们就得应付无数的质疑、鄙弃，还有堆成山的作业。
Windsong: If you become a ley hunter, you will have to deal with doubt from all your peers, even hatred, and homework that piles up to your roof.

尼娜：您说得不对，北方哨歌老师——来亚什基的大家都很团结。
Nina: Ms. Windsong, people in Rayashki are taught not to doubt or hate others. They would never hate you, or us!

彼得森：没错！
Pyotr: Exactly!

面前的孩子们熟悉而陌生。
The children of Rayashki are in some ways so strange to her.

某些无言的、由来已久的退缩悄然消失了。
Their courage and solidarity overcome her long-standing hesitation.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

一种更强烈的好奇感笼罩了她，像是一股无形的、难以抗拒的推力。
Her curiosity at them, at all of this, becomes a palpable force.

将她推向更具体的来亚什基。
One pulling her ever closer to Rayashki.

FR-08 工厂颂 / The Ode of Factory

小镇广场（童话一面）

尼娜：很高兴您愿意参观我们的小镇，北方哨歌老师。
Nina: I'm happy that you let us show you around, Ms. Windsong.

尼娜：自从小镇的外面成了魔精的游乐场，到这儿来的客人们就越来越少啦～
Nina: We haven't had many other visitors here since the critters started coming near the town.

阿夫西维：我见过微笑的盲眼女士，她有一台很漂亮的打字机……维拉说，她是“作家”。
Avgust: I met a blind lady once. She always smiles, and she has a pretty typewriter. Vila said she's a "writer."

阿夫西维：作家去很多小镇，把白纸涂得满满当当，像我一样。所以，我把画儿送给了她……
Avgust: The writer has been to many towns, and she fills up her papers with so much ink, just like I do! So, I made a drawing for her, too.

尼娜：她答应我们，会让更多人了解来亚什基！
Nina: And she promised us that she will tell more people to come visit Rayashki!

彼得森：其他地方的人们……会喜欢我们的小镇吗？
Pyotr: Will people from other places like it here?

阿夫西维努力地掰着手指头，但那些脑子里的模糊影像蹦蹦跳跳的，连半点也抓不住。
Images bounce around in Avgust's mind, just out of grasp.

北方哨歌：别的游客们呢……？
Windsong: What about your other visitors?

阿夫西维：他们手上拿着很多绿色和红色的方格纸，还有闪亮的小松饼。
Avgust: I remember they had green and red rectangular paper and some shiny cookies in their hands.

彼得森：那些人想要用古怪的东西换走我们的罐头和礼物，但不愿意和我们一起劳动。
Pyotr: They tried to trade us their silly paper so they could take our cans and things. They never wanted to work with their own hands.

彼得森：——我们才不欢迎这些客人呢！
Pyotr: And Rayashki doesn't like lazybones!

在这一点上，孩子们的脑袋起伏得相当一致。
On this, the children's heads bob in agreement.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

尼娜：北方哨歌老师，彼得森同学昨晚带领大家一起复习了“如何成为一个好导游”——我们会做好的～
Nina: Ms. Windsong, Pyotr got all of us together last night, and we read through our "how to be a good tour guide" guide. So we can guide you!

彼得森：北方哨歌老师只是有点儿奇怪，她可不是懒虫！
Pyotr: Ms. Windsong is just a bit strange. She's not lazy!

别扭的孩子转过头去，一丝涨起的红晕漫过了他的耳背。
The child hides his face, but the blush on his cheeks reaches up to his ears.

阿夫西维：红甜菜汤、布林饼，还有——欧拉季益！
Avgust: This time, I want borscht, blinchik, and oladyi!

帕索诺：咳咳，阿夫西维同学，别急着许愿奖励……我们还没帮上北方哨歌老师的忙呢～
Pasono: Ahem, let's not hurry on to our rewards, Avgust. We haven't helped Ms. Windsong yet.

阿夫西维：噢……好吧。
Avgust: Oh, right.

较长时间的黑屏

大大小小的身影灵巧地穿过一张张紧闭的铁门。
Figures, large and small, pass deftly through the once tightly-sealed iron door,

终于抵达了唯一一间门锁尚未锈蚀的工厂。
arriving at the only factory left, whose lock has not yet rusted over.

工厂内部（有工人版）

克努特：欢迎到我们的工厂来，北方哨歌姑娘——！
Knut: Good to see you at our little factory, Ms. Windsong!

北方哨歌：你好，先生。
Windsong: Hello, sir.

克努特：我都听孩子们说了，你希望了解来亚什基的历史，还有过去发生的怪事儿，是吗？
Knut: The kids have told me that you want to learn more about the history of Rayashki and the strange things that have happened in the past, yes?

北方哨歌：是的……但这不违规吗？
Windsong: I do. But would that be going against any rules?

克努特：当然不，好姑娘，我们可不是什么吹胡子瞪眼、在家里划拉出一大片禁地的老古董。
Knut: Most certainly not, miss. We're not some stubborn old goats that dismiss people for asking questions.

他大步走上前来。
He strides forward.

克努特：谢天谢地——你比那位刻薄的芝诺先生看起来要友善多了。
Knut: In fact, I'm relieved—it will be much easier to talk to you than that bitter fellow from Zeno.

克努特：那位来自芝诺的先生和他的武装小队匆匆地巡视了咱们的工厂，只一会儿就消失了。
Knut: He came to the factory with his armed squad, took a quick look around, and left even without a polite farewell.

克努特：——就像一阵让人直打哆嗦的西伯利亚冷风。
Knut: Like a whiff of cold breeze, that one.

克努特：废旧的老式机器、几百个年龄参差不齐的工人们……
Knut: These old, out-dated machines and hundreds of workers, young and old, each one a mouth to be fed.

克努特：只能闻见腥味的鬣狗当然看不上我们的宝贝，嘁！
Knut: They are certainly not a pretty sight to the eyes of that greedy hyena. Hmph!

北方哨歌：功利主义的脑袋……
Windsong: A pathetic number-crunching cretin.

小声的“诽谤”清晰地落在了对方的耳朵里。
The whispered insult creeps up to her listener's ear.

克努特：哈哈～我越来越欣赏你了，好姑娘！如果不是忙着生产，我们必须得喝几壶——！
Knut: Hahahaha! I'm starting to like you, miss! We would have much to talk about, perhaps over a drink, if only I didn't have to get on with my work!

好奇的目光显然不止落在这儿的工人身上。
A curious look around goes beyond the hard-laboring workers.

两侧紧闭的大门，周遭飘忽的灰尘，情况似乎远没有想象中乐观。
Tightly sealed doors and a thick layer of dust on aging machinery paint a less than optimistic picture.

克努特：你注意到了，对吧～
Knut: You can see what's going on here, right?

克努特：没什么好难过的……哪怕芝诺不再需要矿石加工厂了，咱们也能把它改造成别的厂子。
Knut: Don't feel sorry for us. Zeno might no longer need this ore processing factory, but we can make use of what's left of it.

克努特：别慌神，只要度过这段被魔精们围困的日子，后续的原料和矿材都能源源不断地运进来！
Knut: Once we get rid of the critters, we can arrange for other minerals or materials to be shipped to Rayashki for processing!

他搓了搓手，靠在某个生锈机器的外壳上。
He rubs his hands together, leaning against the shell of a rusted machine.

克努特：就是可惜了这些个好时候，多少宝贵的时间都被白白地浪费了！
Knut: It is a shame we've wasted so much of our good years, never preparing for these bad times.

克努特：要不是那些猖狂的小怪物，我们至少能到矿场去——那儿才是我们的天堂！
Knut: If those strange little monsters weren't there, we might be able to return to our mines. Ah, then, we'd really be able to turn things around.

北方哨歌：矿场……？
Windsong: About these mining sites ...

她手上的笔记本在不同的页码上迅速地翻了几个身，像是飞溅的火星。
Her notebook flutters rapidly, its pages turning as fast as a rolling flame.

北方哨歌：克努特先生，你在矿场里有挖出过什么新东西吗？——尤其是卢恩矿石以外的东西！
Windsong: Mr. Knut, have you ever found anything there? Other than runium ore?

克努特：唔……
Knut: Hmm.

克努特：我向你保证，绝对没有！哪怕是矿场里的一颗砂砾我都能认得出来……至于新矿石嘛，从来没见过。
Knut: Never! I know those sites like the back of my own hand. I've never seen any other minerals of any worth there.

心思远比外表看起来细腻的大叔显然发现了对方眼底的失落。
The rugged man seems to catch her disappointment, and far quicker than she'd expect.

克努特：别心急，姑娘……让我再想想！
Knut: But give it some time, miss. Well, give me some time.

克努特：早在几个月前，芝诺还在热心地跟咱们打交道的时候——他们在矿区倒是发现了些我们从没见过的小石头。
Knut: Just a few months ago, back when Zeno was still keen to work with us and not just ship us away, I remember they found some strange little pebbles.

克努特：那些黑乎乎的小石子儿嵌在张牙舞爪的小怪物们的指甲缝里。
Knut: Dark pebbles that were stuck in the claws of those little monsters.

克努特：很快，芝诺派来了军队，把它们抓了个干净，连点渣滓都没留给我们……
Knut: Zeno soon sent out some troops and caught all the monsters. They didn't leave a single one behind.

北方哨歌：——！
Windsong: ...!

克努特：后来，芝诺就再也没提过这茬了，我们也再也没有见过那些黑乎乎的小石头了。
Knut: We never heard about those pebbles again, nor have we found more of them in the mines.

克努特：再后来嘛，卢恩矿石被我们开采得一滴不剩，越来越多怪模怪样的魔精霸占了矿区。我们就再也没去过那儿了。那儿也基本废弃了。
Knut: And you know the rest. Now we've exhausted the runium, and more and more strange-looking critters have appeared. So it's not safe to go back there. We left them completely deserted.

北方哨歌：……请你看看这个，克努特先生。
Windsong: Please take a look at this, Mr. Knut.

北方哨歌唰唰地画了起来，对方热情地凑了上来。
Windsong sketches fervently as Knut lumbers towards her with a curious eye.

克努特：不不，它们的爪子比北极熊还粗好几个指节……
Knut: No, no, their claws were thicker than a polar bear's.

画

克努特：噢！——和它们长得很像！
Knut: Ah! But these are closer!

克努特：但是牙齿要比这更大一些，像是把用了好多年的称手矿锄。
Knut: These monsters had much larger teeth. They almost looked like old mining picks.

克努特：没有耳朵——！
Knut: And no ears!

北方哨歌：……难道是霍伊图克？！
Windsong: Could they be some kind of Hoituk?

克努特：没错，就是这样！
Knut: Yes! This one looks just like the creatures!

北方哨歌：好吧……又一条赶来吃“小鱼”的大鱼。
Windsong: If that's true, then it may be another "big fish" that has come here to feed.

克努特：我可不会骗你，小姑娘……很多工人都见过它。
Knut: It is true! You can ask around. Many of the other workers have seen it.

北方哨歌：很好，霍伊图克的性状是明黄质，难怪之前这张理线图上的明黄色线索始终找不着主人……
Windsong: So, the color of a Hoituk is bright yellow, and that matches with these bright yellow lines I've traced here on the map.

北方哨歌：它们生性喜爱挖掘，常常出没于0—50米之间的地下。既然它们出现在这儿，就说明——
Windsong: They are burrowing animals, often living as deep as 50 meters underground. So if they were here, that must mean ...

工厂内部（有工人版）

北方哨歌：这儿一定有尚未被发现的新资源。
Windsong: That there must be some undiscovered resource here.

北方哨歌小声地嘀咕着，但她愈发明朗的脸色显然瞒不过任何人。
The corners of her mouth curl as she mutters the words.

克努特：看来结果不错，好姑娘。
Knut: Talk of undiscovered resources would be music to our ears, miss.

北方哨歌：咳——现在还不能下定论……
Windsong: Ahem. I don't want to get your hopes up. It's still too early to draw any conclusions.

克努特：哈哈，可你的眉毛都快翘到天上去啦～
Knut: Hahaha! Yet, the corner of your mouth is suggesting the opposite!

北方哨歌：在真正的结论出来以前，我必须得再谨慎一点！
Windsong: I must be cautious before confirming there really is a new resource!

北方哨歌：但无论如何，这都是一道新的曙光……谢谢你，克努特先生。
Windsong: Nonetheless, it's a silver lining. Thank you, Mr. Knut.

克努特：没什么好谢的，姑娘——说不准到什么时候，你的研究也能帮上咱们的忙呢～
Knut: Think nothing of it, miss! Maybe one day, you and your research will return the favor.

北方哨歌：但愿会有这么一天。
Windsong: I will, if I can.

她伸出手去，对方以更热情的姿态迎了上来。
She reaches out a hand, and he shakes it heartily with warm strength.

北方哨歌：也祝你们的工厂能早日复工。
Windsong: I hope your work here can be resumed shortly.

克努特：哈哈～就算没有芝诺，大家也能靠着自己赶走魔精，把工厂重新开起来。
Knut: Don't worry about us! We will find a way to drive those critters away and start production once again.

克努特：咱们的工人们都在这，那些钢铁家伙们也在。
Knut: We have all our brothers and sisters with us, and these machines still run perfectly.

克努特：再说了，我们总在劳动，总在生活，一切都会好起来的。
Knut: As long as we continue to put in our best effort, there is no reason why things won't get better.

他拍了拍周围仍在发颤的巨大机械们，像是在与老友勾肩搭背。
He pats the trembling, coughing machines with affection, like embracing an old friend.

北方哨歌：……这儿的人们都像你这么乐观吗？
Windsong: Is this exceptionally positive spirit common with the people here?

克努特：当然，毕竟全世界也找不着几个来亚什基这样的地方了——
Knut: Well, can't blame us for that! There are very few places in the world like Rayashki.

克努特：每一个人都能靠着自己的双手劳动，享受食物、疗养假期……我们有数不过来的冰球比赛、成人教育，甚至还有乐器培训……
Knut: Here, everyone earns their food and their rest through working hard together. Then, outside of work—ice hockey, learning courses, even music lessons—not everyone is as lucky as us.

克努特：我们可不想让来亚什基荒废下去。
Knut: That is why we won't let Rayashki die.

克努特的声音越来越高昂，像一首快活的乐曲。
Knut's voice rises as if singing.

克努特：咱们手上的功夫、脑袋里的东西，谁都没法抢走它们。
Knut: With busy hands and open hearts, Rayashki will live on.

克努特：就像这儿到处都有的熔炼炉一样～
Knut: It will grow stronger, glowing as brightly as these furnaces!

某种炙热的事物在里面熊熊燃烧着。
Something brilliant indeed burns within those furnaces.

崭新的造物在许多件工装与汗滴的交融中悄然诞生。
A product greater than any ore or slag, emerging from the melding of purpose and sweat.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

停下的笔又一次动了起来。
The pen that stopped stirs once again.

但这次，她似乎想抓住某种更缥缈的东西。
But this time, she seems to be sketching out something far harder to picture.

北方哨歌：……我承认，来亚什基是个相当特别的地方。
Windsong: I have to say, Rayashki is truly a curious place.

北方哨歌喃喃自语。
Windsong mutters to herself.

北方哨歌：它拥有任何地方都没有的某种特别的东西。
Windsong: It has a spirit which I've never found elsewhere.

北方哨歌：是的，这正是过去的理线学始终不曾具备的……
Windsong: Yes. Perhaps that's what was missing from the study of ley lines in the past.

“咕噜——”
*gurgle*

某种古怪的声响打断了她的思考。
An odd sound interrupts her contemplation.

向日葵悄悄地盖住了肚皮。
The sunflower pats against the boy's belly.

阿夫西维：北方哨歌，你想认识帕特里基先生吗？
Avgust: Ms. Windsong, would you like to meet Mr. Patrik?

克努特会意地点头。
The friendly bear Knut nods with an understanding smile.

克努特：你们确实该去食堂了，好姑娘们、小伙子们……你们现在正是长身体的时候呢！
Knut: It's time to go to the canteen, boys and girls. Eat well, and you'll grow strong!

克努特：帕特里基可是个热情的老伙计，镇上最好的厨师。
Knut: Patrik knows how to feed you well. He's the best cook in town.

克努特：不过嘛，你最好躲着他点。
如果你不想被他拉着胡侃上一整晚的话……
Knut: But I would suggest you be careful with that one, if you don't want to get stuck with his endless chatter all night.

北方哨歌：咳，碍于之前毫无必要的担忧，我确实不曾涉足过食堂，那一块儿的数据至今还是空白的。
Windsong: I have never been to the canteen. I stayed out of that area in my previous "visits" to avoid unwanted trouble.

阿夫西维：嘿嘿～向布林同志出发！
Avgust: Heh-heh! Forward, to Comrade Blinchik!

克努特：祝健康，好姑娘——期待看到你的成果。
Knut: All the best, miss! I look forward to hearing good news from you.

克努特挥了挥手，又坐进了他最熟悉的铁皮壳里。
Knut waves them off before settling back into his world of metal.

人影远去，机器声重新充盈了这里。
The churning and wheezing of machinery replacing words.

较长时间的黑屏

热闹的职工食堂里人头攒动。
The canteen buzzes with the din of workers.

孩子们领着北方哨歌，穿梭在排列整齐的餐桌和椅子间。
The children weave through the busy hall, leading Windsong by the hand.

职工食堂【有很多的工人】

阿夫西维：这里是大家的食堂。
Avgust: This is our canteen.

阿夫西维：肚子饿的时候，我们就会来这里玩捉迷藏。
Avgust: We play hide-and-seek here when we're hungry.

阿夫西维：炖汤同志、土豆馅饼同志每次都是最先被找到的！
Avgust: Comrades Stew and Potato Piroshki are always the easiest to find!

阿夫西维：它们一点儿也不聪明。
Avgust: They are not very clever at hiding!

阿夫西维：但是布林饼同志擅长捉迷藏，它只会在每周五的晚餐才会被找到。
Avgust: But Comrade Blinchik is very good at the game. He can only be found at dinners on Friday.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

尼娜：我们有很多好吃的……土豆泥，煮土豆，还有土豆炖汤！
Nina: We have good food, like mashed potatoes, and boiled potatoes, and potato stew!

尼娜：帕特里基先生说，真正的好厨师，能够把最简单的食物做成大家都爱吃的美味！
Nina: Mr. Patrik said a good cook can turn even simple ingredients into delicious food!

尼娜望了望周围，小声地说了下去。
Nina casts a glance around her before she speaks softly.

尼娜：大人们很善良，他们吃掉土豆，把奶酪和沙拉留给我们……
Nina: The grown-ups are so kind to us. Sometimes they give us their cheese and salad, so they only have potatoes to eat.

彼得森：别难过，尼娜同学，你不也总是把阿廖卡分给大家吗？
Pyotr: Don't cry, Nina. Remember when you shared your Alenka with everyone?

彼得森：等长大了，我们也能吃掉更多的土豆！
Pyotr: When we grow up, it'll be our turn to help the grown-ups with their potatoes!

气氛似乎凝重了起来。
There is an awareness in them, a gravity few children possess at their age.

好在有人浑然不觉。
Thankfully, some do retain their blissful innocence.

阿夫西维：我们还有铁帽子节，帽子里藏着很多好吃的！
Avgust: We also have the tin-hat festival, when they gave us metal hats with food in them!

北方哨歌：……？
Windsong: ...?

彼得森：阿夫西维同学，它的名字叫“工人节”。
Pyotr: Avgust, it's called the Worker's Festival.

彼得森：小镇每个月都会举办工人节。所有人围坐在食堂一起唱歌，维拉老师会为我们拉手风琴……
Pyotr: We have it every month. Everyone must sit in a circle in the canteen and sing songs, and Ms. Vila plays the accordion for us.

彼得森：每个人能得到一份罐头，图桑卡罐头、沙拉罐头，或者鲱鱼罐头。
Pyotr: We each get a can with food in it. Sometimes it's tushonka, sometimes it's salad, sometimes sprats.

阿夫西维：是的，过完铁帽子节之后，大家把帽子埋在土里，黄的、红的、白的……帽子会冒出小苗，长出叶子！
Avgust: Yes, and after the tin-hat festival, we would bury our tin-hats in the ground. Yellow ones, red ones, and white ones. Then tiny trees will come out from them next year!

彼得森：我早就说过了！它们不是铁皮土豆，它们也不会长大！它们只是普通的罐头！……堆在一起是、是为了更方便地处理它们，防止雪地被污染。
Pyotr: I have told you many times! They are not tin seeds, and they don't grow into trees! They are just tin cans! We only bury them so they won't pollute the snow.

孩子们的争论冲击着北方哨歌的脑袋，令她头昏脑涨。
The subject of their debate flips a hidden switch in Windsong's mind. The revelation flicking into light.

北方哨歌：堆积的铁皮……食物香气……
Windsong: Piles of tin cans ... Food ...

她猛然展开了地脉能量图，指向了最后一片各色线条与痕迹交织的模糊区域。
She unfolds the ley energy map, pointing to the last blurred area of interwoven lines and traces.

特效，红笔圈出矿区位置

北方哨歌：那些罐头，它们最后都去了这儿吗——？！
Windsong: Those empty cans you mentioned—did you store them here?

帕索诺：噢，我记得那个地方……大人们挖了一个很大的坑，不过现在，它肯定被冰块和石头填满啦～
Pasono: Oh, I know this place. That's where the adults dug a big hole; they put some things inside. It's covered up with rocks and ice now.

尼娜：是的，就是那儿！每个月，大家都会把废弃的钢铁重新熔成一个个方块。
Nina: Yes, Pasono is right! That's where the grown-ups put all our old metal after they make them into little cubes!

尼娜：维拉老师说，这样能让我们的小镇和周围的土壤更加整洁。
Nina: Ms. Vila said it helps keep our town and the whole region clean.

尼娜：那儿有什么奇怪的吗……？
Nina: Why, what's wrong with that place?

北方哨歌：……！
Windsong: ...!

北方哨歌：好极了，那儿一定有不少尚未被发现的“大鱼”！
Windsong: I'm thrilled! There must be lots of "big fish" left to be found around there!

北方哨歌：只要将这个推论形成一份具备可行性的报告，说不定能说服芝……咳，说服他们加派人手！
Windsong: If I can write a report and provide a practical plan, maybe I can get Ze- ... I mean, I could request reinforcements!

收起浮窗

她及时地刹住了车，把那个算不上友好的名字咽回了肚子。
She halts, swallowing back the unfriendly name.

孩子众：太好啦！我们又能去外面玩了！
Kids: Yay! School trip! School trip!

北方哨歌：当然不行！这可不是什么益智游戏——你们都得给我乖乖地留在镇上，所有人，明白了吗！
Windsong: This is no trip, children! I'm not going there for a hike! You must stay in town and be good. That goes for every one of you! Understood?

显然，这一决议难以服众。
Her resolution fails before she even finishes.

抗议声此起彼伏，盖过了周围的一切声响。
The children's protests rise in a disordered chorus, drowning out all other surrounding sounds.

也包括头顶正滋滋作响的电流声。
Only to be matched by the static fizz of an announcement.

贝托尔特：咳咳——！
Bertolt: Ahem!

北方哨歌终于抓住了难得的救命稻草。
Windsong clutches at a thin straw of salvation.

北方哨歌：嘘～安静，小脑袋瓜们！
Windsong: Shh. Quiet, kids!

贝托尔特：亲爱的朋友们，我们将在明天8：00开始举行最后一次听证会。
Bertolt: Attention please. Tomorrow, at 8 in the morning, we will be holding our final hearing.

贝托尔特：本次会议旨在厘清各位对于小镇处理方案的建议与疑虑，欢迎朋友们按需参加。
Bertolt: In this meeting, we hope to finalize our next steps and answer any remaining questions. We look forward to seeing you there.

FR-09 比知识更重 / Heavier Than Knowledge

会议室

贝托尔特懒洋洋地靠在沙发椅上，只瞥了一眼来人，便迅速地低下了头。
Bertolt leans back in his armchair, casting a fleeting glance forward before his head falls.

贝托尔特：怎么——你也打算在芝诺谋个一官半职？
Bertolt: What's this? Are you planning on getting a job with Zeno, too?

北方哨歌：……？
Windsong: ...?

贝托尔特：尽管你在这儿呆了几个月的时间，但很遗憾，你并不在这次的“来亚什基人员特聘计划”的名单上。
Bertolt: It says here you've been staying in this town for months, but it seems you're not on our list for "Potential Recruitment from Rayashki."

他脸上的笑容仍然维持着既有的温和。
The smile on his face remains as affably saccharine as ever.

贝托尔特：我得提醒你，对于你们这样的学者来说，拿出成果才是最重要的。
Bertolt: I should remind you, for you researchers, what you produce tells much more about you than your "efforts."

北方哨歌：这正是我来找你的原因。
Windsong: That's precisely why I'm here.

贝托尔特：噢——？
Bertolt: Go on.

对方终于又舍得抬起那颗矜贵的头颅来。
He finally deigns to raise his head up.

北方哨歌：根据我这段时间的调查，我几乎能够确信，这儿确实存在着某种尚未被开采出的新资源。
Windsong: Based on the recent investigations, I'm confident that there is a new energy source in the area that has yet to be discovered.

贝托尔特：……
Bertolt: ...

贝托尔特：这就是你花了几个月的时间才调查清楚的事？我们早就告诉过你们每一个人，接受委派的小学者，来亚什基一定有我们要找的东西。
Bertolt: And that's it? We already believed there was something here when we sent you out in the first place!

贝托尔特：你的任务是找到它，而不是向我确认这个早有答案的事实。
Bertolt: You were sent here to find it. Instead, all you do is confirm what we already knew.

北方哨歌：可你说的什么“永动能源”只是传说，不是么？
Windsong: But you said that "perpetual energy" was just a myth, didn't you?

贝托尔特：这当然不只是传说，女士。要不然我们怎么会派你们过来呢……？
Bertolt: O-of course, it wasn't "just a myth," lady. Why else would we ask you to investigate here in the first place?

北方哨歌皱了皱眉头，那张失望的臭脸毫不掩饰地在她眼前晃来晃去。
Windsong gives a frown that slips, quite intentionally, into a scowl.

贝托尔特：除此之外，你还有什么需要报告的吗？
Bertolt: Do you have anything else to report?

北方哨歌：……我想申请芝诺的协助调查。你派遣一支武装军队将我送往矿区深处，我会在那里进行下一阶段的研究。
Windsong: No, but I do need your help. I will need an armed squad to come with me to the mining sites so that I can continue my investigations into this subject.

北方哨歌：时间上我无法保证，这得视你们派遣的人员数量而定……
Windsong: I'm afraid I don't know how long it will take. It also depends on the number of soldiers you can spare for the task.

贝托尔特：咳、咳咳——
Bertolt: Aha!

贝托尔特：我猜，你开了一个一点儿也不好笑的玩笑。
Bertolt: You have a terrible sense of humor.

北方哨歌：我很认真。况且，这不也关乎着你们的目标吗！
Windsong: I'm not being funny. You want more research on the new resource too, don't you?

贝托尔特：可是，学者女士，你知道这意味着什么吗——？
Bertolt: Ms. Windsong, do you really think this is even a remotely reasonable request?

贝托尔特：这儿的魔精早已泛滥成灾，为了你的一个虚无缥缈的理论，我们就得耗费巨大的人力与物力——
Bertolt: Critters are running rampant in the area, and you demand help to verify what is, as far as I can see, a highly questionable conclusion. Why should I waste Zeno's time and resources on this?

贝托尔特：甚至搭上辛苦培养的芝诺精锐？
Bertolt: Not to mention putting the lives of our soldiers at risk.

北方哨歌：如果你还有疑惑，可以看看我目前整理出的这些……
Windsong: If you have doubts, please take a look at these files.

学者急迫地翻找着自己的背包，对方毫不客气地摆了摆手。
The researcher dives her hands into her bag but is met with a wave of dismissal.

贝托尔特：让我想想，是你的“理线学”告诉你的吗？
Bertolt: And let me guess, you learned all this from your "study of ley lines"?

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: I ...

贝托尔特：据我所知，这应该只是一门在“神秘学会考评会”和“人类科研课题立项”中几度没能通过的民间学派，没有成果，缺乏官方背书，甚至连研究员都没几个……
Bertolt: To date, the theory of ley lines has neither been approved by the "Arcane Study Review Association," nor accepted by the "Project Assessment of Human Science and Technology." It has zero academic achievements, zero endorsements, and aside from the questionable example in front of me—zero researchers.

北方哨歌：……这只是暂时的。
Windsong: That's all only a temporary setback.

贝托尔特：我同情你的遭遇，但很遗憾，在你拿出切实可行的证据之前，芝诺没法向一位编外的草根学者提供过多的帮助。
Bertolt: Ms. Windsong, I sympathize with the awkward situation I have put you in. However, Zeno simply cannot afford to waste resources on a proposal without any solid evidence.

北方哨歌：我会给你们成果的，只要你们先预支一点儿帮助。我保证！
Windsong: I will give you something; all I need is a bit of help upfront. I promise!

眼前的人没有丝毫动摇，但北方哨歌同样不愿放弃。
The look in his eyes is glazed, bored, but Windsong does not falter.

北方哨歌：协助小镇解决魔精问题，不也正是芝诺向这儿的人们提供的援助方案么？……这不过是举手之劳罢了！
Windsong: Did you not come here to deal with these critters? Then what's the fuss about? Can't you deal with them while accompanying me to these mining sites as well?

贝托尔特瞪大了眼睛，像是听到了些什么了不得的消息。
Bertolt's eyes widen, now unglazed, as he rises.

他在房间里来回踱步。许久，他终于挪到了窗台。
He paces silently, drifting at first, then proceeding to the windowsill.

贝托尔特：噢，天真的女士，你一定是误会了什么。
Bertolt: I'm afraid you've got our intentions altogether wrong.

窗户合拢起来，连风声也透不进来了。
The windows close tightly, sealing the last whispers of wind from the outside.

复位

贝托尔特：芝诺的目标从来都只有一个，就是传说中的永动能源。
Bertolt: Zeno is here for one thing only: a source of perpetual energy.

贝托尔特：这也是你的任务，找出它，而不是在毫无成果的时候向我提要求，我们可不是什么落魄学者的慈善资助机构。
Bertolt: This is what you have been tasked to find, with the resources you were given. We won't approve any further requests until you have a solid lead. We aren't paying you for a charity mission.

北方哨歌：……！
Windsong: ...!

北方哨歌：所以你们从来都不打算清理这儿的魔精灾害，也只堪堪派出了这么一支行动小队……就为了无声无息地彻底掌控这里？！
Windsong: So, then, you never planned on controlling the critters here. The squad you brought here was to control the town?!

贝托尔特：我们不希望引起其他组织的注意，显然，这也不是什么适合与他人分享的成果，不是么？
Bertolt: A force sufficient to deal with critters would have attracted unwanted attention from our rivals. It is not in our interests to share this town or its resources. I'm sure you can see that.

北方哨歌：哪怕最后找到了原矿，你们也不准备保留这座小镇……
Windsong: So, even if we do find the resource for you, you won't leave this town or its people alone.

贝托尔特：这可是人人觊觎的神秘学的终极能源之一，怎么能让一群化外之民来负责呢？
Bertolt: We're talking about the ultimate energy source of arcanum. Do you think we will just walk away and leave it to be squandered by a bunch of ignorant peasants and miners?

北方哨歌：可耻的说法……
Windsong: You should be ashamed of yourself!

贝托尔特的笑意终于收敛起来。
Bertolt's smile fades like a bad aftertaste.

贝托尔特：后续的处理方案并不在你的职权范围以内，你操心过头了，我们早就安排了合适的人选。
Bertolt: What we're going to do with Rayashki should be of no concern to you. We have made every arrangement for them.

贝托尔特：在真正的结论得出前，我们仍会努力地为当地居民提供力所能及的帮助。
Bertolt: We aren't monsters. Before the final decision is made, we will continue to help the locals as much as we can.

贝托尔特：当然，我们同样不会忽略对你的关怀。
Bertolt: Including you.

在草根学者心生异议之前，老练的负责人自然地将话题转到了一个更诱人的方向。
Before the wild-eyed researcher can voice her dissent, Bertolt steers the conversation with well-practiced ease.

他从书页之间抽出了一张漂亮的文书，沿着桌面滑向了北方哨歌。
Wordlessly, he draws out an attractive-looking document and slides it across the table toward her.

北方哨歌：这是……？！
Windsong: Is this ...?!

贝托尔特：别太惊讶，这不正是你心心念念的么？
Bertolt: You seem surprised. Isn't it what you have always wanted?

贝托尔特：想象一下吧，当它盖上芝诺的章，你就能在任何一所大学畅通无阻地开设你想要讲授的课程。
Bertolt: With Zeno's endorsement, you will be able to teach your program in any university.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

贝托尔特：芝诺已经向你表示足够的诚意了。
Bertolt: We have prepared this gesture of our good faith in you.

贝托尔特：别指望那支武装小队的协助，他们有更重要的事得完成。
Bertolt: Now it's your turn to show yours. Forget about an armed squad. They have more important things to do.

贝托尔特：依靠你自己，朋友。向我们展示你的本事，给我们带来你最真实可信的成果，而不是一沓沓枯燥无味的文书。
Bertolt: You're on your own, my friend. But prove to us that you can do this job, and bring us the best answer you can give.

收起浮窗

灰白色的信笺灼痛北方哨歌的指头，令她不自觉地颤抖。
The pale letterhead stings Windsong's fingertips.

贝托尔特：事成之后，它自然归你了。
Bertolt: And this piece of paper will be yours when you complete your mission.

北方哨歌：……我明白了。
Windsong: I understand.

贝托尔特：很好，也祝你好运，女士。
Bertolt: See that you do. Good luck out there, Ms. Windsong.

逐渐走远的脚步声+关门声
缓慢黑屏

雪地上的脚步声迅速而坚定，它孤独而勇敢地朝着某个早已被占领的王国而去。
Deep footprints, now half-buried in fresh snow, trace the path of the researcher's determined march behind her.

全屏大雪

落魄学者的勇气、热情与她的体温一同，于暴雪中迅速地冷却了下来。
Her courage, passion, and body temperature rapidly cooling against the blizzard.

北方哨歌：难道我疯了吗——？
Windsong: Was I out of my mind?!

北方哨歌：芝诺只是在敷衍我……就像是对付一头只擅长拉磨的愚笨驴子，几根胡萝卜就能让它围着磨盘团团转！
Windsong: He was just trying to get me out of his office. He threw a carrot out of the window, and I chased right after it like a blinded mule!

北方哨歌：可——
Windsong: Still ...

她小心翼翼地抚过衣袋里的那张薄薄的信纸。
Her hand lingers on the paper nestled within her pocket.

北方哨歌：这根胡萝卜实在太香甜了……
Windsong: Maybe this "carrot" is too good to let go.

认命般的叹息后，她小心翼翼地向着更深的地方摸索着。
With a sigh of resignation, she reaches deeper.

北方哨歌：现在，只要我补充好缺漏的证据，哪怕一点儿都好……芝诺就会相信我的理论，后续的研究也能够迎刃而解！
Windsong: Focus. Once I fill the gaps in my data, I will be able to pitch it to Zeno, and all subsequent research won't be a problem anymore!

北方哨歌：霍伊图克最主要的食物来源是地底的矿石。人工改造后的铁质物对它们而言仅仅能够果腹，绝不可能吸引它们横渡冰洋来到这儿。
Windsong: The primary food sources for Hoituk are raw minerals underground. Those processed metals only keep them from starving to death. They wouldn't have gone across any icy ocean just to gnaw on old equipment and trash.

北方哨歌：只需要再找到一些它们的活动痕迹，观察它们族群的整体状况，说不定就能知道是否有足以供给它们生存的其他食物。
Windsong: All I need to do is find a trace of their activities so that I can learn about their current conditions and, from there, locate their other food sources.

北方哨歌：冷静点儿，霍伊图克生性温和，它们很少会主动攻击人类……只要我再小心一点儿便好。
Windsong: Stay calm. Hoituk are gentle creatures. They rarely attack humans. I just need to be cautious.

遗憾的是，现实问题显然要比自我斗争复杂得多。
Her internal struggles will have to wait, as more practical problems loom larger.

疾风与暴雪几乎掩盖了这儿的一切，只有零星的几个罐头壳滚落在地。
The blizzard has covered almost everything, leaving a few cans to poke out, rattling along with the wind.

北方哨歌：&%#！*【德涅斯特河东岸粗口】！
Windsong: Crazy! Whoa!

北方哨歌：好吧，换个思路——
Windsong: Alright, change of direction.

北方哨歌：向下挖掘，扫描这片区域的线性结构，确定这边区域的地脉能量延伸方向……就像之前在锡尔伯里山那样～
Windsong: If I were to look down instead of looking forward, maybe I should scan the area and follow where the ley energy is leading. Just like I did at Silbury Hill.

北方哨歌：咳——当然，它们的结局最好有所差异。
Windsong: Ahem! Of course, I hope the outcome will be different this time.

她环顾四周，一望无际的雪地没过了能见的所有土地，也没过了她的仪器。
She surveys the expanse of boundless snow.

北方哨歌：在这之前，先清理出一片干净的区域——
Windsong: Before all that, I need to clear out this place.

北方哨歌：Природа это числа и черты.
Windsong: Природа это числа и черты.

咒术1

北方哨歌：Природа это мозаика цветов.
Windsong: Природа это мозаика цветов.

咒术2

土壤像是成了海边翻涌的浪花，抖落身上覆满的雪渍。
The soil churns in slurry waves along the seashore, a mix of mud, snow, and stone.

剧烈的振响迅速地传了出去，但她丝毫未觉。
A violent resonance spreads beyond it, one to which she is completely unaware.

霍伊图克？：嘶%#！嘶嘶%@——！
Hoituk?: *hiss*

显然，它们对领土遭到的破坏相当不满。
Clearly, these creatures harbor some discontent at these scars on their land.

北方哨歌：糟了！这儿的动静似乎闹得太大了。
Windsong: Shoot! Now I've done it.

北方哨歌：彻底退化的掘矿齿，三指长的锐牙——你们不是霍伊图克？！
Windsong: Those vestigial digging teeth, the three-fingers-long tearing teeth—these are not Hoituk!

霍伊图克？：嘶！
Hoituk?: *hiss*

它们张牙舞爪，像是在进行某种进食前的神秘仪式。
They bare their teeth and claws in a rhythmic way, like a primitive pre-feeding ritual.

北方哨歌：这副便于泅渡的鳞翼，你们是——
Windsong: These scaled wings must be for swimming. Then you must be ...

北方哨歌：基基图克的奥尔加异种！
Windsong: Mutant Kikituk from the Olga area!

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

北方哨歌：你们应该逡巡在奥尔加海峡，捕食那儿洄游而过的鲑鱼与鲸，而不是待在这儿！
Windsong: You should be at the Olga Strait, hunting for migrating salmon and whales, not here!

基基图克异种：吼&*#——！
Mutant Kikituk: *roars*

基基图克们再也按捺不住，朝着北方哨歌的方向扑了上来。
The Kikituks can no longer contain themselves and pounce towards Windsong.

北方哨歌瘫坐在地，大口地喘着粗气。
Windsong sits slumped on the ground, gasping for air.

基基图克们余怒未消，迟迟不愿离去。
Their fury has not yet abated; the creatures hold their ground.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

北方哨歌：你们怎么会出现在这儿？难道你们也有什么复兴人类捕食计划的远大航海目标吗？
Windsong: Why would you come here? What inspired you to trek across the ocean, just to hunt for humans?

遗憾的是，对方似乎无法理解她的抗议。
Her aggressors show no signs of understanding.

它们垂下长短不一的口涎，向着食物的方向步步紧逼。
They inch closer, drool drooping from their mouths.

北方哨歌：该死的，挖掘的齿爪退化之后，它们的触觉比霍伊图克敏锐得多了……
Windsong: D**n it! It seems, while their claws and teeth have degraded, their reflexes much quicker than a Hoituk's.

北方哨歌：哪怕是采用了人类减震工艺的采线仪，也逃不过它们的触觉。
Windsong: They perceived my approach, even though I used my ley line reader as a dampener.

某种由远及近的轰鸣声盖过了她的叹息。

飞过屏幕的子弹与一侧的开枪火光
A rumble, distant then near, drowns out her sigh.

热烈的枪声呼啸而来，准确地命中一只龇牙咧嘴的基基图克。
A gunshot hammers out nearby, the shot landing on one of the snarling Kikituk.

枪栓再一次被拉响，又一只基基图克落荒而逃。
The bolt is drawn back. The familiar sound sends another scurrying away.

北方哨歌：——！
Windsong: ...!

叶甫根尼：别愣在那儿！
Evgeni: Get out!

叶甫根尼：撤出那片区域，我会掩护你！
Evgeni: Get out of here! I'll cover you!

枪声持续了许久，落荒而逃的基基图克们终于放弃了它们的堡垒。
More gunfire thunders, over and over, until the last Kikituk abandons their position.

奔跑
喘气

北方哨歌：感谢你的救援，先生。
Windsong: Thank you, sir.

紧接着，她又像是突然想起了什么。
Composing herself, the researcher immediately returns to her work.

北方哨歌：那片……罐头园，它在这儿么？
Windsong: Evgeni, the kids told me about a can pile. Is it nearby?

叶甫根尼：罐头园？
Evgeni: Can pile?

他皱了皱眉，瞥了瞥不远处那片被翻得七零八落的雪堆。
He furrows his brow, motioning with his eyes to some hilly snowdrifts nearby.

叶甫根尼：或许是因为附近的野兽，又或者是那些不知道从哪儿冒出来的小怪物——我们埋下的铁块早就被啃食殆尽了。
Evgeni: They must be talking about our waste metal. I'm afraid it's gone, Ms. Windsong. Maybe animals dug it all out, or maybe those little monsters ate it.

北方哨歌：它们对铁块的袭击发生在卢恩矿石枯竭之前吗……？
Windsong: Do you know if that happened before or after the runium mines ran dry?

叶甫根尼：也许吧……
Evgeni: I'm not sure.

叶甫根尼皱了皱眉，扫了一眼那些东倒西歪的仪器们。
Evgeni's brow furrows again, this time casting a surveying glance at her scattered instruments.

叶甫根尼：……你不该来这儿，这儿没有你要找的东西。
Evgeni: You shouldn't be here. There's nothing of value to find in this place.

叶甫根尼：更不应该使用这些神秘学气味过重的装备。
Evgeni: And you're not supposed to be using this arcane equipment here, either.

叶甫根尼：对付这些凶悍的小怪物，应该用更传统的办法……否则，它们只会呼朋引伴，永远没个消停。
Evgeni: We have a better way to deal with these fierce little monsters. What you're doing will just attract more of them.

对方的说法震撼了她的认知。
His statement rattles her.

北方哨歌：你们能驱赶这儿的基基图克——？！
Windsong: You can drive away the Kikituks?!

叶甫根尼：不行，我们没多少家伙了，芝诺没有给我们送来任何新装备，更别说其他重武器了。
Evgeni: Not anymore. We don't have much left to fight them off with. Zeno didn't bring any equipment for our team, let alone any weapons.

叶甫根尼：你还是趁早离开这儿吧……
Evgeni: Go. Leave before it's too late.

他小心地检查手上的步枪，零件们咔哒咔哒，像是在接受检阅。
He carefully checks the rifle in his hand.

北方哨歌：如果我不愿放弃呢——？
Windsong: What if I don't want to just give up?

对方的动作滞缓了下来。
Evgeni slows down, making his inspection come across as even more deliberate.

叶甫根尼：我记得你的居留申请，一位研究学者。
Evgeni: I've seen your residence application. You say you are a researcher.

叶甫根尼：你的学识理应支撑你做出更聪明的决定，而不是继续从事一项绝无结果的危险研究。
Evgeni: Then you should be clever enough not to go down a fruitless and dangerous path.

北方哨歌：……我承认，这份莽撞是出于我的一己私利。但无论如何，这不是什么可以随意摒弃的东西——
Windsong: I admit that what I'm doing here is reckless, and maybe I'm just motivated by my own selfish interests. But I can't just walk away from my commitments.

北方哨歌：你在来亚什基生活了如此之久，关于“理想”的认知，你应该要比我清楚得多。
Windsong: You have lived in Rayashki for a long time. You know what "commitment" means here much better than I do.

对方的脸色变了变，他背过身去。
There is a shift in his face as he turns away from her.

北方哨歌：正如这儿的人们热爱这片土地，他们也从未打算离开。
Windsong: I won't give it up so easily, just like the people here won't give away their land like nothing.

叶甫根尼：只是种令人失望的顽固罢了。
Evgeni: It's stubbornness. That's all.

北方哨歌：……？
Windsong: ...?

叶甫根尼：他们应该在更广阔的地方发挥才能，而不是继续留在这里徒劳地牺牲。
Evgeni: They should have gone to other places and put their talents to good use, rather than staying here to fight for nothing.

北方哨歌坚决地昂起头来。
Windsong holds a stare, lifting her chin to match up to him.

北方哨歌：所以你任由芝诺摆布这儿的一切，什么也不做——你真的了解他们么？
Windsong: Is that why you gave away the town so easily to Zeno? Do you really even know your neighbors?

叶甫根尼：我们共事了数十年。你不觉得这个问题太可笑了么？
Evgeni: I have lived and worked together with them for decades. Don't be ridiculous. I just ...

叶甫根尼：……我认可芝诺的决议。
Evgeni: I agree with Zeno's perspective.

北方哨歌：啧——我走过很多地方，也见过不少像你这样的“家长”，打着为所有人好的名头，然后自顾自地付出，把一切都决定好。
Windsong: Tsk. I've been to many places, and I have encountered many people like you—stuck-up "leader types," making decisions on behalf of other people because "it's what's good for them."

叶甫根尼：无论是他们，还是你，都应该回到更适合你们的地方去。
Evgeni: And they should listen. Just as you should now.

那杆始终高昂的枪屹立着。
He braces the rifle as he motions her back and scans the near horizon.

叶甫根尼：对所有人负责，这才是我的责任。
Evgeni: It's my responsibility to protect everyone, to do right by them.

叶甫根尼：我会说服他们的，就在明天的全员大会。
Evgeni: I will make them see it tomorrow at the hearing.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: Ah!

FR-10 仅有的日子 / The Only Days Left

小镇广场（现实一面）

人们从四面八方鱼贯而入。
People stream in from all directions.

不约而同地站在了小镇命运的关口。
They stand now at the crossroads of the town's fate.

贝托尔特：咳咳——
来亚什基的朋友们，你们好。
Bertolt: *clears throat* People of Rayashki, my dear friends, good day to you all.

贝托尔特：在过去的两天里，芝诺完成了对这一区域的全方位危险评估与价值考察。同时，我们举办了关于小镇处理方案的听证会。
Bertolt: Over the past two days, Zeno has assessed the potential risks and benefits in the area, and held hearings on what should be done about the future of this town.

贝托尔特：我们的听证会似乎响应者寥寥，这似乎说明了一件确凿的事实：各位对芝诺的决定相当信任。
Bertolt: Our hearings saw very limited attendance. We've taken that to be a gesture of approval.

贝托尔特：当然，我们仍需感谢叶甫根尼先生在此次行动中的大力支持与配合。
Bertolt: Mr. Evgeni has put in a great effort helping to make these changes happen. We all owe him a great deal. Thank you, sir.

他向一旁的叶甫根尼致意。
He motions to Evgeni at his side.

一页崭新的文件展示在所有人的眼前，芝诺的印章刻意地盖在了最显眼的位置。
A freshly printed document unfurls before all present, Zeno's seal stamped deliberately in the most prominent position.

贝托尔特：请相信，我们已做出了对各位而言最妥当的安排。
Bertolt: Please believe that we have made the best decision we could for you.

贝托尔特：首先，来亚什基的卢恩矿石已经枯竭，在未来百年之内已无再生可能。
Bertolt: We all know the runium here has run dry, and the land has been exhausted of all further material wealth, now and into the foreseeable future.

贝托尔特：受此影响，当地的矿石加工厂已无继续运行的必要。
Bertolt: As a result, your local processing factory has lost its intended purpose.

贝托尔特：最重要的是，因全球形势的影响，芝诺大幅调整了对外政策。相比于继续维系缺少价值的关系，我们期待更有分量的合作对象。
Bertolt: What's more, Zeno has changed our cooperation strategy. Though your town's loyalty will never be forgotten, we must have a sober-minded view of its costs and benefits.

贝托尔特：综上所述，我们得出了最终的结果——
Bertolt: To sum up, our final decision is that ...

贝托尔特：来亚什基已无作为芝诺合作方的必要性与价值。
Bertolt: We will be ending operations and all future cooperation between Zeno and Rayashki.

一记重锤在广场上摆荡着，振出阵阵风声。
A heavy hammer swings in the square, producing a whistling wind.

克努特：咳，贝托尔特先生，您可能了解得还不够仔细。我们不止有卢恩矿石，我们有许多别的工厂……
Knut: Well, Mr. Bertolt, you have just got here; perhaps you didn't have enough time to get to know us well enough. Rayashki's value is not just in our runium. We have many other factories, too.

热切而急迫的话语从四面八方涌来。
Urgent words of protest flood in from all sides.

贝托尔特：是的，你们有砖墙厂、有发电厂、有搬运铲车，甚至还有运输带，可这一切都建立在开采卢恩矿石的基础上——
Bertolt: Yes, you have a brick factory, a power plant, many forklifts, a smattering of conveyor belts. But all these were all built and suited for only the processing of runium ore.

贝托尔特：但现在，它们已经失去了意义。
Bertolt: Without the ore, they simply have no benefit to us.

镇民众：……
Residents: ...

人群窃窃私语，不同的声音在一起呜鸣，像是滚开的沸水。
The crowd murmurs, voices bubbling up and simmering like boiling water.

贝托尔特敲了敲桌子，遏住了这一势头。
Bertolt raps the table, ending the broil.

贝托尔特：以上是对于来亚什基当下状况的说明。根据这一状况，我们为来亚什基准备了两套方案。
Bertolt: Now that you have full knowledge of the situation and our intentions, we want to assure you that your loyalty has not been forgotten, so we have generously prepared two choices for the future of Rayashki.

会场短暂地沉寂了下来。
The assembly hushes.

贝托尔特：芝诺认为，各位具有宝贵的坚定意志与非比寻常的技术能力。这是一种值得敬佩的精神……
Bertolt: Firstly, Zeno believes that you have many valuable qualities. The determination and skills you've shown in the past year of our cooperation have proved that your people can be a great asset to us.

贝托尔特扫过许多人的面庞。
Bertolt scans across the faces looking back at him.

贝托尔特：在座的不少人都符合芝诺的入职标准与需要。
Bertolt: Indeed, many of you already meet the entrance requirements to join Zeno.

贝托尔特：因此，我代表芝诺军备学院，向你们发出最诚挚的邀请——
Bertolt: Therefore, on behalf of Zeno Arms Academy, I wish to extend a heartfelt invitation to you.

贝托尔特：希望各位能够与我们一同撤离来亚什基，到芝诺各个分部任职。
Bertolt: Leave Rayashki. Join us and work for one of our other branches as members of Zeno.

克努特：什么意思？……难道芝诺打算彻底收拢这儿的所有人吗？
Knut: What are you saying!? You want us to abandon our home for some promise of a job?

贝托尔特：冷静点，克努特先生。我更愿意称之为一项基于理性的组织优化安排，一份为世界和平而出力的新机会。
Bertolt: Calm down, Mr. Knut. This is not about abandoning your home. It's about joining us in our efforts to contribute to world peace. Through a more optimized allocation of manpower.

镇民Ⅰ：你打算把我们所有人都糊弄到芝诺去——？
Resident I: So you're just going to pack us all up and ship us away to work for Zeno?

贝托尔特：……你误会了，女士。
Bertolt: You misunderstand, madam.

收起浮窗

他合拢文件夹，瞥了瞥北方哨歌身旁的孩子们。
He closes the folder, looking conspicuously towards the children beside Windsong.

贝托尔特：在芝诺，每年因未通过考核而淘汰的人员约占整体人数的4%，而因公牺牲的更多……
Bertolt: Every year, Zeno dismisses 4% of our employees because they failed to pass our rigorous work reviews. And the number of our colleagues that are killed in the line of duty is even larger still.

贝托尔特：芝诺的工作并非娱乐场，我们无时无刻不在面对着战火、纷争以及随时可能发生的地区冲突。
Bertolt: Working for Zeno is a privilege, not a gift.

贝托尔特：很遗憾，芝诺并不是什么滥造滥收的慈善机构，仅仅有一小部分人能够有机会入职芝诺。
Bertolt: That's why only a small number of you will be allowed to come and work for us.

镇民Ⅱ：什么……？
Resident II: What?

贝托尔特：当然，按照《视界线公约》第二章中关于“神秘学家权利保障条例”部分的第58条细则——
Bertolt: Now, according to Article 58 in the section on "protection of arcanist rights" signed at the Event Horizon Convention ...

贝托尔特：我们会在后续为没有被选上的镇民们提供基本的生存保障，将他们转移到就近的救济点，直到后续相关福利机构的介入。
Bertolt: We will provide basic supplies for any residents who haven't been offered a position with Zeno. They will be transferred immediately to the nearest relief station until our social workers contact them for further arrangements.

克努特：把小镇的孩子和老人统统扔到一边，送去某个谁也不清楚的福利院、养老院……
Knut: So then, you're suggesting you will send our children and elderly away to some kind of refugee station?

克努特：——然后咱们乖乖地当芝诺的乖狗狗？
Knut: And the rest of us must go to work for Zeno without any questions?

克努特：你**的【来亚什基粗口】！在说什么胡话呢！
Knut: You ****! This is total rubbish!

他愤怒地挥舞着双臂，撞开抵在前面的芝诺卫兵。
He waves off, then pushes aside the Zeno soldier in front of him.

芝诺卫兵：先生，请你冷静。
Zeno Soldier: Sir, please lower your voice.

贝托尔特：……顺带一提，克努特先生，就芝诺的标准而言，您的履历相当出色。
Bertolt: Well. You would be glad to know that your work experience in particular is valuable to Zeno, Mr. Knut.

他拍了拍克努特的肩膀，对方毫不客气地甩开了他。
He attempts a pat on Knut's shoulder, who shrugs him off.

但贝托尔特似乎全然不在意，他不紧不慢地展开了那份文件。
But Bertolt acts entirely unfazed, unfolding the document further.

贝托尔特：除此之外，我们同样准备了第二个方案。
Bertolt: If you're not interested in our first plan, we have another.

贝托尔特：如当地民众的撤离意愿较低，据前述分析，来亚什基本身仍拥有矿石加工厂基础，改造成本较低，且地处北极地区，隐秘性强——
Bertolt: If the residents in the area prove reluctant to relocate, Zeno can offer another alternative. As stated earlier, Rayashki is a remote town that possesses some significant industrial infrastructure.

贝托尔特：可作为新的军工厂设址地。
Bertolt: Therefore, it could be considered an ideal location for a new complex of arms factories.

维拉：……！
Vila: ...!

贝托尔特：同时，扩建码头也已列入优先选择项之一，这一调整属于芝诺全球海港战略的一环。
Bertolt: There would be a need to substantially upgrade the Rayashki wharf. To turn it into one of the seaports Zeno plans to build across the globe.

贝托尔特：除此之外，无线电广播基地的设计同样在我们的考虑之中。
Bertolt: Additionally, a radio station will be constructed within the town.

贝托尔特：建立稳定的信号收发系统利于维护北极地区的局势稳定，协调这一区域的国际关系。
Bertolt: Which will better facilitate our communication throughout the Arctic region so as to stabilize and coordinate with other powers in the area.

贝托尔特：……
Bertolt: ...

贝托尔特：接下来，我将为各位发放意愿登记书，请各位择选出自己更期望的方案……
Bertolt: We will now be passing out forms, listing the options I've presented. Please fill them in with your choice.

收起浮窗

维拉：你打算让来亚什基彻底成为芝诺的附庸吗？
Vila: So your only other option is to turn Rayashki into some kind of military base under Zeno's control?

贝托尔特：很遗憾，你可以这么理解。
Bertolt: I won't put it so bluntly, but you're not incorrect.

贝托尔特：我们得把有限的人力资源投入在更关键的地区，而不是芝诺以外的地方。
Bertolt: Our resources, as much as anyone's, are limited, and they must be put to good use. We cannot afford to waste them on strategically usele- ... costly people and places.

贝托尔特：如果你们需要芝诺的帮助，那总得付出点什么，对吧？
Bertolt: If you want Zeno to help you, you should be able to give us something in return, don't you agree?

他满意地合上了方案书。
He folds the proposal again with satisfaction.

人群的喧嚣与抗议被卫兵们远远地隔开了。
The crowd heaves in protest, held at bay by the soldiers around Bertolt.

克努特：叶甫根尼，这就是你说的最好的选择——？
Knut: So, Evgeni, this is "the best choice" you made for all of us?

贝托尔特：咳咳，我必须为叶甫根尼先生辩解几句……他是一位相当尽责的军人，也很希望能为他优秀的同胞做一些力所能及的事。
Bertolt: Ahem! I must speak in Mr. Evgeni's defense. He is committed to his duty and only wishes to do what he can for his compatriots.

克努特：啐！你为了自己口袋里的几个子儿，就把大伙给卖了个好价钱？
Knut: Shameless! All you've done is sold us out!

镇民Ⅰ：说得好，克努特！
Resident I: You tell them, Knut!

镇民Ⅱ：依我看，这儿的风可真够大的！要不然叶甫根尼的脑子怎么会被吹糊涂了呢！
Resident II: Do you think it's getting a bit windy lately? Clearly, with all the hot air in Evgeni's head, his mind has been blown away!

无数的目光落在叶甫根尼的身上。失望，难过，或许更加复杂。
Countless eyes fall on Evgeni. Disappointment, sadness—perhaps something more complex.

叶甫根尼：……
Evgeni: ...

叶甫根尼：我向你们保证，我的行为不涉及我任何的私人利益。
Evgeni: I swear to you, I am not doing this out of my own interest.

叶甫根尼：同志们，你们有更好的地方可去，有更远大的使命可以实现。
Evgeni: Comrades, there are many better places in this world, and you have better purposes to fulfill.

叶甫根尼：你们不应该在这儿虚度……
Evgeni: You shouldn't waste your time here.

克努特：呸——
Knut: Bah!

愤怒的潮水拍打在他的脸上。
The bear of a man puffs up with anger.

贝托尔特：朋友们，请冷静。是时候让理性回归你们的大脑了！
Bertolt: Let's all calm down, my friends! It's time to be reasonable!

贝托尔特：好好想想，芝诺已经向你们开出了极其丰厚的条件。
Bertolt: Think carefully. Zeno has been very generous regarding the offers before you.

他正打算洋洋洒洒地演讲下去，却不由得打了个寒噤。
He readies himself, as if about to launch into a grand prepared speech, but his hand trembles.

一道凛冽的风刮过了这位骄傲的芝诺先生。
A chill wind sweeps over him.

维拉：很遗憾，你还是得出了这样一个可笑的结论。
Vila: Generous? Now that's ridiculous!

维拉：我们不会放弃任何一位同胞，也不打算成为芝诺的应声虫。
Vila: We won't let you take away our family and friends, nor are we about to let you turn our town into a puppet state!

镇民Ⅱ：咱们绝不离开这儿！
Resident II: We will stay here! No matter what!

叶甫根尼：同志们，我理解你们的心情。
Evgeni: Comrades, I understand how you feel right now.

叶甫根尼：但我们不得不面对这一切，面对“撤离来亚什基”的现实。
Evgeni: But we must face the cruel reality of our situation.

维拉：……所以你不得不大义凛然地牺牲一部分人，又或是牺牲掉整个来亚什基。
Vila: And you're willing to send away our own people or give up on all we've built here because of this so-called "reality."

叶甫根尼：至少我们的处境得到了改善。
Evgeni: It is the only way forward.

叶甫根尼：如果继续固执地留在这里，所有人都会毫无意义地牺牲。
Evgeni: If we continue to stay here without any help, it will be the end of us either way.

维拉：难道我们不能依靠自己吗——？
Vila: Do we have to turn to Zeno for this help?

颓丧的神情笼罩了对方的脸。
Evgeni fails to react at first, but a defeated expression comes over him.

叶甫根尼：事实上，来亚什基的经济依托于卢恩矿石，依托于同芝诺的合作。
Evgeni: The truth is, just as Rayashki's economy has been dependent on runium, we remain dependent on Zeno.

叶甫根尼：如果没有芝诺……按照现在的消耗速度估算，来亚什基的资源将在一年内消耗殆尽。
Evgeni: Without them, at the present rate of consumption, we will be out of supplies and materials within a year.

维拉：……
Vila: ...

巨大的遗憾与沉默横亘在了所有人的面前。
A silent tidal shift sweeps over those assembled.

拉远

一切悄悄地落在自诩见多识广的学者眼里。
The researcher observes the change with harsh recognition.

北方哨歌：如此苛刻的条件么……
Windsong: This situation looks bad.

北方哨歌：芝诺控制这儿的决心实在令人讶异。
Windsong: Zeno is determined to gain control over this place.

她鬼使神差地摸到了那封尚未盖章的信笺，像是触电一般，迅速松了手。
She touches the unsealed letter. Her fingers jump away, as if it had been electrified.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

北方哨歌：如果我真的完成了芝诺指派的任务，这是不是意味着……
Windsong: But if I complete the task as Zeno requested, does it mean ...

贝托尔特关于小镇“化外之民”的论调言犹在耳。
Bertolt's words echo in her ears.

北方哨歌：……我也成了他人理想的刽子手。
Windsong: I will shatter their dream?

北方哨歌：可我同样是为了自己的理想……
Windsong: And what about my dream?

自我的辩白如鲠在喉。
The words stick in her throat.

北方哨歌：那些无端排挤理线学的人，他们也是如此安慰自己的么？
Windsong: Did the people who refused to acknowledge the study of ley lines act out of the same self-interest?

北方哨歌：嗯，我见过这一幕……
Windsong: I've seen this happen so many times before.

北方哨歌：只要沾上了一点和世俗格格不入的东西，就得应付类似的倒霉选择……陈词滥调的理想悲剧，聪明人的见好就收……
Windsong: A simple dream is made to face a cruel reality. Where the clever ones give up and leave, and the stubborn fools remain, waiting to be crushed.

北方哨歌：“是啊，这是我们自找的……”
Windsong: "We asked for our misery."

拉近

她拧过头去，据理力争的呼喊丝毫不曾退潮。
She turns, her mixed feelings refusing to settle.

冷酷的芝诺阵线阻拦了在场所有的异议，人群被推搡着后退。
The wall of soldiers has suppressed most of the dissent in the square.

但仍有人为之前赴后继。

拉近
But still, some bravely charge forward.

维拉：等等——！
Vila: Wait!

维拉：我还有话要说……
Vila: I'm not finished.

贝托尔特甩了甩手，毫不留情地走下台去。
Bertolt dismisses her with his hand as he leaves the stage.

贝托尔特：我已言尽于此，维拉女士。
Bertolt: But I am, Ms. Vila.

拉远

孤独的学者怔在一旁，那些奋力与坚决的呐喊声前赴后继地挤入一颗滞涩的脑袋。
The researcher remains stunned, but this potent chemistry of hope and resolve begins to catalyze something in her.

北方哨歌：……

北方哨歌：…………
Windsong: ...

北方哨歌：无意冒犯，芝诺老爷。仅仅靠我一个人，是没法完成你们的任务的。
Windsong: Sir! With all due respect. I can't complete this task alone.

北方哨歌：既然如此，请原谅草根学者的一颗挣扎与煎熬的心吧。
Windsong: As an ordinary researcher, I can relate to them. Please forgive me for interrupting.

她抬起头来，凝望着人群的方向。
She lifts her head proudly, looking out in the direction of the crowd.

北方哨歌：这些天，我听闻了许多关于来亚什基的故事。
Windsong: I have heard so much about Rayashki these days.

北方哨歌：一个艰难的开始，一群可爱的人们，以及无数个汗滴与鲜血熔铸的故事……
Windsong: They started from nothing, but bit by bit, they accomplished the impossible.

北方哨歌：他们至少应该获得一次为自己发声的权利。
Windsong: Their voice should be heard.

北方哨歌：Природа это числа и черты.
Windsong: Природа это числа и черты.

咒术1

脚下的土壤与雪块仿佛被赋予了新的生命。
The soil and snow under her feet becomes imbued with new life, rising up around her.

它们钳住军靴，堵塞枪口，像是孩子顽皮的恶作剧。
They clamp onto military boots and surge up and into gun barrels, plugging them up in a comical fashion.

拉近

芝诺卫兵：……？！
Zeno Soldier: ...?!

维拉：——！
Vila: ...!

娇小的身体显然不会放过如此良机。
The teacher seizes on this opportunity.

她翻过高大的人墙，向前追去。
She climbs over the wall of confused soldiers and charges forward.

芝诺卫兵：贝、贝托尔特先生……
Zeno Soldier: Miste- ... Mister Bertolt.

芝诺卫兵：不好了，我们快要拦不住他们了！
Zeno Soldier: We can't hold them any longer!

冲突短暂地中止了。
Their conflict ceases.

鳞片包裹的手掌用力扯住了贝托尔特的手臂，锋利的指甲撕破了他的袖口。
Scaly palms forcefully grab Bertolt's arm, sharp nails tearing at his sleeve.

维拉：现在，你愿意听我说了吗？
Vila: Now, will you listen to me?

一本干净如新的登记簿被塞回了贝托尔特的手里。
A clean, new ledger is stuffed into Bertolt's hands.

维拉：我们不需要芝诺的怜悯，也不接受芝诺的管制。
Vila: We don't need your help. Your soldiers and your tyranny are no longer welcome here.

贝托尔特：……
Bertolt: ...

拉远

维拉转过身去，面向更多的人们。
Vila turns around to face her people.

维拉：同志们，我们能够依靠自己的智慧与双手，解决我们的问题，你们能坚信这一切吗？
Vila: Comrades, what do you say? Shall we solve the problem with the strength of our own hands and hearts?

叶甫根尼：哼……
Evgeni: ...

克努特：当然，之前的每一次，咱们不都是这么过来的吗～
Knut: What else can we do? This is what we've always done when there was a problem!

镇民Ⅰ：只要我们所有人一同努力，就一定能想到好办法！
Resident I: There will be more solutions than problems if we work together!

镇民Ⅱ：说得没错！就算死，咱们也得死在一块儿！
Resident II: If I must die, I will die here with all of you!

克努特：臭小子，别胡说，现在还远没到要叫苦放弃的时候哩！
Knut: Just stop talking nonsense, you idiot! Nobody is going to die!

维拉：来亚什基是属于我们所有人的，它当然该由我们所有人来共同坚守！
Vila: Rayashki belongs to all of us. We will stand with it till its last moment!

那团温润的水竟在人群中烧得如此炽热。
The sudden surge of conviction and unity cows the guards as they move backwards.

反而更让人羞愧得面红耳赤。
Many blush with shame.

有人悄悄地退了出去。

心里
Some of them quietly withdraw.

北方哨歌：嗯……让人无地自容啊……
Windsong: Huh, they might say they're just ordinary people, but they are so brave and noble.

FR-11 最后一位乡下人 / The Ley Hunter

萧索的背影漫无目的地游荡在来亚什基的广场。
A lonely researcher aimlessly paces through Rayashki's square.

镇上的冷风显然不能抚平她的褶皱。
The town's cold wind clearly cannot smooth the wrinkles of her brow.

进独白

北方哨歌：理线学的新大厦，一定要建立在他人的废墟之上么？
Windsong: Could I really have traded the future of these people away for my ley line studies?

北方哨歌：唉，芝诺……
Windsong: *sighs* Zeno ...

北方哨歌：它迫使我来到这儿，用一根胡萝卜吊足了我的胃口，它毁了我的一切！
Windsong: I was a mule chasing after a carrot on a stick. They lured me here all so I could help ruin everything!

消人
出独白

那激荡的心声几乎要冲出胸膛。
Her voice bursts up from her chest.

跑

维拉：呵呵，你的精神看起来还不错。
Vila: Heh! You seem to be in a good mood.

北方哨歌：……？
Windsong: ...?

维拉：芝诺的人栽了跟头，他们被迫收拾好自己的计划书，灰溜溜地下台了……我们终于回击了他们一次。
Vila: We taught Zeno a lesson. They were forced to leave with their devil's bargains and tails tucked behind them. We fought back, finally.

维拉：一个很不错的小把戏，不是么？……谢谢你，北方哨歌同志。
Vila: A nice little trick, that was. Thank you, Comrade Windsong.

她朝着北方哨歌眨了眨眼，露出一个感激的笑容。
She smiles at Windsong, giving her a wink.

维拉：当然，我们深知这一壮举出自某位不愿透露姓名的正义人士之手。
Vila: We all know who the mysterious hero was that gave us a helping hand.

北方哨歌：我……什么也没做。
Windsong: I, I didn't do anything.

维拉：作为小镇的朋友并不是什么应该羞愧的事，反抗芝诺的强权更不是。
Vila: It's no shame to have helped your friends, not to mention to stand up to Zeno.

维拉：北方哨歌同志，你应该更自信些。
Vila: Have more confidence in yourself, Comrade Windsong.

北方哨歌：类似的反抗会有所结果吗……？
Windsong: But will you really gain anything from this fight?

维拉：也许会，也许不会。但我们总得做些什么，不是么？
Vila: Not sure, but we have to do something, right?

维拉：这正是我来这儿的目的。
Vila: That's why I'm here.

北方哨歌：为了……我？
Windsong: To talk to me?

北方哨歌：维拉女士，尽管我不清楚原因，但你似乎对我产生了一些过高的期待。
Windsong: I don't know why, but Ms. Vila, you must have thought too much of me.

北方哨歌：事实上，我只是一个无籍籍名的草根学者，也不具备显赫到足以影响芝诺决议的学术背景——
Windsong: In fact, I'm only a simple researcher. I'm not powerful enough to change Zeno's decision.

维拉：理解有误的是你，北方哨歌同志。
Vila: You are the one thinking too much, Comrade Windsong.

维拉：你的理线学并没有你想象的那般不受欢迎，它对孩子们产生了许多积极的影响……
Vila: Your ley line lessons were much more popular than you think. They have had a positive effect on the children.

维拉：他们开始关心更辽阔的世界，一个更立体、更细微的世界。多亏了理线学，现在孩子们总有问不完的问题……
Vila: Now, they are looking at the bigger picture and observing the world in a more detailed way. You've unleashed their curiosity.

维拉：“极光是远星们吐出的泡泡吗？它们的线条也像是一张漂亮的理线图，它们也是理线学家吗……？”
Vila: "Is the aurora the bubbles spit out by the stars? They form such a beautiful map. Do they study ley lines, too?"

维拉故作苦恼地摇了摇头，童稚的疑惑在此前的无数时刻缠住了她的眉间与臂膀。
Vila feigns distress, shaking her head with a pretended childlike confusion.

北方哨歌：但理线学，归根结底只是个仍然停留在理论上的学派。
Windsong: But it remains the case that the study of ley lines has never been verified.

北方哨歌：这个学派太小，野心却太大。迄今几十年来，它都只是一小撮人的自娱自乐，并且越来越少，直到现在……
Windsong: For all its ambitions. Only a limited number of people studied it in the past decades, and that number is decreasing even now.

对方若有所思地点了点头。
Vila nods thoughtfully.

北方哨歌：——！
Windsong: ...!

维拉：正如你瞧见的这样，这并不是某种难缠的皮肤病，而是我的过往。
Vila: What you are looking at is not some skin problem, but my past.

维拉：……身为鲁萨尔卡的过往。
Vila: My past as a Rusalka.

北方哨歌：鲁萨尔卡……传说中的人鱼——？！
Windsong: Rusalka? You mean the mermaid from folklore?!

维拉：呵呵，那是我的族群，一个来自北方的避世族群。
Vila: My people used to live in a far-secluded place in the north, away from the humans.

维拉：几百年来，我们与人类的交集只有敌视、掠夺，以及杀戮……
Vila: For hundreds of years, there was only hostility, plunder, and slaughter between us and them.

维拉：在最近的短短几十年，鲁萨尔卡才逐渐与人类有了更多的交集，也诞生了我……我在人类社会举步维艰了数十年，也习惯了人类的生活。
Vila: We only started to learn more about each other in the last few decades, and then I was born. It's been a hard life growing up within human society, but I've become used to it.

维拉：可现实并没有我想的那般顺利。
Vila: Still, some things never got easier.

维拉：对于更普遍的人类社会而言，他们并不欢迎像我这样的畸形生物。相比于接纳，鄙夷与取乐显然更符合他们的胃口。
Vila: Most humans still thought I was a freak. They "welcomed" me with mocking, sarcasm, and contempt for my people, my heritage.

维拉：而鲁萨尔卡同样无法容忍一条混迹在人类社会中的混血人鱼，他们始终不认同我的选择，不接受我在人类社会、在莫斯科、在圣彼得堡的躲躲藏藏……
Vila: As for the Rusalki, they too found a half-blooded mermaid unacceptable. They didn't approve of my living among the humans, forcing me to live as a fugitive in Moscow and St. Petersburg.

一个令他们作呕的名词，一片被人类夺取的家园，一个肮脏的内陆港口。
"Half-blooded." It was a nauseating term, one separating the Rusalki from the "scaleless" humans who had stolen their homeland.

是的，鲁萨尔卡的仇恨如此古老而长久。
An ancient myth that was the source of the enduring hatred between Rusalki and humans.

维拉：他们千方百计地抓捕我，试图洗礼、净化，抹去我这颗糟糕的污点。
Vila: They tried to catch me by every means possible, so they could wash away the "stain" they saw in me.

北方哨歌：听起来……是段相当煎熬的日子。
Windsong: That sounds very difficult.

维拉：当然，人类对鲁萨尔卡的污名化已经持续了几个世纪，鲁萨尔卡对人类船只的掠夺与捕食同样是刻在血脉中的本能。
Vila: Humans have stigmatized and hunted the Rusalki for centuries, while Rusalki still have the instinct to attack and plunder human ships even now.

维拉：如此深远且长久的仇恨又怎么能在一夕之间消弭呢？
Vila: How are they supposed to make peace in such little time?

维拉：数年前，我也认为这几乎是不可能的事……直到我来到了这儿。
Vila: That was what I thought years ago. Then, I came to this town.

她环顾这片洁白的土地，茫茫的大雪盖住了周遭的一切差异与缺陷。
She surveys the white land; the unifying cover of snow removes all distinctions, differences, and flaws.

维拉：“一个人类与鲁萨尔卡共同生活的美好世界”，我终于确信了这一件事——
Vila: "A wonderful world where humans and Rusalki could live in peace." I was finally convinced.

维拉：在来亚什基的土壤上，每一个人都能凭借自身所学发光发热。不论是人类、鲁萨尔卡，还是你的理线学。
Vila: In Rayashki, everyone can make contributions with their skills, whether you are a human, a Rusalka, or a ley line researcher.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

维拉：这并非强迫，你也不必为此感到负担。无论如何，你都是来亚什基的朋友。
Vila: I don't mean to give you more stress or push you. You will always be our friend, whatever your choice is.

维拉：它也绝不是一场短暂而遥不可及的梦。
Vila: But this is not an unreachable dream. It's real.

某种熟悉的话语又一次涌了上来。
A familiar phrase wells up inside her again.

一如某些早已沉寂的过往。

德涅斯特河沿岸地区，理线学社
Conjured from a long-silenced past.

拉近

北方哨歌：哈哈～
Windsong: Haha!

一个远比现在瘦削、顽固的少女忍不住欢呼起来。
The girl, then much thinner and more stubborn than now, couldn't help but cheer.

其余的理线师们似乎并没有受她干扰，他们漫不经心地整理着散乱的文件。
The other ley hunters fail to take notice, as they comb through their scattered papers.

北方哨歌：我成功地说服了《环境研究》的编辑，他终于同意刊登我们的报告了！
Windsong: The editor of the Environmental Research agreed to publish our report, finally!

北方哨歌：不过字数只能在五千字以内。
Windsong: But he only gave us 5000 words.

北方哨歌：版面也被严格地限制在最后几页……
Windsong: On the last few pages.

北方哨歌：但毫无疑问，这是一个美好的开始，重振理线学的第一步！
Windsong: Undoubtedly, it's still a good start, our first step to reviving the study of ley lines!

北方哨歌兴冲冲地分享着，她手忙脚乱地趴在桌子上，精心挑选着最经典的那一篇论文。
Windsong beams with excitement, clumsily sprawling over the table to select from their papers with care.

那些枯燥的理论映在女孩的瞳孔里，显得明亮、充满活力——
Dull, dry theories shine anew, bright and vivid in her eyes.

像是黑夜中闪烁的点点繁星。
A table of twinkling stars.

遗憾的是，再明亮的星也无法照亮整片黑夜。
Yet, these stars must shine against an all-consuming field of darkness.

理线师Ⅰ：我打算放弃了……去研究些别的，像是城市规划、景观设计之类的……
Ley Hunter I: That's it. I give up! Maybe I'll study something else, like urban planning, or landscape design.

理线师Ⅰ：至少，它们不会让我饿肚子……
Ley Hunter I: At least I can make a living that way.

北方哨歌仍埋头在层层叠叠的典籍与稿纸堆里，似乎并没有注意到对方在说什么。
Windsong remains buried in her heap of books and manuscripts, oblivious to the loss.

理线师Ⅱ：理线学已经被时代抛弃了，大家都说，它超出了科学验证的范畴……
Ley Hunter II: The study of ley lines is outdated. Everyone agrees now that it can't be verified by science.

理线师Ⅱ：“这是个没有出路的学派，是……毫无根据的神秘运动。”
Ley Hunter II: "This whole study was a dead end. Ley lines are only a baseless theory of arcanum."

桌子上的故纸堆大多是一些失去吸引力的、毫无意义的文字与线条。
The old papers on the table filled with nothing more than nonsense and wasted ink.

至少对大众而言已是如此。
At least that's how the world received it.

理线师Ⅲ：我试图参与其他神秘学家们的讨论，但几乎没有人听说过理线学，他们更关注拉普拉斯的前沿报告……
Ley Hunter III: I tried talking about our study of ley lines with other arcanists, but almost no one has ever heard of it. They are more interested in Laplace's breakthroughs.

理线师Ⅲ：或是更有趣的学界逸闻，比如那篇署名为“洛伦兹蝴蝶”的文章提出的“混沌能量”采样。
Ley Hunter III: Or anecdotes in their own fields, like the Chaotic Energy sampling mentioned in the paper written by the Butterfly of Lorentz.

星星们几乎全然黯淡了下去。
The stars have dimmed.

特写

北方哨歌：理线学……只是场短暂的梦吗？
Windsong: So, maybe it is an unreachable dream?

破
回到现实场景

片刻的恍惚令她迅速地清醒了过来。
A long moment of wistful distraction falls back into reality.

犹豫了许久，她终于缓缓开口。
After much hesitation, she begins to speak again.

北方哨歌：我很希望能帮上忙，但……
Windsong: I do wish I could help, but ...

北方哨歌：为了验证理线学当下的结论，需要耗费大量的人力与物力，也极有可能面临巨大的危险与牺牲……
Windsong: It would take a lot of resources to verify the theory behind ley lines. There may be even danger and sacrifice.

北方哨歌：哪怕是……芝诺，在我的研究产出实质性成果前，他们也不愿意为之倾注过多的注意力。
Windsong: Even Zeno has paid little attention to my research. They only see it as a means to an end.

北方哨歌：专家们著作等身，研究成果不可计数，他们能够互相引证，而我……甚至失去了我的师承。
Windsong: Researchers in other fields can stand on the shoulders of giants, while I, I don't even have a school to return to.

北方哨歌：从可预想的结果上来看，理线学也许很难对你们产生多少帮助。
Windsong: I doubt that the study of ley lines will help you much.

她低下头，艰难地向后退缩了几步。
She retreats a few steps back.

维拉：……原来如此。
Vila: I see.

维拉：谢谢你的坦诚，北方哨歌同志。
Vila: Well, thank you for your honesty, Comrade Windsong.

维拉遗憾地点了点头，没再说话。
Vila looks away, holding the regret deep in her chest.

北方哨歌：我很抱歉……
Windsong: I'm sorry.

维拉：那么，祝健康。
Vila: I'll see you soon.

北方哨歌：再见，维拉女士。
Windsong: See you, Vila.

她的头颅低了下去，转过身，艰难地迈开了步子。
She bows her head and turns, taking a few more difficult steps away.

也许是为那遥不可及的复兴之梦，也许是为这眼前所发生的糟糕一切。
Perhaps it was her unattainable dream of revival that slowed her, or the weight of all that had gone wrong.

维拉：请等等，北方哨歌同志——！
Vila: Wait, Comrade Windsong!

轻盈的步伐又一次跃向了她。
A burst of light steps leaps toward her once more.

北方哨歌：……？
Windsong: ...?

维拉：别忘了下一堂课的内容，孩子们都在等着你呢～
Vila: Don't forget your next lesson. The children are still waiting.

北方哨歌：可小镇……
Windsong: But the town is ...

维拉：生活仍在继续，我的朋友。
Vila: Life must continue, comrade.

维拉：至少现在，我们还是得大步地朝前走去，对吧？
Vila: We can't let our worries stop us.

北方哨歌：……好的。
Windsong: Okay.

FR-12 晚班列车 / The Night Train

学校课堂

粉笔在黑板上落下了最后一笔，讲台上的人也长舒了一口气。
As the chalk marks its final stroke, the lecturer exhales a long breath.

北方哨歌：孩子们，下课了。
Windsong: Class is over.

北方哨歌：谢天谢地，我还没把《理线学生物考》课上的内容忘个干净……
Windsong: Thank goodness, I still remembered the basic premises of "Ley Lines and Biology."

北方哨歌：如果你们有任何疑问的话，欢迎向我提问。
Windsong: Feel free to ask me any questions.

北方哨歌：高兴点吧，小家伙们～这门课程可不需要考试。
Windsong: Cheer up, little ones. There won't be any exams for this subject.

她开了个不大不小的玩笑，试图缓解课堂的尴尬。
She offers a hesitant joke to ease the awkwardness of the class.

往常的玩闹声并未响起，四周静悄悄的。
But their usual playful responses never emerge.

北方哨歌：嗯……？
Windsong: Mm?

她抬起头来，对上了许多双清澈的眼睛。
She turns to face a class that must be bored, asleep, maybe distracted. She's met instead by clear and focused eyes.

阿夫西维：北方哨歌，你还打算一个人偷偷去摘铁皮土豆吗？
Avgust: Ms. Windsong, are you going to dig up those potatoes alone again?

尼娜：我们能为您做些什么吗？
Nina: Is there anything we can do to help you?

尼娜：维拉老师说，我们一定能打败外面的魔精。
Nina: Ms. Vila said we will work together to beat the critters out there.

尼娜：如果我们能帮您画好地脉能量图，就一定能发现它们的弱点——！
Nina: That we will find their weakness as long as we finish the map with you!

彼得森：就像您教我们的那样！
Pyotr: Just like how you taught us to!

彼得森：“奇肯恩一点儿也不可怕，它们是草食性魔精，不会伤害人类……”
Pyotr: "Qiqirn are not dangerous at all. They are plant-eating critters and pose little threat to humans."

阿夫西维：我有绳子、花朵、白色的手套，可以挖出很多的土豆。
Avgust: I have ropes, flowers, and white gloves. We will dig up a lot of potatoes together.

阿夫西维：彼得森的力气很大，他能搬开路上的石头……尼娜会给大家准备暖和的水壶……还有、还有……
Avgust: Pyotr is strong. He can move any rocks that are in our way. Nina can prepare a kettle of warm water for everyone. And ...

孩子们的声音此起彼伏，哽咽与某些湿润的液体混在其中。
The children's voices rise and fall. What began as icy determination soon melts into a cascade of sobbing tears.

北方哨歌：……抱歉，小家伙们。
Windsong: I'm sorry, little ones.

北方哨歌：我也很希望能确定我当前所有的研究理论，但……
Windsong: I wish I could verify all the theories we've been working on, but ...

彼得森：……
Pyotr: ...

她将来亚什基的地脉能量图贴在黑板上，圈出了某块巨大的黑色漏洞。
She affixes Rayashki's ley energy map to the blackboard, circling an empty void.

北方哨歌：正如你们所见，这张地脉能量图并不完整。它仍缺少了关键的一角。
Windsong: As you can see, a critical part is missing.

北方哨歌：按照我一个人的精力，再快也得好几个月才能初步完成。
Windsong: It might take months to finish it.

北方哨歌：更何况，那儿还可能有其他更危险的魔精种群。
Windsong: Besides, there may be even more dangerous critters in that area.

阿夫西维：小镇会成为女巫的新城堡吗？空荡荡的，什么也没有。
Avgust: Then the town will become the witch's new castle? Or perhaps an empty castle.

孩子众：……
Kids: ...

收起浮窗

讲台下的目光们黯淡了下去。
Her attempt to turn the mood again falls flat.

新一堂课的铃声终于响了起来，中止了这个并不美好的话题。
A merciful bell rings out the dreary topic like a dirge.

下一堂课的老师及时地赶来了这儿。
Thankfully, the next teacher arrives swiftly to relieve her.

维拉：孩子们，请安静下来。
Vila: Quiet, children.

她的目光坚定，缓缓扫过台下无数的孩子们。
She holds her gaze firm, sweeping over the assembled children.

维拉：擦擦眼泪，高兴点儿～我们的来亚什基可不会轻易地被打倒——！
Vila: Wipe your tears and cheer up! Our Rayashki will stand strong!

彼得森：真的吗？！
Pyotr: Really?!

北方哨歌：……可你们要怎么坚持下去？
Windsong: But what are you going to do?

北方哨歌有些惊讶地望着对方，随即，她想到了一个最可能发生的结局，斟酌着开口。
Windsong is taken aback at first. Then, contemplating the possibilities, she delicately weighs her words.

北方哨歌：维拉……你们该不会向芝诺……贝托尔特并不简单，你得小心些……
Windsong: Vila, I hope you aren't seriously considering Zeno's ...

维拉：当然不，我们绝不向他们低头！
Vila: Of course not. They might try, but we will never give in!

维拉：但无论如何，让小镇维系下去，让所有人都能有个安全的去处。这才是最重要的……
Vila: No matter what, for now, we must find a way to protect our town. We will need a shelter from these critters.

维拉：这是来亚什基所有人的决定。
Vila: We've all decided to stay.

窗帘升了起来，窗外的阳光洒了进来。
The curtains part, and sunlight pours in from outside.

维拉：看看外面吧，孩子们～
Vila: Look outside, children.

维拉：这儿的每一个人，都在为小镇的存续做着力所能及的事。
Vila: Each and every one of us is doing what we can to hold our town together.

阿夫西维：克努特的工厂们在吐泡泡——！
Avgust: Knut's factory is spitting out puffy bubbles.

维拉：呵呵……
Vila: Heh heh.

维拉：工人先生们计划改造那些早已废弃的矿石加工厂。
Vila: The workers are going to transform the abandoned factories into something useful.

维拉：他们正在清理加工厂的石料与碎屑，这可不是件轻松的工作。
Vila: They are cleaning the ore and debris there. Not an easy job.

维拉：之后，我们会努力开展新的生产线，同周边的其他城市建立合作关系，鳜鱼养殖、罐头生产、土豆种植，这些不都是我们擅长的吗？
Vila: After that, we will start new production lines and cooperate with the surrounding cities. We will grow potatoes, breed fish, and make canned food. We will find our strengths together!

阿夫西维：我们要为工厂化妆吗？扎辫子，梳好头发，戴上漂亮的花环——！
Avgust: Are we putting makeup on the factories? We can paint their faces and put beautiful garlands on them!

尼娜：咦……帕特里基先生在做什么呢？
Nina: Hmm? So what is Mr. Patrik doing?

阿夫西维：大家都在排队，今天是铁帽子节吗？
Avgust: Everyone's waiting in line. Is it the tin-hat festival again?

维拉：很遗憾，小阿夫西维……我想我们很长一段时间都见不到布林饼同志了。
Vila: I'm sorry, Avgust. I think we will have to live without our tin hats and Comrade Blinchik for a long time.

维拉：他们正在举行签名仪式。
Vila: They are signing on to a reform of our rationing.

维拉：为了能把工厂涂成新的模样，我们需要缩减公共食堂的后续开支……
Vila: To transform our factories, we need to cut down the budget for the canteen.

阿夫西维：噢，谢谢你，布林同志——
Avgust: Oh, thank you for your sacrifice, Comrade Blinchik.

阿夫西维：你应该得到奖状，还有阿廖卡！
Avgust: You deserve a medal and some chocolate!

帕索诺：你们看，那边的推土机正在拆掉我们的房子！
Pasono: Look, the bulldozers are tearing down those houses!

维拉：是的，所有人都同意住得更紧密一点儿——
Vila: Yes. We all agreed to exchange some of our living space.

维拉：这样我们就能腾出更多的好土地，种下更多的食物～
Vila: For more land to grow food.

孩子们好奇而骄傲地趴在窗前，像是在告别，又像是在致意。
The children crowd the window, silent but beaming with pride, as if paying tribute.

北方哨歌的目光无声地跟随着维拉的讲述行进着，直到终点。
Windsong follows Vila's narrative to its conclusion.

学校课堂
北方哨歌：北方思考动作

北方哨歌：如此沉重的牺牲，值得么？
Windsong: The price is much higher than it first seemed. Is it worth it?

维拉：当然。
Vila: Of course.

维拉：无论是芝诺、慈善机构，还是其他任何一个地方，都不是来亚什基人的归宿。
Vila: You cannot find what we have here in Zeno's barracks, or in a relief camp. You can't find it anywhere in the world.

维拉：那些尚在襁褓的婴儿，那些垂垂老矣的同志们，他们也是来亚什基的过去和未来，我们又怎么能抛弃他们呢？
Vila: Think about the old comrades and the babies. They are the past and the future of Rayashki. How could we leave them behind or subject them to Zeno's whims?

窗外的机械声响远远地传来，像是来自土地的呼唤。
Mechanical sounds from outside carry across the snow from afar, as if the land itself is calling.

维拉：在来亚什基，没有人应该被放弃。
Vila: No one shall ever be abandoned in Rayashki.

北方哨歌：这是块令人羡慕的土地……
Windsong: I think people out there would be envious if they saw what you are doing here.

她没有再追问下去，窗外的一切映在她的眼里。
She doesn't press further.

维拉：我们并没有你所想的那么伟大……这是我们应该做的事。
Vila: We really aren't doing anything so special. We're only doing our job, our duty to one another.

北方哨歌的目光落了下来，那些细微的棘刺与鱼鳍又一次凝固在她的眼前。
Her scales and spines have risen, though whether it's a sign of pride or fear, she can't say.

北方哨歌：外面多的是类似的事，就像……夹在鲁萨尔卡与人类之间的你。
Windsong: There are lots of conflicts out there, conflicts like the one between humans and Rusalki.

北方哨歌：他们贬低、排挤着理线学，逼迫它解散……仅仅因为这个东西可能会抢走他们的研究经费、他们的名头。
Windsong: Like the ones that mocked the study of ley lines and dissolved our school. They did so simply because it might take from their funds or steal their glory.

北方哨歌：大家继续经营着各自的护城河，直到永远。
Windsong: Everyone forever building walls, just to keep separated from each other—Hoarding whatever they could get their hands on.

北方哨歌：然后一切的责任都可归咎为“当下的时代”。
Windsong: Then they blame the aftermath—the harm they do to others on "cruel realities."

北方哨歌：呵，当下的时代……所有人的头号大敌，一个完美的借口。
Windsong: Heh, "cruel reality." It seems to be everyone's mortal enemy, the cause of all suffering, war, greed—the perfect excuse to never care.

她愤愤不平地低诉着，坚实的力量从肩膀上传来。
Her voice trails into a mutter.

维拉：可来亚什基并不一样。
Vila: But things are different in Rayashki.

维拉：它毫无理由地接纳了我，从一周，到几个月，许多年……直到现在。
Vila: They took me in unconditionally when I came here. And they stayed friendly for a week, a month, a year, and even now.

维拉：它理所当然地成了我的理想——
Vila: So naturally, it became my dream, too.

维拉：一个属于所有人，也依赖所有人的美好构想，一个共同劳作、共同生活的健全社会。
Vila: Everyone here shares a beautiful dream, a dream that we can work and enjoy life together.

维拉：我们一同建设，也一同分享着其中的成果，不再需要与任何人勾心斗角，不需要忧心自己的未来，所有人都能够在他所希望的任何一个领域成就事业。
Vila: That someday there will be no more conflicts between people or worries about tomorrow. That everyone will be able to work to achieve their passions whatever field they wish to pursue. A utopia.

维拉：不仅是当下，也是未来。
Vila: It's not just a way of life for now, but the future we're always trying to reach.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

维拉：我将你的理线学与它所拥有的可能性传达给了来亚什基的许多人。
Vila: I've spread the study of ley lines in Rayashki, along with its potential.

一张朴素的邀请函落入北方哨歌的眼里，密密麻麻的签名潦草而坦率地挤满了所有的空白处。
A simple invitation catches Windsong's eye, with dense, messy signatures filling every possible space.

维拉：他们对这样一个能够发掘土壤中秘密的学派相当感兴趣。
Vila: They showed great interest. The study tells us about the secrets that could lie beneath the earth, after all.

维拉：“说不定，里面就藏着来亚什基的希望呢……？”
Vila: "Perhaps it will bring hope to Rayashki."

北方哨歌：可我并不是来亚什基人……
Windsong: But, I'm not one of you.

维拉：你帮助了这儿的孩子们，教授他们新知识，也同我们一起探索着来亚什基的可能性，不是么？
Vila: You taught the children something new, and you helped us explore our town's potential, didn't you?

维拉：这儿的所有人都很乐意帮助你。克努特同志骄傲地告诉所有人，他在工厂也参与了理线学的研究。
Vila: Everyone here is more than happy to help you. You know, Comrade Knut has been boasting about the assistance he was able to provide for your studies.

维拉：许多人都在羡慕他……
Vila: And many others are envious. They want to help you, too.

维拉：更重要的是，在这儿，你的理论已经有了一批好奇的学生。
Vila: More importantly, you already have a group of curious students here willing to study your theory.

收起浮窗

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

维拉：让我再问一次吧，北方哨歌同志。
Vila: Now, allow me to ask you again, Comrade Windsong.

维拉：——你愿意为来亚什基的全体镇民举办一场关于理线学的讲座吗？
Vila: Would you hold a lecture on ley lines for all the citizens of Rayashki?

北方哨歌：……哪怕理线学在外没得到任何的好名声，哪怕我还没有一丁点儿的实质性成果？
Windsong: Even though my research doesn't have any endorsements or achievements?

维拉：正因如此，我们拥有了一同建设的动力。
Vila: Of course. Perhaps we can be the first to endorse it, after your lecture.

北方哨歌：这是赤裸裸的引诱，维拉。
Windsong: You're being far too obvious in your recruitment tactics.

维拉亲切地笑了笑，不顾对方微弱的抗议，继续说了下去。
Vila smiles, ignoring her feigned protest.

维拉：这是个并不美好的世界。它有许多糟糕的问题，巨头倾轧、贫困问题、利己主义、排外运动……
Vila: The world is not a beautiful place. Poverty, privilege, egoism, exclusivism, so many problems.

维拉：但未来并不见得始终如此。
Vila: But that doesn't mean it can't get better in the future.

维拉：至少在来亚什基，我们能有一些新的试验。它说不定会成为一个未来的符号，一个新世界的预兆，一张所有种族、所有主义都能和谐共处的蓝图。
Vila: Perhaps, the experiment we're doing in Rayashki now will become the symbol of a better future, a new world where all races and ideas can coexist.

维拉：当然，它也许会失败，留下一片废墟与遗憾。
Vila: Well, of course, it may fail and end up a ruin.

维拉：但至少——我们来过。
Vila: But at least we've tried.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

她注视着维拉的背影，仿佛看到一艘驶向远岸的巨轮。
She watches Vila standing proudly, as if gazing at a great ship bound for distant shores.

它孤注一掷，永不退缩。
Venturing all, never shrinking back.

维拉：我们热爱这里，也情愿为之牺牲。
Vila: We love our home, and we're ready to devote our lives to it.

北方哨歌：我这算是上了一艘摇摇欲坠的新船？
Windsong: I can't shake the feeling you're inviting me aboard a leaky boat that could sink any moment.

维拉：或许吧，北方哨歌同志。
但在这儿，鲁萨尔卡不是你的敌人，而是朋友。
Vila: Maybe, Comrade Windsong. But should we sink, remember your friend is a Rusalka, and we do well underwater.

对方不置可否地眨了眨眼睛。
Windsong blinks, half-wondering if her new friend has gone mad.

一双手郑重地接过了那封邀请函。
And finding it madder still that she is reaching out to solemnly accept the invitation.

北方哨歌：荣幸之至。
Windsong: What an honor.

FR-13 别了芝诺！ / So Long, Zeno!

小镇广场（童话一面）
The crowd has gathered together again.

人群又一次汇聚在了这里。

北方哨歌：我……
Windsong: I ...

她又一次登上了魂牵梦萦的地方。
It is a familiar place—one she's visited in dreams before.

好奇抵过了鄙夷，期待漫过了指责。
This time, though, her watchers seem more curious than doubtful.

无数热忱的目光落在她的身上。
Their eager eyes follow her every move.

北方哨歌：接下来，我将为在座的各位介绍我的学派，理线学——
Windsong: Today, I am going to introduce the study of ley lines.

北方哨歌：以及对来亚什基当前状况的研究进程。
Windsong: And the progress of my research on Rayashki.

北方哨歌深吸了口气，从笔记本里抽出了几页“古老”的研究笔记。
Windsong takes a deep breath, pulling out a few pages of research notes.

它们在一双双振奋起来的手掌间传递着。
The pages are passed from hand to hand, stirring excitement.

北方哨歌：多亏了在座各位的帮助，我绘制出了一张初具雏形的地脉能量图谱。
Windsong: Thanks to your help, I have finished a draft of the town's ley energy map.

北方哨歌：也确认了来亚什基地区的大部分资源存量情况。
Windsong: And I have confirmed the presence of many precious resources.

克努特：就凭着这些五颜六色的线条……？
Knut: Through these colorful lines?

北方哨歌：不同颜色的线与光点昭示着地脉能量在不同生物及土地矿物中的留存状态。
Windsong: These lines and spots show us the state of local ley energy. Each color represents a different concentration of creatures or minerals.

北方哨歌：简而言之，冻土与冷霜覆盖着这一区域的绝大部分土地，它们的资源量相当富裕。
Windsong: Simply put, this area covered in frozen earth and frost contains many rich resource veins.

北方哨歌：象征着它们的冷灰色痕迹铺满在了能量图的大部分角落，但它们始终没能入侵小镇的内部。
Windsong: These gray marks symbolize them. They are located in most of the corners of the map, all of them outside of town.

镇民Ⅰ：噢！爷爷辈总念叨着这事，最早的时候，小镇一无所有，连半颗种子也种不活……
Resident I: Oh! Maybe that's why Grandpa said we couldn't grow anything here in the beginning.

镇民Ⅰ：后来，咱们从遥远的北方运来了一方方丰沃而柔软的黑土，它们成了小镇的基石。
Resident I: They eventually solved that problem by importing rich black topsoil for our fields.

北方哨歌：而这儿赖以生存的卢恩矿石，则是铅色的。
Windsong: As for the runium you've mined to make a living, look at the dark gray marks.

北方哨歌：根据图谱显示，这儿呈现出的铅色痕迹越发模糊，我们几乎无法观测到它的存在了。
Windsong: According to the map, they are becoming increasingly scattered and faint, so it can be hard to see them.

克努特：……
Knut: ...

北方哨歌：除了本身的自然资源，我们同样能根据地脉能量图确认生物痕迹的存在。
Windsong: Besides resources, we can also find concentrations of different creatures using the map.

北方哨歌：深蓝色的痕迹属于奇肯恩，而湖蓝色则属于出没于港口与海湾的奇肯恩变种，它们以植物为食，小镇内部的各个角落都能发现它们的痕迹。
Windsong: The navy blue marks represent the Qiqirn, while the aqua green ones represent the mutant Qiqirn from the wharf. They feed on plants, and you can find their traces in many corners of the town.

北方哨歌：而红棕色的痕迹则属于基基图克，它们生性凶狠，喜欢一切神秘动物与神秘学气息丰裕的“食物”。
Windsong: The red brown marks are the Kikituks, an aggressive species. They're vicious by nature and prey on just about anything arcane they can find, even other creatures.

收起浮窗

克努特：这些东西快把咱们的脑袋给挤满啦～咱们可记不住这么多东西。北方哨歌同志，你有什么更简单的法子吗？
Knut: I feel as though my head is going to explode from all this new information. Can you explain a little simpler for this old workhorse, Comrade Windsong?

北方哨歌：当然。
Windsong: Of course.

她自信地点了点头，小心翼翼地掏出了一小撮绒毛。
She proudly produces a small handful of fluff.

北方哨歌：它来自一头在矿区活动的基基图克，在叶甫根尼先生的协助下，我完成了取样。
Windsong: This sample comes from a Kikituk in the mine. I took it with Mr. Evgeni's help.

叶甫根尼：……
Evgeni: ...

克努特：可再怎么观察，它看上去不也就是一撮普通的软毛吗？
Knut: Seems like just a normal piece of fluff, no matter how I look at it.

北方哨歌：在旁人看来，这甚至不能做成一把小刷子。
Windsong: Yes, and in most people's eyes, it's nothing more than that.

北方哨歌：但在理线师的眼中，它呈现出了巨大的信息量。
Windsong: But in a ley hunter's eyes, it reveals a great deal of information.

北方哨歌：嗯……深蓝色与红棕色交织在了一起，还掺杂了些许铅色的光点。
Windsong: Ah. The navy blue marks and the red brown ones seem to mix together. And there are also dark gray ones popping out among them.

北方哨歌：看来这位基基图克先生的伙食还不错，说不准是一顿奇肯恩肉汤配卢恩矿石特调开菲尔。
Windsong: So it looks like our Mr. Kikituk ate well. Perhaps he had a Qiqirn soup with runium-flavored kefir.

克努特：哈哈，看来咱们率先在魔精群体中实现了共同理想。
Knut: Hahaha, looks like these critters have realized our dream long before we could.

镇民Ⅱ：可那些黑色的小玩意是……？
Resident II: But what about those black marks?

镇民Ⅱ：如果我没记错，北方哨歌同志，你刚才给咱们展示的能量图也有一大片类似的黑色痕迹……
Resident II: If my memory serves me right, the map you just showed us had those black marks, too.

收起浮窗

北方哨歌：是的，它们与目前已知的任何一种生物或非生物都无法匹配。
Windsong: Yes, but they don't match any creature or resource we know.

北方哨歌：我认为，它属于一种新的资源。
Windsong: I believe it represents a new kind of resource.

普通镇民：噢……可这种新玩意儿在哪儿呢？！
The Other Resident: Oh! Well, where is it then?!

场上的气氛明显地热烈了起来。
The mood has intensified, residents clamoring around to see.

北方哨歌：我想，这一问题的答案，只能在那一块区域才能找到了。
Windsong: We can only find the answer in this area here.

克努特：……是矿区的最深处？
Knut: You mean in the depths of the mine?

北方哨歌点了点头，继续说了下去。
Windsong gives a slow affirmative nod.

北方哨歌：也是地脉能量的源头。地脉能量从那儿蒸腾而出，附着在所有生物与非生物之上。经过食物链的演化与循环，它们又无一例外地朝着那儿回流。
Windsong: The ley energy is emanating from there. Afterwards, it flows throughout the "food chain," passing through all kinds of creatures and materials before eventually returning to its source.

北方哨歌：而我们所尚未勘测到的大片新资源，也极有可能出现在那儿。
Windsong: Then our new resource is probably somewhere there.

克努特：如果咱们能找到它们，就再也不用受那芝诺的鸟气了！
Knut: So we need to find it! Then we won't have to put up with Zeno anymore!

像是抛入了一颗闪烁的火星，人群开始窃窃私语。
The audience sparks up. Rippling murmurs turn into a burst of questions and excitement.

克努特：你……还有别的证据么？
Knut: But, do you have any other proof?

他激动地搓了搓手，像个等待糖果的单纯孩子。
He lays out his hands, as if expecting Windsong to put something there.

北方哨歌：当然。克努特先生，你还记得之前在矿场里挖出的魔精么？
Windsong: Of course. Remember the critter you found in the mine, Mr. Knut?

克努特：你提到过它的名字，叫霍、霍伊……
Knut: Yes, you said it was called, em, a Hoi-Hoitoo.

北方哨歌：霍伊图克，基基图克的亚种。与基基图克相反，它们活跃于地底，喜食一切矿石。
Windsong: Hoituk, a subspecies of Kikituk. They live underground and feed on minerals.

克努特：可那时候，咱们的卢恩矿石已经不剩多少了。
Knut: That was around the time we had begun to run out of runium.

北方哨歌：但它们并没有因此离去，反而愈发活跃了起来。显然，有别的东西吸引了它们，不是么？
Windsong: Is that so? But they were still there, perhaps even more active than usual. That could only mean they were attracted by some other mineral or energy source, right?

北方哨歌：而在我之前的调查中，尽管没有发现它们的踪迹，但我确实找到了与它们关系密切的另一种魔精，奥尔加异种。
Windsong: And even though I didn't find any further Hoituks during my research, I did find the Olga mutants, one of their close relatives.

北方哨歌：而对于这类群居性魔精而言，这至少能佐证霍伊图克的存在！
Windsong: Since they are social creatures, my discovery must prove the presence of some of these Hoituks, even if we cannot find them yet!

四周的欢呼声越来越大，叶甫根尼干咳了两声。
The surrounding cheers swell again, prompting Evgeni to clear his throat.

叶甫根尼：就为了一个缺乏实证的猜想，我们就得浪费无数人力去开凿冻土层叠的地底么？
Evgeni: But in the end, this is all just conjecture. Are we really going to waste all our time and money on your assumptions?

叶甫根尼：你的说法有完整的论证吗？
Evgeni: Or can you prove it's something more than conjecture?

北方哨歌：这只是初步的结论。
Windsong: I would call it a preliminary conclusion.

叶甫根尼：它们是否得到任何一种官方学说的支持或引证？
Evgeni: But could it be endorsed by any authorities or proven theories?

北方哨歌：目前……没有。
Windsong: So far, no.
