叶甫根尼：所以，它们只是如同童话故事般的臆想与猜测，对么？
Evgeni: So then, it is little more than a fairy tale. Am I right?

北方哨歌：我承认，这确实是场风险极高的豪赌……
Windsong: I admit it's a gamble.

叶甫根尼的眉头皱得更厉害了，嘴角挂着一丝冷笑。
Evgeni's now-infamous brow furrows once more.

叶甫根尼：开采并不是件轻松的事情。
Evgeni: It's never easy to dig, you know.

叶甫根尼：芝诺撤走了他们的挖掘设备，只给来亚什基留下了一堆过时的老家伙。
Evgeni: And Zeno has already withdrawn all their own equipment. All we have left in Rayashki are some outdated machines.

叶甫根尼：而刚才北方哨歌女士提到的魔精……它们确实能作为证据，但无可否认的是，它们同样代表着危险。
Evgeni: Besides, Ms. Windsong mentioned the critters. Maybe their presence there is some kind of proof, but they are themselves a danger.

叶甫根尼：那儿的魔精显然比小镇周边泛滥得更加厉害。
Evgeni: It is obvious that there will be many more critters there than near the town.

叶甫根尼：难道你们打算为了一个虚无缥缈的理论浪费时间，然后眼睁睁地看着同胞们牺牲在那儿吗？
Evgeni: And you would have us waste time—perhaps even sacrifice our comrades—to pursue what could just be a fairy tale?

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

对方步步向前逼近。

北方哨歌无声地张了张口，眼前的一切变得更熟悉了。
He advances closer, step by step.

闭眼

缓缓黑屏
Windsong's mouth opens silently. The look on his face far too familiar.

理线学轰然倒塌前的那一刻。
The moment before the collapse of ley line academia.

是的，正是这样的眼神。
Yes, that is the look.

质疑、痛惜，压得人几乎喘不过气来。
The suffocating weight of questions and regrets.

考评员Ⅰ：毫无疑问，这是个验证成本极高的理论。
Examiner I: There is no doubt, the cost is simply too high.

考评员Ⅰ：有人乐意去那些荒郊野岭，再挖出几个深坑，来确认里面有没有什么魔精骨头之类的吗？
Examiner I: Who would be foolish enough to dig some holes in the wild just to see if there are critter bones in there?

四周有低低的窃笑声传来。
Harsh sounds of laughter come from everywhere and nowhere all at once.

考评员Ⅰ：答案已经很清晰了，我们并不需要一个掺杂了神秘学的地理学分支，也没有必要浪费不必要的人力。
Examiner I: The answer is very clear. We don't need a new kind of geography mixed with arcanum. Let's save everybody some trouble.

考评员Ⅰ：关于理线学的正式立项申请：不予通过。
Examiner I: Conclusion: the application for Project: Ley Line should be rejected.

考评员Ⅱ：附议。
Examiner II: Agreed.

北方哨歌：我……
Windsong: I ...

考评员Ⅱ：呵，现在谁都想挂个乱七八糟的学科名，然后试图在这儿分一杯羹么？
Examiner II: Heh, even cranks can apply for research funds nowadays.

她踉跄着退了几步——

撞在某个结实的物体上。
She staggers back.

开眼
Bumping into something solid.

某种陌生而熟悉的水润触感从肩膀后头传来。
A strange yet familiarly cool sensation lands on her shoulder.

不知什么时候，维拉站到了她的身后。
Vila stands behind her.

维拉：往前走，北方哨歌同志——往前走。
Vila: Keep moving, Comrade Windsong. Keep moving.

维拉：遇到一丁点儿困难就退缩，这可不是来亚什基人的作为。
Vila: The people of Rayashki don't back down in the face of their problems.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

维拉：困难也好，问题也罢，我们都能一同解决它，对吧？
Vila: Whatever it is, we can fix it together, right?

一阵冷冽的风突兀地袭来。
A cold wind rushes between them through the open window.

叶甫根尼：直入正题吧——
Evgeni: Let's skip to the point.

叶甫根尼：我希望你能终止目前的研究。
Evgeni: I want you to stop your research.

北方哨歌：……什么？
Windsong: What?

叶甫根尼：开垦矿区已经让许多人受伤了，而这只是个开始。
Evgeni: Our exploration has only just started, yet many of our people have already been hurt.

叶甫根尼：你能保证未来不会有人因此牺牲么？
Evgeni: Can you promise there won't be further injuries, or worse, before we've found this fairy-tale treasure?

叶甫根尼：你所称的新资源只是个未知数，而我们不得不为之支付高昂的代价……他们本应在更好的地方参与建设。
Evgeni: Your so-called new resource is still unconfirmed, yet the price we've paid looking for it is already mounting. We had other options, safer options for all of us.

雨点密密麻麻地淋了下来，把北方哨歌浇了个通透。
The snow has turned to wet rain; it splashes up from the windowsill and on to her as they speak.

北方哨歌：我们会用更充分的知识武装自己……
Windsong: We just need to be better prepared. We will arm ourselves with more knowledge for next time.

叶甫根尼：我理解你的诉求，为了你的理线学，是么？
Evgeni: I know what you're after here: the study of ley lines, right?

叶甫根尼：比起这儿只有满腔热情的门外汉，我为你找来了更合适的人选。
Evgeni: The people here may be enthusiastic, but they are only laymen. I've spoken with someone who can help you far more.

不紧不慢的脚步声踏入了房门。
The unhurried steps of expensive boots mark an unfortunately familiar guest.

贝托尔特：很高兴见到你，北方哨歌女士。
Bertolt: It is good to see you, Ms. Windsong.

贝托尔特：或者说，一位来自非正式学科的敏锐学者。
Bertolt: Our proud scholar of a budding, if still informal, school.

他的面庞显得真诚而惊喜，就像是他们从来没见过似的。
His expression is genuine and surprised, as though this is the first time they've ever met.

北方哨歌：你好，芝诺的大人物先生……不得不说，你的态度真让人受宠若惊。
Windsong: And you, the Big Shot from Zeno. Should I feel flattered you stopped by?

对方像是根本没意识到北方哨歌刻意的揶揄。
He feigns obliviousness to Windsong's teasing.

贝托尔特：在叶甫根尼先生的强烈要求下，我向芝诺申请调阅了你的详细资料。
Bertolt: I read your files, as Mr. Evgeni suggested.

贝托尔特：芝诺追踪过许多神秘现象，也勘察过不少的神秘学环境，但从未见过对神秘现象的研究如此执着的年轻人。
Bertolt: You know already that Zeno has investigated many arcane cases and been deployed to many places related to arcanum, but we have never met anyone quite as obsessive in their study as you are.

北方哨歌：那现在呢？……高高在上的大人物打算信任一门乡野学派了？
Windsong: What now? Have the big shots decided they are going to trust my studies?

贝托尔特不置可否地笑了笑。
Bertolt smiles. He always smiles, brimming with all the joy of a crocodile.

贝托尔特：尽管我个人十分欣赏你的坚持，但暂时还不行。
Bertolt: Well, while I might admire your perseverance myself, no, they're not convinced.

贝托尔特：我更好奇的是，遍布全世界的足迹为你和你的学派带来了什么收获吗？
Bertolt: We just wonder what you and your school have gained from this long journey?

他的目光穿过北方哨歌，打量着她身后散落一地的资料与纸张。
He looks past her, assessing the mounds of scattered papers.

北方哨歌：说正事吧。
Windsong: Enough with the crap.

贝托尔特：感谢叶甫根尼同志吧～
Bertolt: As you wish. First, I believe you owe Comrade Evgeni some thanks.

北方哨歌：……？
Windsong: Huh?

一封崭新的推荐信递到了北方哨歌的手上。
A fresh letter of recommendation is handed to Windsong.

贝托尔特：尽管你的成果在芝诺看来并不足够，但叶甫根尼同志主动将自己的名额出让给你。
Bertolt: The less than satisfactory results from your study may not have earned this letter from Zeno, but Comrade Evgeni insisted on us offering it to you.

贝托尔特：在他的举荐下，你获得了一个难得的新机会——芝诺的试验场地，与知名学者的交流机会，一封正式的盖有芝诺印章的推荐信。
Bertolt: Once you have our recommendation, you will be able to communicate with all the renowned scholars in our lab. Your long wait for recognition will be over. A once-in-a-lifetime opportunity.

他的语气不紧不慢，仿佛胜券在握。
His tone is calm. His victory is assured.

叶甫根尼：我唯一的要求是……你能放弃这场不切实际的闹剧。
Evgeni: All I ask is stop this farce.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: Heh!

收起浮窗道具

北方哨歌：真让人感激涕零……
Windsong: Well, I am so grateful. I think I might cry.

北方哨歌：大家一起巴巴地望着，等着芝诺大发慈悲，为我们分好一个个去处，然后我们再为此滴下几滴热泪来，对么？
Windsong: All we have to do is wait for Zeno's grace to be bestowed on us. We should be moved to tears by your mercy, no?

贝托尔特：撇去你发言中那些情绪化的成分，我不认为这一选择有什么问题。
Bertolt: Putting aside your sarcasm, I would suggest you consider the danger of throwing away this opportunity.

贝托尔特：相比于前赴后继地扑倒在可能性不大的矿区，让所有的精英都能走上正轨，这有什么问题吗？
Bertolt: You are wasting time, effort, maybe even lives on some foolish wild goose chase. We can offer the people here a much safer and more feasible way forward. Don't you see?

贝托尔特挑了挑眉，像是在宣布一条颠扑不破的社会真理。
Bertolt raises an eyebrow. He presents his case less as reason than as indisputable truth.

北方哨歌：那来亚什基呢……？
Windsong: And what about Rayashki?

对方古怪地看了她几眼。
He looks at her pitifully.

贝托尔特：对于一些过时之物而言，悄无声息的消失是最好的结局。
Bertolt: All things come to an end. It will disappear quietly, overtaken by the wilds of this land, when the time comes.

贝托尔特：……当然，它们将会留在历史长河中的某个角落，不是么？
Bertolt: At least, it may leave a small place in the historical records.

贝托尔特：无意冒犯，叶甫根尼先生。
Bertolt: No offense intended, Mr. Evgeni.

叶甫根尼：……如果得不到芝诺的帮助，我们显然无法解决当下的所有问题。
Evgeni: We cannot solve the problems we're having without Zeno's help.

北方哨歌：只要找到新的资源，一切的问题都会迎刃而解——
Windsong: All of these problems will be solved as long as we find this new resource.

贝托尔特：咳咳——你误会了，北方哨歌女士。
Bertolt: Ahem! I'm afraid you're mistaken, Ms. Windsong.

贝托尔特：这片土地对于芝诺的意义在于其中的神秘学家，而不是一个孤零零的空壳。送走所有的镇民后，我们便会将这儿彻底封闭。
Bertolt: As far as Zeno is concerned, the value of this land is exhausted, fairy-tale resources notwithstanding. Once we've transferred the arcanists away, Rayashki will be abandoned.

他终于露出了些许真实的愠怒。
The crocodile smile cracks again, growing annoyed at his now long-overdue victory.

贝托尔特：这是出于芝诺的责任感与危机意识，而非什么别的可能性，你明白了吗？
Bertolt: We are aware of the danger that staying here poses to these people, and it is our responsibility to save them. Whether they wish to resist us or not. That's the only reason for our decision, understand?

北方哨歌：——！
Windsong: ...!

北方哨歌放下了那张凝聚着无数人心血的地脉能量图，什么也没说。
Windsong sets down the ley energy chart, the culmination of her countless efforts, without saying a word.

贝托尔特：还是关注些更现实的问题吧～
Bertolt: Let's be practical.

贝托尔特：芝诺有许多出色的年轻人，有良好的环境……也有更好的未来。如果你能通过考核，你就能得到一个真正重振理线学的机会。
Bertolt: Zeno has many outstanding young people, a strong academic atmosphere, a better future. You will get your opportunity to revive your school of ley lines, if you pass the exam.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

她的手指按在那张信纸上，手指从新印的纹章上缓缓划过。
Her fingers press onto the paper, tracing a newly embossed seal.

一根比之前更为甘甜与芳香的“胡萝卜”，它无声地倒映在北方哨歌的瞳孔中。
The "carrot" is sweeter and more fragrant than before.

在过去的许多时间里，她曾不止一次地想象过类似的画面。
How long now had she imagined this moment?

在幽闭而沉闷的地下室里，在薪水微薄的编辑社里，在无数促狭而冷冽的目光里。
In dim, stuffy basements, in underpaid editorial offices, under faceless, nameless, scrutinizing gazes.

贝托尔特：这是为了你们所有人好。
Bertolt: This will be a better choice for all of you.

北方哨歌：呵……
Windsong: Haha.

北方哨歌：这位高不可攀的先生，放下你那被消费主义和精英主义彻底销蚀掉的脑袋瓜，你就没理解到点更高尚的原因吗？
Windsong: Mr. Big Shot, could you use your rusted brain to think of a more noble reason than consumerism and elitism?

北方哨歌：我们不愿放弃这里，难道仅仅是因为对个人优渥生活的向往？
Windsong: Do you really think our desire for a better life is the only reason why we refuse to leave?

北方哨歌：你们理所当然地踩着普通的人们跃升，将我们这样的草根芦苇视为理所当然的代价。
Windsong: You used ordinary people as a stepping stone to power and privilege, and even now you take our sacrifices for granted.

贝托尔特：你得面对这个残酷的现实，尽管是芝诺，我们也没法拯救所有人。
Bertolt: Reality is cruel: not you, not Rayashki, and not even Zeno can save everyone. You will have to deal with that.

贝托尔特：倒不如说，这是一种社会运转中必然发生的自我优化。
Bertolt: You should take what is to come as an inevitable optimization of our society's development.

北方哨歌：是的，就算找到了新的资源，他们也不得不面临着更贫乏的生活、更艰难的前路。
Windsong: I know. Life may still get harder even if we find this new resource.

北方哨歌：但那又如何呢？
Windsong: So what?

她终于拾回了某种久违的勇敢。
The defiance in her voice reignites her long-lost courage.

北方哨歌：精英主义的旗帜插满了一切随处可见的角落，但至少它还没能打败这儿。
Windsong: Your brand of elitism may have invaded every corner of the world, but not this town, not yet.

贝托尔特：我理解你，草根学者大都保有如此朴素的认知。
Bertolt: I see, most scholars like you hold the same naivete.

北方哨歌：他们不愿抛下任何一个同胞，不愿为个人的美好未来而放弃没能搭上新快艇的同胞们。
Windsong: They refuse to leave any of their "comrades" behind, even if the price is their own future.

叶甫根尼：……
Evgeni: ...

北方哨歌：让各位前赴后继的并非理线学，也绝非某人的个人理想。
Windsong: What we would sacrifice ourselves for is not the study of ley lines, or any other personal goals.

北方哨歌：——而是千千万万个携手并进的夙愿。
Windsong: But our dream to thrive together!

北方哨歌：一个光明的未来。
Windsong: To live in a bright future we all can share!

北方哨歌：至于这个……
Windsong: As for this ...

她卷起了那张精致的推荐信。
She scrunches up his gaudy recommendation.

画面震动+清晰的揉皱纸团的声音

北方哨歌：我不再需要它了。
Windsong: I don't need it.

贝托尔特：……！
Bertolt: ...!

贝托尔特：呸——草根永远都是草根。
Bertolt: *spits* A leopard never changes its spots.

贝托尔特丢下最后一句话，头也不回地离开了。
Bertolt leaves his final words hanging in the room, departing without looking back.

揉皱的信轻飘飘地飞出了窗外，它落在窗外连绵的大雪中，消失得无影无踪。
The crumpled letter rolls out of the window. It lands in the snow, slowly being covered until there is no trace of it left.

一切会变得更好么？
Will things get better?

北方哨歌无暇他顾，她瘫坐在椅子上，大口地汲取着新新世界的空气。
Windsong, too preoccupied to care, slumps back in her chair, gulping in the crisp air of her new world.

叶甫根尼：……我很羡慕你的单纯，北方哨歌姑娘。
Evgeni: I envy your innocence, Ms. Windsong.

叶甫根尼：在过去的许多年里，我也曾相信过我们是历史性的人物，肩负着改造世界的重大使命。
Evgeni: For many years, I believed that our mission was to change the world.

叶甫根尼：当我抬头看的时候，新世界的大门已经关闭了。来亚什基在惯性中继续向前，我试图维护现在的一切……
Evgeni: But when I looked up, the gate to the new world was already closed. Little Rayashki just coasted along, and I tried to keep everything the way it was.

叶甫根尼：但我失败了。
Evgeni: But I failed.

叶甫根尼：来亚什基已经走上一条注定的路，与所有的努力无关，与我们是否有着坚决的意志无关。我们曾试图生产一个真正的、具有历史意义的东西，但……
Evgeni: Rayashki is doomed. All our efforts, our will, our dreams—nothing can change the creeping reality. We attempted to achieve something meaningful, something that could make history, but ...

叶甫根尼努力昂首，他的面庞隐没在灯光照不到的黑暗里，看不清表情。
Evgeni strains to lift his head, his face obscured in a kind of darkness beyond the reach of light.

叶甫根尼：不仅是芝诺，对于整个世界而言，保守才是当今的主流。
Evgeni: The spirit of the times stands against what we are building here, not just Zeno, but the whole world.

叶甫根尼：现实正是这样，寡淡无味，了无生趣，令所有人失望。
Evgeni: That's what reality is like: boring, cruel, disappointing.

场面一时间陷入了无言的沉默。
The scene falls into a wordless, motionless quiet.

许久，北方哨歌终于慢腾腾地直起身子。
After a long while, Windsong rises.

她终于蜕去了沉甸甸的外壳，甩开了那颗本就不属于她的胡萝卜。
She has shed all other burdens, and the tantalizing carrot is gone.

北方哨歌：你太悲观了，叶甫根尼同志。
Windsong: You are too pessimistic, Comrade Evgeni.

叶甫根尼：……？
Evgeni: Huh?

北方哨歌：芝诺如此反常的积极招徕让我至少确定了一件事。
Windsong: Zeno has tried to recruit me several times. Do you know what I've learned from all their efforts?

北方哨歌：——他们不希望我们继续下去。
Windsong: They don't want us to explore that mine.

北方哨歌：他们努力地贬低我们，为来亚什基的灰暗前路而痛惜，为我们谋划了一条无比远大而光明的前程。
Windsong: They belittled our efforts, offered pity for Rayashki, and then planned out a promising future for us.

北方哨歌：可哪怕有人负伤，甚至因此牺牲——他们也不愿意为来亚什基提供任何多余的帮助。
Windsong: Yet they didn't give us a hand, even when our people were injured or died.

北方哨歌：难道高高在上的老爷们是出于慈悲的关怀，才如此迫切地希望我们停止探索吗……？
Windsong: Do you really think they are so eager to stop us just because they don't want any more sacrifices?

叶甫根尼：——！
Evgeni: ...!

北方哨歌：当然不是，我的朋友。
Windsong: Of course not, my friend.

北方哨歌：就我这些年摸爬滚打得出的经验而言……
Windsong: A lesson I learned from living in their society ...

北方哨歌：——永远别做让你的敌人满意的事。
Windsong: Never do what your enemies want you to do.

她用力地拍了拍对方的肩膀，陌生而熟悉的狡黠又回到了她的脸上。
She grasps his shoulder, giving it a shake to pull him up to his senses.

北方哨歌：芝诺在害怕我们——
Windsong: Zeno is afraid of us.

北方哨歌：他们害怕我们找到新的火种，害怕我们不受蛊惑，拥有只属于我们的、他们无法操控的未来。
Windsong: They are afraid that we may discover a new kindling to relight our fire, that we may burn so brightly that we grow out from their control to create our own future.

叶甫根尼：你……
Evgeni: You ...

北方哨歌：可他们战胜不了我们——来亚什基是我们的，未来也是我们的！
Windsong: But they can't have it their way. Rayashki belongs to us, as does the future!

那团早已燃尽的灰似乎又冒出了些微火星。
Faint flickers of that fire seem to be there, somewhere in the man before her.

叶甫根尼神色复杂地昂起头来。
Evgeni looks up with a complex expression.

叶甫根尼：我会慎重考虑你的看法，北方哨歌……同志。
Evgeni: I, I will give it some thought, Ms. Wi- ... Comrade Windsong.

FR-16 前进进行曲 / Marching March

钢铁巨兽们轰隆作响。
The steel behemoths rumble.

它们驶过压平的雪原，驶过临时开凿的泥浆池，终于驶入了理想之地。
They have plowed through snow, mud, and soil to reach their target.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

北方哨歌：自从理线学被取消资格之后，我似乎就再也没有进行过关于地脉能量的实证研究了。
Windsong: I haven't done any field investigation of ley energy since our school fell apart.

北方哨歌收起改线尺，双手微微颤抖。
Windsong puts away her tools, hands trembling slightly.

克努特：别紧张，北方哨歌同志——你瞧瞧，这儿的石头还是咱们再熟悉不过的样子。
Knut: Don't worry, Comrade Windsong. Look, these stones are still the same stones we've always known.

他看出了北方哨歌眼里的隐忧。
He catches the worry in Windsong's expression.

克努特：也别害怕失败，北方哨歌同志。成功是建立在无数次失败之上的。
Knut: And don't be afraid to fail. My father told me that failure is just success in progress, hahaha!

克努特：哪怕我们没能找到新的资源，也没能保住来亚什基……
Knut: Even if we cannot find this new resource or save our Rayashki ...

克努特：对咱们来说，能重新回到这儿，一条心地干一件事儿，已经没什么可抱怨的哩～
Knut: We've come back here together and worked for our common goal. We have nothing to complain about.

北方哨歌：……好。
Windsong: Alright.

克努特：无论最后的结果如何，咱们都感谢你的付出。
Knut: Whatever the result, we thank you for your efforts.

克努特：接下来就交给咱们吧——！
Knut: Now leave the rest to us!

他拧过头，朝着钻塔的方向大喊。
He turns his head and shouts toward the drilling machine.

克努特：尤里同志，确认管线连接状况。
Knut: Comrade Yuri, check the connection status.

克努特：可别忘了检查钻机状态，埃琳娜同志。
Knut: Don't forget to check the drill, Comrade Elena.

工人Ⅰ：放心吧，这可比徒手开罐头简单多了～
Worker I: Relax. It's much easier than opening a can with only your fingers.

工人众：哈哈～
Workers: Hahahahaha!

兴奋的队列流动了起来，像一团明亮的火。
The excited queue flows like a steady river.

这儿人头攒动，铁锹、锄头和铲子们协力遮蔽了天空。
People crowd together, shovels, hoes, and picks ringing out in unison.

宏伟的钻塔在雪中坚决地探出头来。
Magnificent drilling machines emerge up from the snow.

钢铁巨兽们相互组合，钻机轰鸣，缓缓向下推进。
They roar as their drills pierce the earth.

顽固的冻土没能阻碍钻头的推进，天空与土地的缝隙间似乎只剩唯一的鸣响。
The stubborn frozen soil does nothing to hinder their progress.

某种高亢而热忱的声响又一次萦绕在北方哨歌的耳边。
Their resonance is a sound that echoes in Windsong's ears, the sound of impassioned unity of purpose and vision.

这儿像是广场，像是公共食堂，像是工厂。
This place is like the square, like their public canteen, like their factory.

像是来亚什基的每一个角落。
Like every corner of Rayashki.

显然，这是值得画下的一幕。
Clearly, it is a scene worth capturing.

阿夫西维：克努特长出了细长的手臂儿，它伸进大家都够不着的地方，捞起地下的石头。
Avgust: Knut had grown a slender arm. One that reached places no one could and picked up stones there.

它缓缓崩碎，落入无边的深渊。

一切似乎都回归了平静。

显眼的推进痕迹刻在了冻土之上，像是某种永恒的通路。
The trails of the old machines wore deep into the frozen ground, forming a raised pathway that led up and away from the scene.

雪终于停了。

渐入黑

孩子们抽泣声起起落落，仿佛河水化冻。
The children, finally coming to grips with what they've seen, begin to cry.

维拉：……叶甫根尼同志。
Vila: Comrade Evgeni.

鱼会流泪么？
Do fish mourn? Can a Rusalka cry?

似乎没人能回答这个问题。
No one can really answer this question.

这尾来自遥远北方的鲁萨尔卡周围似乎漫起了一片咸涩的汪洋。
Yet around the Rusalka, a ring of salty water seems to rise.

克努特：该死的！这一点都不公平！
Knut: D**n it! This is not fair!

克努特：他凭什么仗着自己是这儿唯一会驾驶军机的家伙就自作主张！咱们应该投票——！举手表决！

Worker I: That a*e left us behind.

Worker II: But he will always be our comrade, right?

时间在无数的沉默中缓缓流过，像是永不回头的长河。
Time appears to stand still, as all present stand unmoving, unspeaking.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

FR-17 雪与雪之外的 / Snow, and the Others

失去支持的地脉能量重新回归了大地。
The unsupported ley energy returns to the earth.

The soil is smoothed out, a canvas for a new painting.

Their sound covering up the sorrow and the gloom of the moment.

FR-18 你好，来亚什基 / Hello, Rayashki

The people gather again.

FR-19 致后代 / To Descendants

激昂的时间河流在这儿悄无声息地摆荡了数月。
The river of time has moved swiftly in the passing months.

熙熙攘攘的人声此起彼伏。
Rayashki is bustling with the sounds of a busy and hopeful community.

人群在这里合流，又在这里分散，奔向各自的位置。

来亚什基游泳场

维拉：呵呵，没什么好奇怪的，随便坐吧～
Vila: Heh heh, no, it's alright. Have a seat.

维拉：我并不是血统纯正的鲁萨尔卡。如你所见，每隔一段时间，我都要回到水中，汲取海洋所赋予我们的灵感与养分。
Vila: I'm not a pure Rusalka. As you can see, I must get in touch with water every once in a while to replenish my power from the ocean.

北方哨歌：咳——你好，维拉同志。
Windsong: Ahem. Hello, Comrade Vila.

维拉：好久不见，北方哨歌同志。
Vila: It's been a while, Comrade Windsong.

维拉：我听说你整天在矿区里奔波，越来越多的工人们认可了理线学。
Vila: They say you're working hard in the mine, and the study of ley lines is getting popular among the workers.

北方哨歌：他们帮了我很多忙……如果没有他们，对来亚什基环境的研究不会这么顺利。
Windsong: They have helped a lot. My research on the environment wouldn't have gone nearly so smoothly without them.

北方哨歌：理线学在这里重获新生，生根发芽……甚至得到了外部的认可。
Windsong: It's given a second life to my studies, and it is growing so well. It has even gained some recognition beyond Rayashki.

北方哨歌：我……很高兴能来到这儿。
Windsong: I, I'm truly happy that I came here.

维拉：真没想到，对自己所研究的理论顽固而自信的北方哨歌同志也会露出如此羞怯的一面。
Vila: I never thought the Comrade Windsong would be so bashful over her accomplishments. I thought you were more stubborn and confident than that.

北方哨歌：……
Windsong: ...

维拉：我并没有取笑你，北方哨歌同志。事实上，你远不如看上去那般无所畏惧，不是吗？
Vila: I'm only teasing, comrade. It's a matter of fact that you are not as fearless as you pretend to be, isn't it?

维拉：这也正是人们紧紧团结在一起的理由，我们弥补不足，也……
抱歉，我的职业病又犯了～
Vila: That's why we must all stick together to make up for each other's weaknesses and make Rayashki proud! Sorry, speeches have become an occupational habit.

北方哨歌：好吧，我承认。
但这没什么好奇怪的，你也远没有表面上那么温柔，是吧？
Windsong: Fine, you got me. But it's not a big deal. Just as you are not quite the gentle and demure school teacher that you appear to be, are you, comrade?

北方哨歌：——我们扯平！
Windsong: We're even!

聚焦北方哨歌
Windsong clears her throat and hands the letter to Vila.

北方哨歌补救性地轻咳了两声，将手中的信件递给了维拉。

北方哨歌：我是来向你告别的……
Windsong: Actually, I've come to say goodbye.

北方哨歌：科算中心邀请我参加即将在欧洲分部举办的讲座，他们希望我以来亚什基为案例，介绍理线学是如何将神秘学与环境分析学结合起来的。
Windsong: Laplace has invited me to give a lecture for their European branch. They want me to give a lecture on how I combined environmental analysis with the arcanum based on what we've done here in Rayashki.

维拉：听起来是个良好的开始。
Vila: Sounds like a very promising new beginning for your studies.

北方哨歌：来亚什基发展得如何？
Windsong: How are things going in the town?

维拉：到这儿来参观的游客们变多了，他们相当热情，希望见证某些不一样的东西。
Vila: We are getting more visitors now. It seems people are eager to see something different.

北方哨歌：我敢肯定，他们会得偿所愿的。
Windsong: I'm sure they will.

维拉：我们与周边的许多地方都达成了合作，甚至包括基金会。
Vila: We've also begun cooperating with many governments and agencies near us, including the Foundation.

维拉：他们希望为孩子们进行一些简单的神秘学短期培训。
Vila: They hope to carry out some short-term training on the arcanum for the children.

收信
Another letter is passed on.

维拉上岸

维拉动作

另一封湿漉漉的信被递了上来。

北方哨歌：这是……？
Windsong: What's this?

维拉：拆开看看吧，这是从基金会寄来的。
Vila: Open it. It's from the Foundation.

打开信

维拉：命名日先生邀请我到基金会去，与他们商谈更多的合作方案，孩子们也在那儿等着我。
Vila: Mr. Name Day invites me to visit the Foundation and discuss further cooperation. The children are also waiting for me there.

维拉：在基金会学习的时候，他们也一直念叨着你。
Vila: It seems they mentioned you all the time during their training.

维拉：“我们错过了理线学的考试吗？”
Vila: "Did we miss the ley line exam?"

维拉：“基金会里有许多神奇的东西……”
Vila: "The Foundation has all sorts of incredible things."

“阿夫西维”：这儿有会咬人的金币、咋咋呼呼的小煤球、捕捉彩虹的玻璃笔……还有很多很多好玩的东西。
"Avgust": Like biting coins, noisy coal balls, a glass pen with rainbows inside. So much fun!

“帕索诺”：我学到了许多神秘学咒语！
"Pasono": I've mastered a lot of incantations!

“尼娜”：我很想念小镇的大家……
"Nina": I miss the town and everyone.

“阿夫西维”：没错，我们想念阿廖卡同志，想念布林同志，还有友谊同志！
"Avgust": Yeah. We miss Comrade Alenka, Comrade Blinchik, and Comrade Piroshki!

“彼得森”：几个月后，我们就能回家了！
"Pyotr": They say we will be able to go home in a few months!

“彼得森”：我一定能学会最厉害的神秘术，保护好小镇的安全！
"Pyotr": I must master the most powerful arcane skills by then, so I can use them to protect the town!

“阿夫西维”：我们也会变成海燕！
"Avgust": We'll transform into sea swallows!

“阿夫西维”：飞呀～飞呀～飞到更远的地方！
"Avgust": Then we'll be able to fly and fly to far, far away!

缓缓黑屏

调试

电台主播Ⅰ：今日，卡斯林斯卡医学院附属医院接收了一例罕见病例。
Radio Broadcaster I: The Kaslinska University Hospital received a rare case today.

电台主播Ⅰ：某患者血管呈现出了不可逆的电线化特征。截止至18：00时，该患者全身的动脉、静脉及毛细血管组织均已坏死。
Radio Broadcaster I: The patient's veins irreversibly transformed into electric wires. As of 18:00, all arterial, venous, and capillary tissues throughout the patient's body have undergone necrosis.

电台主播Ⅰ：卡斯林斯卡医学院院长受访时称，他们将邀请更多专业人员参与会诊，商讨后续的研究工作。
Radio Broadcaster I: The director said they would invite more professionals to the consultation to decide on further research directions.

电台主播Ⅰ：《世界新奇报》声称，“电线人”症状将会成为新的未解之谜。
Radio Broadcaster I: Global Variety News has claimed the case may become one of the greatest unsolved mysteries of the era.

电台主播Ⅰ：同时，他们发起了专栏活动，旨在分析该“电线人”的血管构造对不同电器的应用频率。
Radio Broadcaster I: They started a new column to analyze possible compatibilities between the patient's new wired veins and different appliances.

电台主播Ⅰ：本电台将持续为您报道——
Radio Broadcaster I: Please stay tuned for more details.

调试

电台主播Ⅱ：近日，“飞毯旅行社”将组织一场巡游北欧的浪漫之旅。
Radio Broadcaster II: The Flying Carpet Travel Agency is starting a tour around Northern Europe ...

电台主播Ⅱ：在那里，你们能见证浪漫的极光，与毛绒绒的奇肯恩们亲密接触，享受雪地飞毯竞速赛……
Radio Broadcaster II: ... where you will be able to see the breathtaking aurora borealis, pet fluffy Qiqirns, and even enjoy a flying carpet race.

电台主播Ⅱ：最后，我们将会抵达一座神秘的小镇，来亚什基。
Radio Broadcaster II: The destination of our tour is Rayashki.

电台主播Ⅱ：那儿有丰富的煤矿，是北极最温暖的地方。
Radio Broadcaster II: A mysterious town, the warmest place in the Arctic Circle, sitting atop many rich veins of coal.

电台主播Ⅱ：在那儿，相比支付金钱，我衷心希望各位参与一些力所能及的劳动来换取所需。当然，这并不是强迫性的。
Radio Broadcaster II: When you get there, we suggest that you abide by the town's wishes and work to earn what you need instead of buying it. Though this is not an obligation, of course.

电台主播Ⅱ：但是，倘若我们能见证一种崭新的、更美好的理想生活，为何不亲自试一试呢？……我相信，它不会令你们失望的。
Radio Broadcaster II: But why not have a try when you are given the opportunity to experience a new and better lifestyle? Trust me, you won't be disappointed.
